ISPE Baseline® Guide Volume 7 (2nd Ed.): Risk-Based Manufacture | p4-p22

本節學習目標

  • 理解 Risk-MaPP 的核心使命：在「共用廠房」中管理交叉污染風險，平衡病患安全與員工安全
  • 掌握本指引第二版修訂的五大驅動因素，尤其是 EU GMP Chapter 3/5 更新與 EMA HBEL 指引
  • 區分 HBEL（Health-Based Exposure Limit） 與 OEL（Occupational Exposure Limit） 的根本差異及應用場景
  • 了解主要法規驅動力：EMA HBEL Guideline（2014）、EU GMP Annex 15（2015）、21 CFR 211.42(c)
  • 認識高危害藥物的分類邏輯：細胞毒性藥物、荷爾蒙、致敏劑（Beta-Lactam）
  • 掌握風險管理生命週期八步驟：識別 → 分析 → 評估 → 控制 → 降低 → 接受 → 審查 → 溝通
  • 理解 GMP 視角（病患保護）與工業衛生視角（工人保護）的差異與平衡策略

Preface（前言）

Original Text

The use of multiproduct facilities for the production of pharmaceutical products is necessary to allow products to be brought to patients in a timely and cost-effective manner. Doing this safely requires an understanding of the products, the facilities, the processes, and the equipment and the risks posed by this combination. The major risk of concern within shared facilities is the risk of cross-contamination.

New GMP guidance for the EU came into effect in 2015 that requires a risk management process to determine if products can be safely manufactured in shared facilities. This new GMP requirement left industry unsure how to perform and document these risk assessments.

This Baseline® Guide provides a scientific risk-based approach based on ICH Q9 to manage the risk of cross-contamination to maintain product quality and operator safety. This allows the selection of the appropriate risk control strategies to be implemented on a case-by-case basis to maintain an appropriate balance between assurance of product quality and worker safety. This Guide also provides examples of risk assessments and the summary report.

This second edition of the Guide is updated to include the new EU GMP requirements as well as additional information for cleaning, HVAC, and examples to assist the reader.

During the development of the first edition of this document, the FDA and EMA were actively involved and other regulatory agencies reviewed the document prior to publication. For the second edition there were discussions with the EMA to ensure that the Guide did not contradict the new GMP requirements and again other regulatory agencies, including the FDA, reviewed the document prior to publication.

Advanced Topics Notice: Advanced Topics are noted and represent topics that require subject matter experts to address. These issues should not be addressed by those that are not familiar with the topic or do not have sufficient experience to understand how to apply the concepts appropriately.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

Risk-MaPP 的存在理由

Risk-MaPP = Risk-Based Manufacture of Pharmaceutical Products。這本指引解決一個真實的產業痛點：

  • 藥廠為節省成本，同一設施生產多種藥品（共用廠房）
  • 2015 年 EU GMP 更新要求必須做風險評估，但沒有告訴業者「怎麼做」
  • Risk-MaPP 就是填補這個空白的實務指南

核心問題只有一個：「在共用廠房製造藥品時，交叉污染的風險是否可接受？」

比喻：共用廚房的食物過敏風險

想像一家餐廳同一個廚房既做花生菜餚也做無過敏原餐點。如何確保花生不污染其他食物？你需要：評估花生的危害程度 → 分析污染途徑 → 設定清潔標準 → 確認殘留量低於安全閾值。

Risk-MaPP 做的就是把這個邏輯系統化、科學化、文件化，適用於製藥的多產品生產。

第二版 vs 第一版：主要變化

  • 納入 EU GMP Chapter 3 & 5 新要求（2015 年生效）
  • 整合 EMA HBEL Guideline（2014 年 11 月發布）
  • 新增清潔、HVAC 章節內容與更新範例
  • FDA 與 EMA 均參與審閱，確保不牴觸新法規

CDMO 實務思考

作為無菌充填的 CDMO，你的廠房同時生產多個客戶的產品——這正是 Risk-MaPP 最直接的應用場景。當客戶稽核問：「你如何確保我的產品不被其他產品污染？」Risk-MaPP 提供了完整的回答框架。

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

作者組成的意義：跨學科整合

這份指引的作者陣容非常特殊——不是單一領域的專家，而是刻意整合了：

  • 毒理學家（Naumann PhD, DABT）——設定科學安全限值
  • 工業衛生師（Abromovitz CIH, Burgess）——員工暴露管理
  • 製程工程師（Marshall CEng）——設施設計與清潔
  • 品質保證（Holmes, Hamilton）——GMP 法規符合
  • 法規機構（FDA, EMA, SwissMedic）——確保法規一致性

這個多元組合正是 Risk-MaPP 最大的特色：它不是「純 GMP 視角」，也不是「純工業衛生視角」，而是兩者的平衡。

比喻：建築法規的多方共筆

這就像制定建築安全規範，需要結構工程師（安全）、消防工程師（逃生）、建築師（設計）、衛生局（衛生）以及建管單位（法規）共同參與——缺少任何一方，規範都會有盲點。

EMA 深度參與的重要性

第二版特別強調 EMA HBEL 實施團隊的參與。這意味著 Risk-MaPP 第二版的核心框架——以 HBEL 作為決策基礎——已取得 EMA 的隱性認可。在 EU GMP 稽核中，引用本指引的方法論具有較強的說服力。

Chapter 1: Introduction（第一章：導論）

Original Text

This ISPE Baseline® Guide: Risk-Based Manufacture of Pharmaceutical Products (Risk-MaPP) provides a scientific risk-based approach based on ICH Q9 to manage the risk of cross-contamination to maintain product quality and operator safety. This allows the selection of the appropriate risk control strategies to be implemented on a case by case basis to maintain an appropriate balance between assurance of product quality and worker safety.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

Risk-MaPP 的雙重目標

開篇一句話點出了 Risk-MaPP 的本質：它同時服務兩個對象——

  • 病患安全：確保產品不因交叉污染而影響療效或安全性（GMP 視角）
  • 員工安全：確保操作人員不因接觸高活性藥物而受害（工業衛生視角）

這兩個目標有時會有張力，Risk-MaPP 的價值在於提供一個系統化的方法來同時滿足兩者。

1.1 Scope of this Guide（指引範圍）

Original Text

When considering multiproduct facilities, to satisfy regulatory requirements risk management processes are necessary to determine and document reasonable and acceptable risk. This Guide provides a process that allows manufacturers to assess risk and determine where control strategies are necessary to meet acceptable limits for cross-contamination. The control strategies to manage risk can vary from administrative to full dedication or segregation.

This Guide is intended to provide professionals in the pharmaceutical industry with a consistent approach on setting acceptable limits to assess the potential of cross-contamination causing an undue risk to patient safety.

It should be noted that the use of the principles in this Guide assumes the following:

  1. There is a basic understanding of the hazard spectrum of compounds and containment fundamentals
  2. Subject Matter Experts (SMEs) are part of the team for the quality risk management process
  3. The integrity of the data used to support the quality risk management process is of high quality and meets regulatory expectations
  4. Risk management principles are not used to justify bad design or engineering practices

The principles described in this Guide can be applied equally to large and small molecular weight APIs, pre-clinical and clinical materials, and commercially marketed products in all dosage forms.

The term "controls" as used throughout this Guide encompasses all types of controls including:

  • Process controls
  • Operational controls
  • The full range of engineering controls
  • Procedural controls

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

適用範圍：比你想的更廣

Risk-MaPP 的適用對象涵蓋：

  • 大分子量 API（生物製劑）與小分子量 API（化學合成藥）
  • 臨床前、臨床試驗材料與上市商業化產品
  • 所有劑型（注射劑、口服固體、外用等）
  • 任何設施規模，從小型研發設施到大型商業生產廠

關鍵前提：這不是給初學者的手冊——第 2 點明確要求 SME 參與。

「Controls」的四個層次

注意本指引對「controls（管制措施）」的廣義定義——這是一個從最輕到最重的連續體：

  • 程序性管制（最輕）：SOP、工作指引、訓練
  • 操作管制：排程隔離、campaign 生產
  • 工程管制：設備設計、HVAC、密閉系統
  • 完全專用/隔離（最重）：獨立廠房、專用設備

Risk-MaPP 的核心貢獻：讓企業能夠根據風險高低選擇適當層次，而非一律採用最嚴格措施。

比喻：駕駛安全等級

一個危險化學品運輸公司的風險管理：低風險貨物（程序控制：注意路標）→ 中風險（操作控制：特定時段行駛）→ 高風險（工程控制：密閉罐車）→ 極高風險（完全隔離：專用道路）。Risk-MaPP 就是幫你決定每種藥品應該用哪個等級的「運輸方式」。

無菌充填 CDMO 的實踐問題

你的廠房同時承接一般抗生素、荷爾蒙藥物、和普通小分子藥品的充填作業。問：

  • 這三類產品應分別採用哪個層次的 controls？
  • 若客戶要求引入一個新的細胞毒性藥物，觸發哪些評估步驟？
  • SME 組成應包含哪些專業背景的人？
1.2 Background（背景）

Original Text

The science of toxicology recognizes the principle of a continuum of hazard associated with all compounds, even within individual classes of compounds. Zero risk is considered scientifically unachievable and not necessary. Some classes of compounds, that have historically included hormones, cytotoxic compounds, genotoxic compounds, pathogenic organisms, and veterinary products, have traditionally been placed in dedicated and segregated facilities to manage the risk. Sensitizers such as Beta-Lactam antibiotics have received particular scrutiny due to the perceived severity of potential allergic reactions.

Dedicated facilities are required for manufacturing active substances and medicinal products with a high sensitizing potential for which scientific data does not support an acceptable level of exposure or the risk associated with the handling of the product at the facility cannot be adequately controlled by organizational or technical measures.

The ICH in their Q9 Quality Risk Management document state: "The manufacturing and use of a drug product, including its components, necessarily entail some degree of risk."

The FDA also has acknowledged: "Although medicinal products are required to be safe, safety does not mean zero risk. A safe product is one that has reasonable risks, given the magnitude of the benefits expected and the alternative available."

The EMA acknowledged: "the concept of 'zero risk' does not apply to medicinal products. The licensing of medicinal products needs to be assessed in the context of the benefit/risk balance concept."

When processing compounds in a multiproduct facility the risk of cross-contamination should be controlled so that products do not have any cross-contamination above established safe levels.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

「零風險」的科學破除

這段背景提出了 Risk-MaPP 最重要的哲學前提：零風險是科學上無法實現的目標。ICH Q9、FDA、EMA 三大機構均一致認同這個立場。

這個前提有實際意義：它允許藥廠用「風險可接受」而非「風險為零」作為決策標準。如果你的稽核員堅持要求「零殘留」，這個概念就是你的科學依據。

高危害藥物的歷史分類

這段列出了傳統上需要專用設施的化合物類型，理解這個分類的歷史背景很重要：

  • 細胞毒性/遺傳毒性藥物：癌症化療藥，低劑量即有效/有毒
  • 荷爾蒙（尤其是性荷爾蒙）：微量即可影響體內平衡
  • Beta-Lactam 抗生素：特殊案例——問題不在毒性，而在致敏性（不可用 HBEL 計算，必須專用廠房）
  • 獸藥：非人體用藥，交叉污染至人用藥風險獨特

注意：Risk-MaPP 的方法論不適用於高致敏性物質（如 Beta-Lactam），那類必須直接專用廠房。

比喻：食品業的過敏原管理

花生過敏者對花生的反應類似 Beta-Lactam 的致敏性——即使是極微量殘留也可能引發嚴重反應（過敏性休克）。這類物質不能用「可接受殘留量」來管理，只能徹底隔離。Risk-MaPP 的風險量化方法適用於「多少量會有多少毒性效果」可以計算的化合物，不適用於「任何量都可能觸發免疫過激反應」的致敏劑。

1.3 Reasons for Revisions（修訂原因）

Original Text

Since the original publication of this Guide there were some significant changes in regulations and application of regulations. These include:

  1. The updated EU GMPs relative to managing the risk of cross-contamination:
    • Chapter 3 was updated to allow the use of quality risk management principles to determine if products can be produced in shared facilities.
    • Chapter 5 was also updated to incorporate quality risk management principles and require toxicological assessments which refers to the EMA guideline.
  2. The EMA issued "Guideline on setting health based exposure limits for use in risk identification in the manufacture of different medicinal products in shared facilities" to provide guidance on how to set health-based limits. This guideline also states "PDE and ADE are essentially synonymous".
  3. ICH issued M7 "Assessment and Control of DNA Reactive (Mutagenic) Impurities" which sets a Threshold of Toxicological Concern (TTC) for mutagenic impurities.
  4. The adoption by US and EU regulators of a "life cycle" approach to process validation incorporating stages of process design, process qualification, and continued process verification.
  5. Industry began implementing risk-based approaches to managing the risk of cross-contamination and sharing some lessons learned.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

五大修訂驅動力的時間軸

第一版（2010 年）→ 第二版（2017 年），7 年間的法規環境劇變：

  • 2014 年 8 月：EU GMP Chapter 3 & 5 更新，正式要求毒理學評估
  • 2014 年 11 月：EMA HBEL Guideline 發布，定義 PDE = ADE
  • 2014 年：ICH M7 發布，設定基因毒性雜質的 TTC 概念
  • 2015 年：EU GMP Annex 15 更新，清潔驗證限值需基於毒理學評估
  • 2011 年起：FDA Process Validation Guideline 推動生命週期方法

關鍵等號：PDE = ADE

這個等式非常重要：

  • PDE（Permitted Daily Exposure）= EMA 用語，源自 ICH Q3C 殘留溶劑概念
  • ADE（Acceptable Daily Exposure）= ISPE/Risk-MaPP 用語，業界工業衛生傳統

兩者計算方法本質上相同——都基於毒理學數據，考慮 NOAEL、不確定因子、體重調整、給藥途徑等。EMA 在 2014 年指引中正式聲明兩者「本質上同義」，統一了業界術語。

實務提示：在文件中，使用 PDE/ADE 都可以被接受，但最好保持一致，並說明與另一術語的關係。

生命週期驗證方法的重要轉變

第 4 點的清潔驗證生命週期概念影響深遠：

  • 舊觀念：清潔驗證 = 三批次測試，通過後完成
  • 新觀念：清潔驗證 = 持續的過程控制，需要：
    設計階段（了解殘留行為）→ 確認階段（驗證清潔有效性）→ 持續驗證（監控日常清潔效果）

這個概念與 Risk-MaPP 高度契合：風險管理不是一次性評估，而是持續的生命週期活動。

1.4 Structure of this Guide（指引結構）

Original Text

This Guide should be read and considered holistically as reading individual subsections in isolation can lead to the unjustifiable conclusions.

The layout of this Guide mirrors the Quality Risk Management Process as defined in ICH Q9:

  • Chapter 2 — Concepts and Regulatory Philosophy: general overview of regulatory expectations and key concepts
  • Chapter 3 — Quality System fundamentals and the "Logic Diagram" (balancing GxP and Industrial Hygiene)
  • Chapter 4 — Risk Assessment overview (identification, analysis, evaluation)
  • Chapter 5 — Risk Identification: health-based exposure limits
  • Chapter 6 — Risk Analysis: factors affecting exposure
  • Chapter 7 — Risk Evaluation: comparison of risk criteria
  • Chapter 8 — Risk Control strategies
  • Chapter 9 — Risk Reduction: areas to address
  • Chapter 10 — Risk Acceptance
  • Chapter 11 — Risk Management Tools
  • Chapters 12 & 13 — Risk Review and Risk Communication (ongoing processes)
  • Appendices — References, glossary, risk assessment examples

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

風險管理生命週期：指引架構圖

整本 Risk-MaPP 的章節結構就是 ICH Q9 風險管理流程的具體化：

Ch.5 識別 Identification
→
Ch.6 分析 Analysis
→
Ch.7 評估 Evaluation
→
Ch.8 控制 Control
→
Ch.9 降低 Reduction
→
Ch.10 接受 Acceptance
→
Ch.12 審查 Review
→
Ch.13 溝通 Communication

「整體閱讀」的警告

指引特別強調必須「整體」理解，不能斷章取義。實務中常見的錯誤：

  • 只看第 5 章（HBEL 設定）而跳過第 6 章（暴露分析），導致限值設錯
  • 只看第 9 章（風險降低措施）而不執行第 5-7 章，無法證明措施是否充分
  • 只引用 ADE 數值而不理解其假設條件，被稽核員質疑

比喻：食譜書的閱讀方式

就像食譜書——你不能只看「加一茶匙鹽」這一步，而要了解整個烹飪流程。每個步驟都有前因後果。Risk-MaPP 的邏輯流程更是如此：前一章的輸出是下一章的輸入。

Chapter 2: Concepts and Regulatory Philosophy（第二章：概念與法規哲學）

Original Text

The current situation is that there exists some variation between regulatory authorities in the interpretation of commensurate control strategies associated with pharmaceutical manufacturing. Worldwide, regulators are beginning to support the use of risk-based approaches to determine the acceptable level of controls required for the compliant manufacture of highly hazardous compounds within multiproduct facilities, but there are still several regions that have not embraced a risk-based approach.

The US FDA and the EMA are expecting a documented risk assessment to determine if products can be produced in shared facilities as well as helping to identify the controls necessary to manage the risk of cross-contamination in these shared facilities.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

全球法規現況：進行中的轉型

截至 2017 年（第二版出版時），全球法規呈現「先進 vs. 保守」的分化：

  • 積極接受風險方法：FDA、EMA、SwissMedic
  • 允許有條件共用生產：WHO、MHLW（日本）
  • 仍堅持嚴格隔離：部分亞洲與新興市場法規機構

FDA 和 EMA 明確要求「文件化風險評估」——這不是選項，是義務。

2.1 EudraLex – EU GMP Updates（歐盟 GMP 更新）

Original Text

In August of 2014 the European Commission updated Chapters 3 and 5 to provide improved guidance on managing the risk of cross-contamination. These changes encourage the use of risk management principles to manage the risk of cross-contamination. Both chapters reference a toxicological evaluation as described in the EMA "Guideline on setting health based exposure limits."

Section 3.6 has updated guidance on when dedicated facilities are required:

"Dedicated facilities are required for manufacturing when a medicinal product presents a risk because:
i. the risk cannot be adequately controlled by operational and/or technical measures,
ii. scientific data from the toxicological evaluation does not support a controllable risk (e.g. allergenic potential from highly sensitising materials such as beta lactams) or
iii. relevant residue limits, derived from the toxicological evaluation, cannot be satisfactorily determined by a validated analytical method."

Section 5.20 states: "A Quality Risk Management process, which includes a potency and toxicological evaluation, should be used to assess and control the cross-contamination risks presented by the products manufactured. Factors including; facility/equipment design and use, personnel and material flow, microbiological controls, physico-chemical characteristics of the active substance, process characteristics, cleaning processes and analytical capabilities relative to the relevant limits established from the evaluation of the products should also be taken into account."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

EU GMP Chapter 3 & 5 的革命性改變

2014 年 8 月的 EU GMP 更新是 Risk-MaPP 第二版的最主要驅動力。改變前後的對比：

必須專用廠房的三種情況

EU GMP 3.6 列出的三個觸發點非常清晰，也是稽核員的檢查清單：

  1. 技術/操作措施不足：即使使用所有工程控制手段，風險仍無法充分控制
  2. 毒理學數據不支持：最典型的就是 Beta-Lactam 的致敏性——科學無法設定「安全殘留量」
  3. 無法驗證的分析方法：如果連殘留量都無法被可靠地偵測，就無法確認清潔有效性

注意：這三點是「必須」（required）專用，不是「建議」。

實務應用：Section 5.20 的稽核意涵

Section 5.20 是 EU GMP 查廠時最常被引用的條文。稽核員會問：

  • 你的 QRM 流程是否包含毒效學評估？（ADE/PDE 報告在哪？）
  • 設施/設備設計、人員/物料流向是否在風險評估中被考慮？
  • 你的分析方法是否足夠靈敏到偵測到相關殘留限值？
  • 是否有定期審查機制確保管制措施持續有效？
2.2 EMA HBEL Guideline（EMA 健康暴露限值指引）

Original Text

The EMA introduced this guideline in November 2014. This guideline introduces the Permitted Daily Exposure (PDE) to determine a substance specific dose that is unlikely to cause an adverse effect if an individual is exposed at or below this dose every day for a lifetime. This is an extension of the PDE introduced in ICH Q3C(R6) for residual solvents.

This guideline outlines the process used to develop a substance specific PDE and a suggested summary document. The EMA document also states that the PDE and ADE are essentially synonymous. This guidance document is applicable to API manufacture as well as finished dosage manufacture.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

PDE 的概念起源與擴展

PDE 概念的發展歷程：

  • ICH Q3C（1997）：PDE 首次用於藥品中殘留溶劑的安全限值
  • ICH Q3D（2014）：擴展 PDE 概念至元素雜質
  • EMA HBEL（2014）：進一步擴展至藥品活性成分在共用設施中的交叉污染控制

PDE 定義的關鍵詞：「一生每天暴露於此劑量或以下，不可能引起不良效應」。注意「終生」（lifetime）和「任何途徑」（any route）兩個重要假設。

PDE/ADE 計算框架（概覽）

PDE = NOAEL × 體重調整係數 / (F1 × F2 × F3 × F4 × F5)

  • NOAEL：無觀察到不良效應劑量（來自毒理學研究）
  • F1：種間差異（動物→人，通常 ×5 或 ×12）
  • F2：個體間差異（一般 ×10）
  • F3：研究期限（短期 vs. 長期研究）
  • F4：嚴重/不可逆毒性調整
  • F5：其他不確定性

計算 PDE 需要具備毒理學專業背景的 SME。不建議非專業人員自行計算。

適用範圍：API 製造 + 製劑生產

EMA HBEL 指引明確涵蓋原料藥（API）製造廠和製劑廠（finished dosage）兩個層次。這意味著：

  • API 供應商做多種 API 共用設備時，需要 HBEL
  • 製劑廠做多產品充填時，同樣需要 HBEL
  • CDMO 同時承接 API 合成和製劑業務，兩個場景都要評估
2.3 EU GMP Annex 2 – Biological Medicinal Products（生物藥品製造）

Original Text

Annex 2 states "Unlike conventional medicinal products, which are manufactured using chemical and physical techniques capable of a high degree of consistency, the manufacture of biological active substances and medicinal products involves biological processes and materials, such as cultivation of cells or extraction from living organisms. These biological processes may display inherent variability, so that the range and nature of by-products may be variable. As a result, quality risk management (QRM) principles are particularly important for this class of materials and should be used to develop the control strategy across all stages of manufacture so as to minimise variability and to reduce the opportunity for contamination and cross-contamination."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

生物藥品的特殊挑戰

Annex 2 提醒為什麼生物製品更需要 QRM 思維：

  • 固有可變性：生物製程（細胞培養、發酵）天然就有批次間差異，副產物組成不固定
  • 複雜性：蛋白質、多醣等大分子的特性遠比小分子複雜，難以用單一化學指標評估風險
  • 交叉污染的特殊形式：生物藥的交叉污染可能包括宿主細胞蛋白、DNA、病毒等

Risk-MaPP 原則可以應用於生物製品，但 Annex 2 的引用是提醒：評估時需要考慮生物製品的獨特複雜性。

CDMO 無菌充填的實際含義

若你的 CDMO 同時承接生物製劑（如單株抗體）和小分子注射劑的充填，需要特別注意：

  • 生物製劑的 ADE 計算需要不同的毒理學考量（效價、免疫原性等）
  • 清潔驗證需考慮大分子蛋白質的清潔困難性
  • 分析方法需能區分並偵測生物製劑特有的殘留物
2.4 EU GMP Annex 15 – Qualification and Validation（確效與驗證）

Original Text

The cleaning validation section of Annex 15 (as well as other sections) was updated in 2015. The Annex states that "Limits for the carryover of product residues should be based on a toxicological evaluation." and the EMA guideline on setting health-based exposure limits is referenced. PIC/S Annex 15 adopted the same language in a recent update.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

Annex 15 的清潔驗證革命

2015 年 Annex 15 更新前後的清潔驗證方式對比：

PIC/S 跟進：台灣 GMP 的影響

特別注意：PIC/S Annex 15 同步採用了相同語言。台灣 PIC/S GMP 成員國，這意味著台灣 PIC/S 認證廠的清潔驗證計算方式，也應轉向基於毒理學評估的方法。

如果你的廠房目前仍使用「10 ppm」或「1/1000 TDD」作為唯一清潔限值依據，可能需要更新至 ADE/PDE 基礎的計算。

比喻：食品最大殘留量（MRL）的科學化

就像食品農藥殘留標準從過去的「感覺合理」進化到現在的「基於每日可接受攝入量（ADI）科學計算」，藥品清潔驗證限值也完成了同樣的轉型——從經驗法則轉為科學依據。

2.5 US FDA 21 CFR 211.42（美國 FDA 法規要求）

Original Text

The US FDA regulation that often is cited when there are concerns with cross-contamination is 21 CFR 211.42 that states "There shall be separate or defined areas or such other control systems for the firm's operations as are necessary to prevent contamination..."

During the planning meetings for the original ISPE Risk-MaPP Baseline® Guide published in 2010, the FDA specifically requested that this Guide:

  • Provide an approach to identify highly hazardous drugs
  • Provide a risk management/assessment model that gives a clear view on how to address the controls to comply with 21 CFR 211.42(c)
  • Discuss how the approach fits into cleaning validation

2.5.1 Approach to Identify Highly Hazardous Drugs

The original intention of this Guide was to provide a method to identify highly hazardous compounds. However, during the development of the first edition, it became apparent that an approach to identify acceptable risk in the manufacture of pharmaceutical products was more appropriate.

Health-based limits should be developed by toxicologists from available toxicological and pharmacological data. This Guide refers to this health-based limit as the Acceptable Daily Exposure (ADE) value. The ADE value represents a dose that is unlikely to cause an adverse effect if an individual is exposed, by any route, at or below this dose every day for a lifetime.

This Guide is predicated on some key concepts:

  • Hazard: the inherent property of a compound to produce harm.
  • Exposure: contact with the hazard; dependent on the control systems used.
  • Risk: the probability of occurrence of harm at a given level of exposure, reflecting severity of harm.

2.5.2 Risk Management Model for 21 CFR 211.42(c)

21 CFR 211.42(c) states that "Operations shall be performed within specifically defined areas of adequate size. There shall be separate or defined areas or such other control systems for the firm's operations as are necessary to prevent contamination or mixups..."

2.5.3 How the Approach Fits into Cleaning Validation

Residues from a compound which remain after cleaning on equipment or other product contact surfaces may pose a risk to patient safety. Cleaning procedures should be developed to minimize the risk from residues. To reduce risk, cleaning procedures should be capable of reducing residues to, or below, a predetermined safe level based on the risk assessment.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

21 CFR 211.42 的解讀重點

這條法規的關鍵在於：「separate or defined areas or such other control systems」。

「or such other control systems」是 Risk-MaPP 存在的法律空間——FDA 的條文本身已允許用「其他管制系統」替代「實體隔離」。Risk-MaPP 提供的就是這個「other control systems」的科學依據和文件架構。

危害 × 暴露 = 風險：三角關係

Risk-MaPP 的核心風險公式：

  • 危害（Hazard）：化合物的固有屬性，不能改變（ADE 是量化指標）
  • 暴露（Exposure）：接觸危害的程度，可以透過管制措施降低
  • 風險（Risk）= 危害嚴重性 × 暴露發生機率

結論：因為危害（化合物毒性）無法改變，降低風險的唯一手段是降低暴露。這就是所有管制措施的理論基礎。

「高危害藥物辨識」的概念轉變

值得注意的思維轉變：第一版原本想提供「高危害藥物清單」，但最終改為提供「可接受風險評估框架」。

原因：

  • 「高危害」是相對概念，取決於管控能力
  • 貼標籤（cytotoxic、potent）容易引發情緒化決策
  • 科學的做法是：設定 ADE → 評估暴露 → 計算風險 → 決定管控等級

清潔驗證整合框架

Risk-MaPP 與清潔驗證的整合邏輯：

  1. 取得化合物 ADE（毒理學評估）
  2. 根據批量大小、設備接觸面積、後續產品最小劑量計算清潔限值（swab 或 rinse 限值）
  3. 確認分析方法靈敏度足以偵測該限值
  4. 驗證清潔程序可將殘留量降至限值以下
  5. 持續監控（生命週期方法）
2.5.4 Regulatory Environment（法規環境演進）

Original Text

From 2003 through 2015, ICH working groups produced several significant documents: ICH Q3C(R6), Q3D, Q7A, Q8(R2), Q9, Q10, Q11, Q12 and ICH M7. These documents have been or are being adopted by the ICH parties (US, Japan, and EU) and used worldwide.

Key milestones:

  • ICH Q3C(R6): Introduced the PDE concept for residual solvents
  • ICH Q3D: Clarifies PDE limits for elemental impurities
  • ICH Q7 (section 4.4): Dedicated production areas for highly sensitizing materials (penicillins, cephalosporins) and consideration for high pharmacological activity compounds
  • ICH Q8(R2): Introduced Quality by Design — "quality should be built into a product with a thorough understanding"
  • ICH Q10: Effective pharmaceutical quality system throughout the product life cycle
  • ICH M7: Mutagenic impurities — limit of 1 in 100,000 excess cancer risk

In 2002, the FDA announced its Pharmaceutical cGMPs for the 21st Century – A Risk-Based Approach initiative. In 2007, it was renamed to "Pharmaceutical Quality for the 21st Century" to capture the larger issue of product quality.

In 2011 the FDA Process Validation Guideline states quality product is defined as the absence of unacceptable adulteration due to cross-contamination with other products produced in a shared facility.

The FDA OPQ key concepts applied to cross-contamination:

  1. Risk is a function of hazard and exposure
  2. There is a continuum of hazard — no distinct lines between low and high hazard
  3. Pharmacological and toxicological descriptions (NOAEL, ADE) should be used — not subjective terms like "potent"
  4. A consistent, robust, science risk-based approach across the hazard continuum
  5. Health-based exposure limits should not be artificially reduced
  6. GxP is primary; IH (worker safety) also must be addressed holistically

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

「不得人為降低 ADE」的重要警示

第 6 點（健康暴露限值不應人為降低）是業界常見錯誤的直接反應：

錯誤做法：毒理學家算出 ADE = 1 mg/day，管理層說「太高了，改成 0.1 mg/day 更安全」。

問題：如果 0.1 mg/day 是正確的科學限值，那原本的毒理學評估有誤；如果 1 mg/day 是科學正確的，人為降低到 0.1 mg/day 的唯一效果是讓不必要的「不符合規定」更容易發生，然後需要解釋「為什麼超出一個不必要嚴格的限值是可接受的」——這在邏輯上是自相矛盾的。

「避免情緒化標籤」的文化意義

第 3 點批評「cytotoxic」「potent」等主觀標籤——這是對舊文化的挑戰。在製藥業，「這是細胞毒性藥物，必須最高等級防護」是一種自動觸發的決策模式，不需要科學計算。Risk-MaPP 說：不對。你需要算 ADE、評估暴露、才能決定管控等級。這個轉變需要組織文化的改變。

2.6 Overview of the Risk Management Approach（風險管理方法概覽）

Original Text

A risk management approach should be applied to the handling of pharmaceutical products. This should be a holistically defined process to formally identify hazards and understand risks to assist decision making for the implementation of appropriate approaches for risk control. Although this process should be a formal part of an organization's quality system, the level of effort and detail for the risk management process can, and should, vary based on the perceived risks which are based on hazard, including severity and probability of occurrence.

The risk assessment process should be used to derive criteria that can assist in decision making and control strategies to manage the risks to the patient. The risk assessment should be a transparent evaluation of all data relevant to hazard identification, assessment of potency (dose response) and severity, exposure assessment, and characterization of risk.

ICH Q9 outlines a quality risk management process that is iterative and consists of the identification of the hazards and the analysis and evaluation of risks associated with exposure to those hazards, as well as control strategies to manage the risks.

Figure 2.1🔍: ICH Q9 Quality Risk Management Process [referenced in original — includes Risk Identification, Risk Analysis, Risk Evaluation (with loop back for Unacceptable risk), Risk Control (→ Risk Reduction / Risk Acceptance), Risk Review, and Risk Communication as an overarching thread]

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

ICH Q9 風險管理流程詳解

Figure 2.1🔍 雖然是圖表，但核心邏輯是：

① 危害識別
→
② 風險分析
→
③ 風險評估
→
④ 風險可接受？
若不可接受 ↓           若可接受 ↓
⑤ 風險降低
→（循環回③）
⑥ 風險接受
→
⑦ 風險審查
⑧ 風險溝通（貫穿全程）

「努力程度與風險成比例」原則

這個原則很實用：

  • 低 ADE 化合物（高危害）→ 需要詳盡的定量風險評估
  • 高 ADE 化合物（低危害）→ 定性或半定量評估可能已足夠
  • 已有大量歷史數據的熟悉化合物 → 可引用既有評估
  • 全新、數據稀少的化合物 → 需要更保守的評估方法

不是每個化合物都需要完整的 500 頁風險評估報告——但這個判斷本身需要專業判斷。

2.7 Use of Health-Based Exposure Limits（健康暴露限值的應用）

Original Text

An API represents a hazard, as it is capable of producing biological effects (e.g., pharmacological or toxicological). The likelihood that these effects will occur depends on:

  • The dose-response relationship
  • The amount absorbed as determined by the route, level, and duration of exposure

The ADE takes these into consideration and reflects a safe dose which incorporates a margin of safety. The main premise of this Guide is that if exposure to an API is kept below a prespecified level that is determined to be safe, this would indicate low risk for adverse health effects.

A number of different terms have been used to describe health-based limits:

  • PDE — Permitted Daily Exposure (ICH Q3C, Q3D; EMA 2014)
  • ADE — Acceptable Daily Exposure (ISPE Risk-MaPP; industrial hygiene)
  • ADI — Acceptable Daily Intake (food additives)
  • TI — Tolerable Intake
  • RfD / RfC — Reference Doses/Concentrations (US EPA)
  • OEL — Occupational Exposure Limits (OSHA PELs, ACGIH TLVs, EC SCOEL IOELVs)

For carcinogens: a different risk-based approach — ICH M7 uses 1 in 100,000 excess cancer risk for mutagenic impurities.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

HBEL vs. OEL：關鍵區別

這是 Risk-MaPP 最重要的概念區分之一：

致癌物的特殊處理：線性無閾值模型

一般毒性化合物使用「閾值模型」（NOAEL → 安全係數 → ADE）；但對基因毒性/致突變物質（mutagens），使用不同的「線性無閾值模型」：

  • ICH M7 設定 1/100,000（十萬分之一）終生超額癌症風險
  • TTC（毒理學關注閾值）= 1.5 μg/day（當數據不足時的保守預設值）
  • 這個數字比一般 ADE 通常要嚴格得多

比喻：速限的制定原理

ADE 就像道路速限——不是「越慢越安全」就越好。速限是根據道路設計、事故統計、使用者特性等數據科學制定的「平衡點」。人為將 ADE 降低十倍，就像把安全速限 60 km/h 改為 6 km/h——雖然更「保守」，但不必要的嚴格且不符合科學。

2.8 The GMP and Industrial Hygiene Balance（GMP 與工業衛生的平衡）

Original Text

A clear strategy is necessary to assess risk in either the Industrial Hygiene (IH) or cGMP setting and to define scientifically based criteria in order to make decisions for managing risk. Although criteria for both are derived from the same toxicological or clinical data, the way in which these data are used to derive acceptable limits and adequate control strategies will differ.

The key differences relate to the application and interpretation of target population, routes of exposure, and acceptability criteria. These are summarized in the table below:

Balancing the needs of both IH and GMP interests is very important in ensuring that all risks, to product or worker, are adequately managed. Only through recognizing the differing needs and identifying a strategy that can address both is it possible to achieve safe, efficient, and economic operation of a manufacturing facility.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

GMP 視角 vs. 工業衛生視角：為何兩者都重要

這兩個視角在製藥廠中代表兩個不同的職能部門：

  • GMP/品質部門：關注病患安全，產品殘留，清潔驗證
  • 工業衛生/HSE 部門：關注員工安全，工作環境暴露，PPE

問題：這兩個部門使用不同的標準體系，有時會產生矛盾。例如：某藥品 OEL = 0.01 mg/m³（工業衛生認為極危險）但 ADE = 5 mg/day（GMP 認為殘留風險很低）。如何整合？

OEL vs. ADE 的數值關係

兩者可以相互換算但不能直接比較：

  • OEL（mg/m³）需要乘以呼吸量（約 10 m³/8小時工作日）才能得到每日攝入量
  • ADE（mg/day）是更通用的基礎，可以轉換成任何暴露場景的限值
  • 通常：ADE < OEL 轉換後的日劑量（因為病患保護需要更嚴格）
  • 但也有例外：某些藥物對工人的吸入途徑特別危險（職業性哮喘），OEL 可能更嚴格

比喻：工廠消防安全 vs. 生產安全的協調

消防部門說：「這個化學品儲存量超過消防規定，必須減少」；生產部門說：「我們需要這個量才能保持生產連續性」。兩者都對，但需要一個整合方案。Risk-MaPP 的 IH-GMP 平衡就是同樣的整合思維——不能只顧一方而忽略另一方。

CDMO 組織架構啟示

這個章節對 CDMO 組織架構有直接啟示：

  • Risk-MaPP 風險評估團隊應同時包含 GMP/品質代表和工業衛生/HSE 代表
  • 新產品引入評估流程應同時觸發 GMP 風險評估（交叉污染）和 IH 暴露評估（員工安全）
  • 兩者都認為「可接受」才能啟動生產，不能只過一方的審核
  • 如果兩者結論衝突（例如 GMP 說 OK 但 IH 說需要更高防護），需要有明確的決策程序

本節重點摘要 Section Summary

  • Risk-MaPP 使命：為共用廠房的交叉污染風險管理提供科學的、基於 ICH Q9 的系統化方法，同時保護病患（GMP）和員工（IH）
  • 零風險哲學突破：ICH、FDA、EMA 三大機構一致認可「零風險不可及亦不必要」，以「可接受風險」替代「零容忍」作為決策標準
  • 五大修訂驅動：EU GMP Ch.3/5 更新、EMA HBEL 指引（2014）、ICH M7、生命週期驗證方法、業界經驗積累
  • 關鍵等號 PDE ≡ ADE：EMA 明確聲明兩者「本質上同義」，統一了 EU（PDE）與業界（ADE）的術語
  • 必須專用廠房的三個條件（EU GMP 3.6）：管制措施不足、毒理學不支持可控風險（如 Beta-Lactam 致敏性）、無法驗證的分析方法
  • HBEL vs. OEL 核心差異：HBEL（ADE/PDE）保護病患，以 mg/day 表達；OEL 保護工人，以 mg/m³ 表達——兩套標準需分別評估且同時滿足
  • 風險管理生命週期：識別 → 分析 → 評估 → 控制 → 降低 → 接受 → 審查 → 溝通（貫穿全程）——對應 Risk-MaPP 第 5-13 章
  • Annex 15 清潔驗證革命：2015 年更新要求清潔限值必須基於毒理學評估（ADE/PDE），取代舊有的 10 ppm 或 1/1000 TDD 經驗法則；PIC/S 同步跟進
3

Chapter 3: Quality System & Logic Diagram

品質系統與邏輯決策圖 | p23-p36

ISPE Baseline® Guide Volume 7 (2nd Ed.): Risk-Based Manufacture of Pharmaceutical Products

Chapter 3 — Quality System Requirements
ISPE Baseline® Guide Volume 7 (2nd Ed.): Risk-Based Manufacture | p23–p36

本章學習目標 Learning Objectives

  • 理解品質系統如何應用於交叉污染風險管理，並與 ICH Q10 生命週期方法整合
  • 掌握 Logic Diagram（邏輯圖）的結構與決策流程——GMP/法規邏輯 vs. 工業衛生邏輯
  • 分析各 GMP 因素（清潔、混淆預防、機械性轉移、空氣傳播）對共用設施可行性的影響
  • 評估健康/衛生因素（曝露評估、工程控制、PPE）對人員保護策略的重要性
  • 了解控制策略結果（專用設施 vs. 活動式製造 vs. 同期製造）對 CDMO 業務決策的意義

本節內容目錄

3.1 應用於交叉污染 3.1.1 建議品質政策 3.2 Logic Diagram 3.2.1 GMP/法規因素 3.2.2 健康衛生因素 3.2.3 控制策略結果 邏輯圖全覽
3

Quality System Requirements

Chapter 3 — p21–p22 | 品質系統要求：整體框架

3. Quality System Requirements

A well-defined quality system should consist of governance documents which are complemented by a concise set of tactical or procedural requirements. The overarching documentation matrix should provide the basis of consistency required for the creation of a sustainable quality system model which enables the ICH Q10 life cycle approach across the GxP regulated functions within an organization.

3.1 Application to Cross-Contamination

The key concepts discussed in this Guide should be used as a framework from which to develop standards, tools, and approaches to manage the risk of cross-contamination.

A case by case assessment should be performed of the risk factors that the concurrent manufacture of several products may cause. Risk assessments should be performed to properly understand the implications for both IH and GxP. While each is normally considered separately, to prevent any significant imbalance, the implications of decisions taken during an assessment for IH should be checked against those for GxP, and vice versa.

Figure 3.1🔍: Quality Management System — illustrates the governance hierarchy from quality policy through standards, SOPs, and forms, embedded in the ICH Q10 lifecycle framework.

中文解析 — 品質系統整體框架

核心概念：品質系統三層架構

ICH Q10 要求品質系統涵蓋整個產品生命週期。在交叉污染管理情境下，文件層級由上而下：

  • 政策層（Policy）：高層次宣示，由高階管理階層核准
  • 標準層（Standard）：技術性要求，如 ADE 決定程序
  • SOP 層：具體操作步驟（清潔、換產、風險評估）

重點提示：IH 與 GxP 雙軌評估

同一危害物質須同時進行兩條評估軌道，且結果必須相互對照：

  • GxP 角度：保護病人，使用 ADE（可接受日曝露量）
  • IH 角度：保護操作人員，使用 OEL（職業曝露限值）

若 IH 決策（如工程控制）影響 GxP 表現（如清潔可及性），必須重新評估。

比喻說明：品質系統如同城市法規

品質政策是憲法，標準是法律，SOP 是施工規範。三者缺一不可——憲法確立原則，法律設定邊界，施工規範確保每天的執行一致性。

3.1.1

Suggested Quality Policies / Standards for Managing CC Risk

p22–p23 | 建議的六大品質系統領域

3.1.1 Suggested Quality Policies / Standards for Managing the Risk of Cross-Contamination

While many aspects for managing the risk of cross-contamination are covered in various quality documents such as cleaning and cleaning validation, line clearance, etc., it is suggested that overarching quality policies, standards and SOPs are put in place to manage the risk of cross-contamination that tie together these various aspects.

Other quality systems that are impacted or related to managing the risk of cross-contamination include:

1. Technology Transfer (New Product Introduction)

Firms should have a well-documented procedure for assessing potential products prior to introducing them into the facility. This should include:

  • A mechanism that triggers an assessment of the potential cross-contamination risks prior to bringing the product/compound into the facility.
  • The hazards of the product(s) should be identified typically via an ADE monograph.
  • Cleaning process development prior to introducing the product into the facility.
  • Analytical methods sensitive enough to meet the required acceptance criteria.

2. Risk Management

The Risk Management quality system should provide a common understanding of risk and how to assess it. Senior management should provide guidance on how to determine acceptable and unacceptable risk. It is suggested that this be established at the corporate level so that there is a common understanding across the organization.

3. Change Control

It is suggested that the change control process includes a trigger for risk review when the change may impact the risk of cross-contamination. Such changes may include: new product introduction, the ADE value of product, maximum daily dose for products, equipment changes, facility changes including changes to HVAC or water quality/pressure, process changes, or procedure changes.

4. Corrective and Preventative Action (CAPA)

An outcome of the risk assessment activities may be to implement some risk reduction controls. The CAPA system may be used to track the risk mitigation measures until implemented and confirmation of performance is complete.

5. Product Quality Review

Results from the risk management process may become part of the product quality review as appropriate. In addition, requalification or monitoring programs should also provide an indication that the risk of cross-contamination is in a controlled state.

6. Training

It is important that basic GMP training for all relevant staff includes practices that are designed to avoid cross-contamination as well as understand how cross-contamination occurs. Staff involved in managing the risk of cross-contamination should have further training in both how to avoid cross-contamination and quality risk management.

中文解析 — 六大品質系統領域

系統性管理框架：六個交叉點

ISPE Vol.7 識別出六個與交叉污染風險管理交織的品質系統，每一個都是潛在控制點或失效點：

CDMO 業務重點：技術轉移觸發點

對 CDMO 而言，新產品引入（NPI）是最高風險時刻。ISPE 要求在化合物進入廠區之前就完成：

  • ADE 單體分析（毒理評估）
  • 清潔開發或歷史數據風險評估
  • 分析方法靈敏度確認

這個觸發機制應嵌入合約審查流程（Business Development → Quality → Engineering）。

實務應用：Change Control CC 觸發清單

以下任一變更應自動觸發 CC 風險重新評估：

  • 新產品或化合物引入
  • ADE 值更新或最大日劑量變更
  • 設備設計或材質變更
  • HVAC 配置或水系統壓力/品質變更
  • 製程規模放大或配方變更
  • 清潔程序或清潔劑變更

比喻：變更控制是「CC 的早期預警系統」

如同航空器維修系統——任何結構修改都會自動觸發安全審查，不需要靠人員記憶或手動觸發。CC 風險評估觸發應內建於 Change Control 流程，而非事後補做。

3.2

The Logic Diagram

p23 | 邏輯圖：決策框架總覽

3.2 The Logic Diagram

A logic diagram is a simple tool that can be used to guide a team through a process to determine the adequacy of existing controls or the need for dedicated facilities. (Section 3.6.1 should be read in conjunction with the flow diagram in Chapter 14.) Determining the need for dedicated facilities should be performed by a multidisciplinary team, so that all required areas are addressed appropriately.

The logic diagram is divided into two, addressing both GMP/Regulatory logic and IH logic. Both are equally important as they deal with aspects of risk associated with the different populations that may be exposed to the hazard under review:

  • Left side — product (patient risk)
  • Right side — worker (personnel risk)

Where dedicated facilities are implemented for business reasons, the risk assessment should clearly state that this is a business decision and not a cross-contamination issue.

中文解析 — Logic Diagram 的核心地位

Logic Diagram 是什麼？

Logic Diagram 是一個結構化決策工具，透過一系列是/否問題，引導跨職能團隊判斷：

  • 某產品是否可在共用設施製造？
  • 需要什麼程度的專用（dedication）？
  • 現有控制措施是否足夠？

結果有三種：共用設施可行 部分專用 完全專用設施

重點：業務決策 vs. CC 風險決策的區分

ISPE 特別強調：若基於商業原因（客戶要求、市場隔離）選擇專用設施，必須在風險評估文件中明確標注這是業務決策，而非 CC 控制必要性。

這樣做可防止：業務決策被誤解為監管要求，也避免未來類似產品引入時設定錯誤先例。

CDMO 應用：Logic Diagram 作為 BD 篩選工具

對 CDMO 而言，Logic Diagram 應成為新客戶/新品種業務審查的標準流程：

  • BD 階段：初步 ADE 篩查，快速判斷是否可接受
  • 技術評估階段：完整 Logic Diagram 評估，確定設施需求
  • 報價階段：將專用設備或隔離成本反映於合約條款

比喻：機場安全通道決策樹

Logic Diagram 如同機場入境流程——每個問題節點過濾一層風險。大多數旅客（低風險化合物）順利通過；少數需要進一步檢查（部分專用）；極少數被攔截要求特殊處理（專用設施）。重要的是：流程對所有人一視同仁，依風險而非直覺決策。

3.2.1

Considering the GMP / Regulatory Factors

p23–p29 | GMP 邏輯鏈：從法規要求到技術控制

3.2.1 GMP / Regulatory Factor — Logic Chain

3.2.1.1 Gathering Hazard Information (e.g., Health Based Criteria)

Both the IH and GMP criteria are drawn from common toxicological or clinical data sources. The ADE value is normally the health-based criterion used in assessing GMP concerns related to cross-contamination. The OEL is normally the health-based criterion used in assessing airborne product for worker protection.

3.2.1.2 Specific Requirements for Handling Product in a Dedicated Facility

"Is there a written regulation that would preclude the co-manufacture of this product with other non-related materials?"

The usual example is the beta-lactam class of antibiotics where 21 CFR 211.42(c)(d) requires separate facilities. The updated EU EudraLex Vol. 4 Section 3.6 requires dedicated facilities if:

  1. "the risk cannot be adequately controlled by operational and/or technical measures"
  2. "scientific data from the toxicological evaluation does not support a controllable risk (e.g. allergenic potential from highly sensitizing materials such as beta lactams)"
  3. "relevant residue limits, derived from the toxicological evaluation, cannot be satisfactorily determined by a validated analytical method."

Additional reasons to dedicate include: agency inspection consequence, internal QA recommendation, unique manufacturing technology, or high sales demand utilizing all capacity.

3.2.1.3 Determining an ADE

"Can an ADE be determined?"

If the scientific data supports the determination, then an ADE value should be determined and passed on to other stakeholders. If the information does not support the determination of an ADE value, then a dedicated facility is required. This is where the beta-lactam family of products would be addressed.

3.2.1.4 Detection of Residue Limits

"Can relevant residue limits be detected?"

Compounds that can be denatured/degraded/deactivated require studies to ensure the effectiveness of the process to render the residues safe. If analytical methods cannot be validated to the appropriate level, then a dedicated facility is necessary.

3.2.1.5 Technical and Operational Controls

"Do technical and operational controls manage the risk?"

Each of the modes of cross-contamination should be assessed to determine whether technical and operational controls can manage the risk. Care should be taken when assessing manual operations and the controls in place to detect manual errors.

中文解析 — GMP 因素決策鏈

重點：法規強制要求的第一道關卡

Logic Diagram 第一個問題直接問：是否有法規文字明確禁止共用製造？

答案是「是」的情況極少但清晰：

  • Beta-lactam 抗生素（21 CFR 211.42 / EU GMP 附錄）
  • 某些生物製品（活病毒疫苗）

若答案為「是」→ 直接終止評估，必須專用設施。不需要進一步 ADE 計算。

重點：無法確定 ADE = 無法共用製造

若化合物毒理數據不足以推導出 ADE（例如：早期臨床試驗化合物、毒理數據缺失），預設結論是需要專用設施。

這是 ISPE Vol.7 的關鍵邏輯：不是「沒有數據所以安全」，而是「沒有數據所以必須保守假設」。

實務應用：Analytical Method 靈敏度要求

分析方法必須在 ADE 計算所得清潔限值以下偵測到殘留。常見計算路徑：

  • ADE（mg/day）→ 計算最大殘留限值（MRL, μg/cm²）
  • LOQ 必須 ≤ MRL（通常要求 LOQ ≤ 50% MRL）
  • 若無法開發符合要求的方法 → 考慮部分或完全專用

3.2.1.6 Cleaning (Retention) Aspects

"Can cleaning be carried out to meet the required criteria?"

Factors to be considered include:

  • Feasibility: analytical detection capability; effects of aggressive cleaning agents on equipment materials
  • Practicability: consistency of manual vs. automated cleaning; procedure clarity
  • Cost: direct and indirect costs of extended clean-down, particularly for frequent changeovers
  • Patient: patient risk is the primary focus and supersedes operational considerations

If these factors can all be addressed satisfactorily, then the use of a multiproduct facility with shared equipment may be a viable option.

3.2.1.7–3.2.1.8 Cleaning Resolution and Partial Resolution

If the current method cannot be validated to appropriate sensitivity, consider improving the method. If partial resolution is possible, dedicating specific equipment in the train (rather than the entire facility) may be a cost-effective option.

3.2.1.9 Mix-Up Aspects

"Are procedures, controls, and facilities designed such that mix-up is avoided?"

Factors include:

  • Procedures/SOPs: areas where procedures may fail or be too complex to follow consistently
  • Controls: adequacy of existing controls; need for additional controls
  • Facility Design: no shared process flows or areas of overlap; effective procedure + control combination

3.2.1.12 Mechanical Transfer

"Is the potential for mechanical transfer to be controlled to safe predetermined levels?"

Factors include:

  • Process: is the process closed? Can material escape and be transported via equipment, personnel, or supplies?
  • Procedures: gown changes, equipment wipe-down prior to leaving processing rooms, foot/wheel transfer prevention
  • Facility: differential pressures between zones; GxP issues with personnel/material flow
  • Operational Standards: adequate training; engineering vs. procedural controls; CMO-specific considerations

3.2.1.15 Airborne Transfer

"Is the potential for airborne transfer to be controlled to safe predetermined levels?"

Factors include:

  • Process: is the product exposed to the room environment during processing, transfer, or cleaning? Is the process closed?
  • Facility: adequacy of differential pressures; material and personnel airlocks; HVAC performance

3.2.1.18 Accommodating Product in a Multiproduct Facility

"Can the product be accommodated in a multiproduct facility, but with more specific dedication?"

Options for limited dedication include:

  • Dedicated Suite/Room in a multiproduct facility
  • Dedicated Equipment: individual vessels, contact parts (feed chutes, compression tooling, filling heads)
  • Disposable Equipment: filling tubing, filters, glassware — with proper decontamination and disposal assessment

中文解析 — 清潔 / 混淆 / 機械/空氣傳播控制

重點：清潔評估的四個維度（病人優先）

ISPE 明確指出：成本和可行性考量不能凌駕於病人安全之上。評估順序：

  1. 可行性：分析方法能達到所需偵測限嗎？
  2. 可操作性：自動化 vs. 手動清潔的一致性
  3. 成本：週期性（年度 vs. 週次）清潔的經濟性
  4. 病人安全：最終判斷標準，不可妥協

CDMO 應用：CMO 特殊考量

ISPE 3.2.1.12 特別點名 CMO 情境：

  • 操作標準必須足以處理委託產品
  • 若依賴工程控制，換產時的隔離切換程序需特別評估
  • 員工是否需要化合物特定專業培訓？
  • 維修人員的交叉污染風險是否被納入評估？

這些問題在與新客戶簽訂技術協議時應逐一確認。

比喻：部分專用如同共用廚房分區

高級餐廳的廚房可能設有獨立的過敏原料理區（專用砧板、刀具），但使用共用烤箱。這就是「部分專用」的精神——針對風險點精準隔離，而非整個廚房廢止共用。ISPE 3.2.1.18 的三個選項（專用套房、專用設備、拋棄式設備）正是這種梯度思維的體現。

3.2.2

Considering the Health and Hygiene Factors (Personnel)

p30–p33 | 工業衛生邏輯：人員曝露評估與控制

3.2.2 Health and Hygiene Factors (Applicable to Personnel)

3.2.2.1 Gather Hazard Information

The OEL is normally the health-based criterion used in assessing airborne levels of API from bulk or finished product for protection of workers.

3.2.2.2 Assess Exposure Potential

Risk is a function of both hazard and exposure. Several factors should be considered:

  • Who is at risk? — Workers at the line, maintenance personnel, general personnel, QA personnel when sampling
  • What factors influence exposure? — Dusty powder? Liquid? Closed or open process? Training level? Routine or frequent task?
  • What is the exposure pathway? — Inhalation, ingestion, or skin absorption?
  • When is exposure most likely? — Sampling, process breakdown, clean down, or product changeover?

3.2.2.3 Control of Exposure

"Are the exposures adequately controlled?"

Review available information: adverse health effects reported? Monitoring data available? Similar processes in other facilities? Controls should be commensurate with the risk and consistent with manufacturing process requirements (e.g., engineering controls must not make interventions or cleaning difficult).

3.2.2.4 Process Changes

"Is elimination, substitution, or process change possible?"

Examples where this has been effective:

  1. Removal of a solid recovery step between stages in a chemical process
  2. Change to a wet granulation process from a direct blend process
  3. Addition of a film coat to a tablet to reduce exposure during packing
  4. Formulate as a liquid/semisolid in a capsule rather than a conventional tablet or powder filled capsule

3.2.2.5 Selection of Engineering Controls

Once risk factors have been investigated, control measures can be considered. Factors include: cost, feasibility, ergonomics, ease of cleaning, and failure mode operation (what happens if the control measure fails).

3.2.2.6 Level of Exposure Risk

"Is the exposure risk still too high?"

Is it reasonable to add in a secondary system, such as an extract system? Is routine use of PPE acceptable for short-duration activities? Discuss with operating personnel, plant management, and HSE specialists. Operators may prefer PPE if a rigid barrier makes a process step ergonomically difficult.

3.2.2.7 Emergency Recovery

"Is emergency recovery required?"

Considerations: what will need to be recovered? What supporting infrastructure is required — PPE, change areas, showers, storage for PPE, separate air supply to service PPE?

3.2.2.8 Secondary PPE

"Is secondary control or PPE required?"

The rationale for secondary PPE should be well understood and documented: is it provided to supplement a primary control measure, or for emergency use only?

中文解析 — IH 曝露評估與控制層級

工業衛生 (IH) 控制層級（Controls Hierarchy）

ISPE 遵循傳統工業衛生的控制優先順序：

  1. 消除 / 替代（最佳）：改變製程以消除曝露源
  2. 工程控制：密閉系統、通風、隔離屏障
  3. 行政控制：SOP、訓練、工作輪班
  4. 個人防護設備 PPE（最後手段）：口罩、手套、防護服

PPE 應視為補充工程控制的手段，不應作為主要防護措施。

重點：OEL vs. ADE 的關鍵差異

即使來自相同毒理數據，OEL 和 ADE 的應用情境不同：

  • OEL：保護健康成年工人，以 8 小時吸入量為基礎（μg/m³）
  • ADE：保護病人（包括老人、兒童、免疫低下者），以每日口服或注射劑量為基礎（mg/day）

因此同一化合物的 OEL 和 ADE 數值可能差異很大，應分別評估，不可相互替換。

比喻：工程控制如安全氣囊，PPE 如安全帶

安全氣囊（工程控制）是主動防護，設計上盡量讓乘客不需要靠它；安全帶（PPE）是被動防護，在主動防護失效時提供最後防線。兩者不可互相取代——PPE 的存在不能減少對工程控制的投資。

緊急恢復計畫的三要素

若主要圍堵系統失效，緊急應變計畫需包含：

  • What：需要回收什麼？由誰執行？
  • How：需要什麼基礎設施（PPE 儲存、更衣區、淋浴間）？
  • Air：是否需要獨立供氣系統服務防護 PPE？

緊急應變計畫應在產品引入前完成，而非在事故發生後才制定。

3.2.3

Consequences of Control Strategy

p33 | 控制策略的結果與回饋循環

3.2.3 Consequences of Control Strategy

The consequences of adopting any particular exposure control strategy should be rechecked against the GxP/regulatory logic to ensure plant operability is not compromised.

"The consequences of adopting any particular exposure control strategy should be rechecked against the GxP/regulatory logic to ensure plant operability is not comprised."
— ISPE Baseline Guide Vol. 7, Section 3.2.3

This bidirectional check is critical: decisions made purely on IH grounds (e.g., adding rigid physical barriers for worker protection) may inadvertently compromise GMP operability (e.g., making cleaning access impossible or creating contamination traps). Similarly, GMP-driven decisions must be re-evaluated for their impact on worker safety.

Three Possible Outcomes of the Logic Diagram

中文解析 — 控制策略結果與 CDMO 業務意義

三種決策結果的業務意涵

Logic Diagram 最終產出三種設施策略，每一種對 CDMO 的商業模式影響截然不同：

重點：雙向回饋循環的重要性

Section 3.2.3 的核心訊息：IH 決策與 GMP 決策不能各自獨立最優化。

典型衝突案例：

  • IH 要求密閉隔離箱 → GMP 清潔人員無法進入 → 殘留風險上升
  • GMP 要求開放式清潔設計 → 操作員粉塵曝露增加 → OEL 超標
  • IH 推薦一次性設備 → GMP 需要驗證拋棄性設備的殘留安全性

解決方案：跨職能評估，工程 + QA + IH 同時參與設計審查。

CDMO 業務決策流程建議

將 Logic Diagram 整合到新產品引入（NPI）的業務流程：

  1. BD 接洽時：索取化合物 ADE 或毒理概要，初步判斷可接受性
  2. 技術可行性評估：完整執行 Logic Diagram，確定設施策略
  3. 報價與合約：將專用設備成本、驗證費用、換產損失納入定價
  4. 技術協議：明確記載是 CC 控制需求還是業務決策的專用設施
  5. 定期回顧：ADE 值更新或製程變更時重新執行評估

比喻：Logic Diagram 如建築許可審查

在城市建設前，必須通過結構安全（GMP/病人安全）和消防規範（IH/人員安全）雙重審查。建商不能因為消防設施成本高就跳過——同樣地，CDMO 也不能因為 IH 控制成本高就忽略對製程的影響。兩個審查必須同時通過，且相互不矛盾。

Chapter 3 — Key Decision Points Summary

中文解析 — 章節總結與核心洞察

Chapter 3 四大核心洞察

  1. 品質系統是 CC 管理的骨架：技術轉移、變更控制、風險管理、CAPA 必須相互連結，形成完整的 CC 管控網絡。
  2. Logic Diagram 是客觀決策工具：跨職能團隊使用，防止主觀判斷和情緒性決策（如「這個化合物聽起來很危險所以一定要專用設施」）。
  3. ADE 是 GMP 邏輯的核心數值：無法確定 ADE = 無法科學評估風險 = 必須最保守假設（專用設施）。
  4. IH 與 GMP 必須雙向協調：兩者互為約束，任何控制策略必須同時滿足病人保護和人員安全，且不互相妥協。

CDMO 關鍵外帶訊息

對於 CDMO 的 Operations Director 而言，ISPE Vol.7 Chapter 3 提供了一個可防禦的、科學化的產品接受決策框架。

當客戶或稽查員質疑「為什麼這個化合物能在共用廠房製造？」，完整記錄的 Logic Diagram 評估結果就是最有力的答案——不是直覺，不是歷史慣例，而是系統化的風險評估文件。

這也是 ISPE Vol.7 相較於一般 GMP 指引最獨特的貢獻：它給了製造業者一個說「Yes，我們可以共用製造」的科學依據，而不僅僅是告訴你何時需要說「No」。

4-5

Chapter 4-5: Risk Assessment & Identification

風險評估與識別 | p37-p52

ISPE Baseline® Guide Volume 7 (2nd Ed.): Risk-Based Manufacture | p37–p52

本節目錄 Table of Contents

Ch.4 Risk Assessment Overview Ch.5 Risk Identification Intro 5.1 Hazard Definition 5.2 Hazard Continuum 5.3 Establishing HBEL 5.3.1 Data Collection 5.3.2 Critical Effect 5.3.3 Dose-Response 5.3.4 NOAEL / BMD 5.3.5 Adjustment Factors 5.4 Setting OEL 5.5 Documentation

學習目標 Learning Objectives

  1. 理解 ICH Q9 風險評估三步驟：風險識別、風險分析、風險評估。
  2. 區分「危害 (Hazard)」與「風險 (Risk)」的定義與應用範疇。
  3. 掌握危害連續光譜 (Hazard Continuum) 的分類邏輯與優先排序工具。
  4. 理解 HBEL（健康基礎暴露限值）的完整推導流程：NOAEL → 調整因子 → ADE/PDE。
  5. 區分 OEL（職業暴露限值）與 HBEL 的目的與計算差異。
  6. 了解 HBEL 評估文件的必要內容與資格要求。
4

Risk Assessment

ICH Q9 three-step framework — identification, analysis, evaluation | p37–38

Original Text — Chapter 4

Risk assessment as described in ICH Q9 encompasses three steps: risk identification, risk analysis, and risk evaluation. Each of the three steps helps to answer the three fundamental questions:

  • What might go wrong?
  • What is the likelihood (probability) it will go wrong?
  • What are the consequences (severity)?

The risk assessment steps may be considered the most important aspects of an overall quality risk management process. If the risks are not identified, analyzed, and evaluated properly, the decisions on how to control the risk cannot be made adequately.

The criteria for judging acceptability of risk for cross-contamination and operator exposures differ, although GxP and IH (Industrial Hygiene) considerations are linked because they share the same underlying toxicological data as the starting point from which they are both derived. In addition, the application and interpretation of the criteria in the risk assessment process will be different.

Part of the risk assessment process is to consider if there are realistically any plausible pathways that might give rise to an increased risk of exposure. For example, when considering airborne transfer, the following risk questions should be asked:

  • Can cross-contamination from an airborne pathway occur? Specifically, can product A be directly distributed via the air stream or resuspended back into the air (after being deposited) in a room/suite/facility, and then settle or get redeposited directly into product B or onto contact parts?
  • Can this occur in sufficient amount that the ADE for product A might be exceeded should a patient be administered the now contaminated product B?
  • Is it plausible for product that has been deposited on equipment or adjacent work surfaces to be redispersed into the air stream and present an exposure risk for operators via inhalation?

Similar questions should be asked to understand the risks associated with mix-up, retention, and mechanical transfer.

At the conclusion of the risk assessment, risk should be expressed in quantitative or qualitative terms depending on the data available from the three steps. This information should then be used in the decision making to accept or reduce the risks under the risk control steps.

解說 Commentary

ICH Q9 風險評估三步驟

  • 風險識別 (Risk Identification)：確認「什麼可能出錯？」，辨識所有危害及其可能後果。
  • 風險分析 (Risk Analysis)：估計已識別危害的風險大小，評估暴露可能性與嚴重度。
  • 風險評估 (Risk Evaluation)：對照可接受標準，判斷風險是否需要控制。

三步驟缺一不可：若危害識別不完整，後續分析與決策必然失準。

GxP vs. IH — 同源異用

共同基礎：兩者都源自相同的毒理學數據（NOAEL、LOAEL、劑量反應）。

差異在應用：

  • GxP (交叉污染控制)：保護病患，問題是「殘留物是否超過 ADE？」
  • IH (工業衛生)：保護操作員，問題是「空氣中濃度是否超過 OEL？」

風險可接受標準不同，但數據來源相通，計算邏輯相似。

實例思考：空氣傳播路徑評估

製造 Product A 的粉塵懸浮在空氣中 → 沉降到 Product B 的開口容器 → 病患服用含殘留的 Product B。

關鍵問題：「沉降量是否讓病患暴露超過 Product A 的 ADE？」這就是跨污染風險評估的核心邏輯。

四種暴露路徑 (Transfer Mechanisms)

  • Mix-up（混淆）：標籤、實物配置錯誤
  • Retention（殘留）：清潔不完全的殘餘物
  • Mechanical transfer（機械轉移）：設備接觸面帶走的殘留
  • Airborne transfer（空氣傳播）：粉塵、氣溶膠懸浮後沉降

每條路徑須分別評估可行性，並以合理可信的情境為基礎（Plausible Pathway 原則）。

5

Risk Identification — Introduction

Qualitative hazard identification as first step in risk assessment | p37

Original Text — Chapter 5 Intro

This Chapter describes risk identification, which starts with qualitative hazard identification, i.e., the process by which existing hazards are identified, initially without assigning magnitude. All available animal and human data should be reviewed to address the question: "What could go wrong?"

This first step in the risk assessment process also includes identifying possible consequences. It serves as a prelude to later steps of risk analysis and risk evaluation that ultimately lead to appropriate exposure control and management of risk.

解說 Commentary

風險識別的本質

定性、不定量：第一步只需識別危害是否存在，無需立刻計算數值大小。

資料基礎：需要系統性地回顧所有動物及人體研究數據。

前置功能：為後續的「風險分析（量化暴露）」與「風險評估（與標準比對）」打好基礎。

比喻

就像急診分診：先確認病人有什麼問題（危害識別），才能排優先順序（風險評估）並決定治療方案（風險控制）。跳過分診直接開藥，後果不堪設想。

5.1

Definition of Hazard

Active pharmacological, toxicological, microbiological properties | p37–38

Original Text — Section 5.1

Hazard is defined in ICH Q9 as a potential source of harm. ICH Q9 also includes the severity of harm in the definition of risk. Within the context of this Guide, hazard describes the inherent property of a compound to produce adverse effects, e.g., in patients that may be exposed to the compound as a trace contaminant in another pharmaceutical product.

The compounds typically considered include:

  • APIs (Active Pharmaceutical Ingredients)
  • Process intermediates
  • Solvents
  • Excipients

Other compounds that may need to be considered include impurities, byproducts, and degradants. Each compound has its own inherent ability to cause adverse effects (i.e., toxicity) — effects that may be well documented in the case of the API, but may be unknown for other compounds.

解說 Commentary

危害 (Hazard) 的定義

ICH Q9 定義：一種潛在的傷害來源（a potential source of harm）。

本指南的特定意義：化合物對人體造成不良影響的「固有屬性」，包括：

  • 藥理活性 (Pharmacological)：治療劑量即有作用的化合物，低量暴露也可能影響病患。
  • 毒理特性 (Toxicological)：在超過安全劑量時導致器官毒性、致癌或生殖毒性。
  • 微生物危害 (Microbiological)：雖本章聚焦於化學性危害，微生物污染亦屬廣義危害範疇。

哪些化合物需要評估？

  • API：資料最完整，通常有完整的毒理數據包。
  • 中間體 (Intermediates)：合成過程化合物，毒理資料往往有限。
  • 溶劑 (Solvents)：依 ICH Q3C 分類，有殘留限量要求。
  • 賦形劑 (Excipients)：通常認為低毒，但特殊族群（兒童、腎病患者）仍需關注。
  • 雜質/降解物 (Impurities/Degradants)：最難評估，往往缺乏完整毒理數據，需以 TTC 方法估算。

危害 vs. 風險 — 核心區別

危害 (Hazard) = 化合物固有的傷害能力（inherent property）。

風險 (Risk) = 危害 × 暴露可能性（Hazard × Probability of Exposure）。

即使是高危害化合物（如強效細胞毒素），若暴露路徑被完全阻斷，實際風險可以接近零。這正是多產品廠房風險管理的核心邏輯。

5.2

Hazard Continuum and Prioritization

From no hazard to poorly characterised hazard — OEB/OEL estimation | p38–39

Original Text — Section 5.2

Depending on the hazardous properties of an individual compound, resulting from its mechanism-of-action and potency, health-based limits such as the ADE values can span several orders of magnitude. It is preferable to derive health-based values for all pharmaceutical compounds, regardless of potency, to ensure the protection of patients.

Similarly, there is a need to focus attention on those compounds with the lowest health-based exposure limits because these may be the compounds that are the most difficult to control, and the consequences of overexposure may be the greatest.

As part of an overall risk management approach, it is useful to have a qualitative tool to help determine the need for, and to prioritize, comprehensive quantitative risk assessments. This tool should ideally incorporate the severity of the effect/impact on quality of life, reversibility of the effect and likelihood of death.

Criteria for identifying hazardous drugs and prioritizing risk assessments include:

  1. Genotoxic compounds that are known to be or highly likely to be carcinogenic to humans
  2. Compounds that can produce reproductive and/or developmental effects at low dosages*
  3. Compounds that can produce serious target organ toxicity or other significant adverse effects at low dosages*

*For example clinical doses <1 to 10 mg/day or animal doses <0.1 to 1 mg/kg/day

The use of Occupational Exposure Limits (OELs) and Occupational Exposure Bands (OEBs) can be used to estimate ADE values for the purpose of prioritization in risk assessments. Extrapolating an OEL to an ADE value, in its simplest sense, is accomplished by:

ADE (µg/day) = OEL (µg/m³) × 10 m³

Many companies assign new compounds to an OEB, or equivalent designation corresponding to airborne concentration ranges, to provide guidance on safe handling before sufficient data are available to establish a numerical OEL.

Table 5.1: Estimating ADE Values Using OEBs

* Estimated ADE = Low End of Band × 10 m³

解說 Commentary

危害連續光譜 (Hazard Continuum)

危害程度並非二分法（危險/安全），而是一條連續帶，依化合物作用機制與效力跨越數個數量級：

無危害
No Hazard
ADE > 10 mg/day
特徵明確危害
Well-Characterised
ADE 0.01–10 mg/day
特徵不明危害
Poorly Characterised
ADE < 0.01 mg/day

對 ADE 極低的化合物（如細胞毒性藥物、高效激素），控制成本高，超標後果嚴重，優先進行詳細風險評估。

三類高危藥物識別標準

  • 基因毒性致癌物：ICH M7 適用；需以 TTC 或線性外推計算 ADE。
  • 生殖/發育毒性：低劑量即可能影響胎兒或生育能力，調整因子需包含 AFD。
  • 器官毒性高效藥：臨床劑量 <1–10 mg/day 即有顯著效應，ADE 估值極低。

OEB 快速估算 ADE（優先排序用）

在正式 ADE 文件尚未建立前，可用 OEB 作為臨時分類工具：

ADE (µg/day) = OEL_low_end (µg/m³) × 10 m³

例如：OEB 4 的低端濃度 = 1 µg/m³
估算 ADE = 1 × 10 = 10 µg/day

注意：OEB 估算值僅供優先排序，不可替代正式毒理評估建立的 ADE。一旦有足夠數據，應建立正式 ADE 文件。

CDMO 實務應用

承接新分子時，若客戶尚未提供正式 ADE 文件：

  • 先以 OEB 分類估算 ADE，決定清潔驗證目標及廠房配置要求。
  • 要求客戶提供毒理數據包；CMO 有責任確保所有製造的化合物都有科學根據的 ADE。
  • 若無任何數據，適用 TTC 方法：潛在致癌物 1 µg/day，高毒性 10 µg/day，一般化合物 100 µg/day。
5.3

Establishing Health-Based Exposure Limits (HBEL)

Foundation of risk-based manufacturing — hazard identification + dose-response + limit derivation | p40

Original Text — Section 5.3

The foundation of a risk-based approach for manufacturing pharmaceutical products comprises:

  • The identification of hazards
  • Assessment of dose-response relationships
  • Establishment of health-based limits

The identification of hazards and assessment of dose-response relationships are collectively referred to as hazard characterization.

Having an understanding of how a compound can cause harm, and at what dose, is crucial to evaluating risks and deciding on appropriate exposure controls.

The approach used to derive ADE values is consistent with a number of guidance documents on setting health-based exposure limits (e.g., WHO 2005). The EMA guidance document on setting Permitted Daily Exposure limits (PDEs) based on the ICH Q3C(R6) guidance for residual solvents utilizes a similar set of adjustment (assessment) factors. The PDE is essentially synonymous with the ADE.

In practice, the methods used to derive health-based exposure limits may differ slightly, but it is the responsibility of the organization to ensure that all relevant sources of uncertainty and variability are addressed, regardless of which adjustment factor covers them, and that their recommended limits are scientifically defensible and adequately protective.

解說 Commentary

HBEL 三個縮寫的關係

  • HBEL (Health-Based Exposure Limit)：總稱，所有以健康數據為基礎推導的暴露限值。
  • ADE (Acceptable Daily Exposure)：ISPE Risk-MaPP 使用的術語，用於清潔驗證和跨污染評估。
  • PDE (Permitted Daily Exposure)：EMA 指南和 ICH Q3C 使用的術語。

ADE ≈ PDE，數值應相近，差異來自調整因子的選取細節。

HBEL 的法規驅動力

EU GMP Annex 15 (2015) 要求多產品設施必須以 HBEL/ADE 作為清潔驗證的設定依據，取代早期的 1/1000 治療劑量法則。

HBEL 方法被認為更科學且更具針對性，因為它考慮了化合物特定的毒理特性，而非統一套用安全係數。

危害特徵化 (Hazard Characterization) 的兩個組成

  • 危害識別：確認化合物有哪些毒理端點（致癌、生殖毒性、器官毒性等）。
  • 劑量反應評估：量化在什麼劑量下、多嚴重的效應會出現。

兩者合力，才能定義出「臨界效應 (Critical Effect)」及其對應的 NOAEL，進而計算 ADE。

5.3.1

Data Collection and Analysis

Qualified toxicologist, regulatory data, literature sources | p40–41

Original Text — Section 5.3.1

For hazard identification, a formal review of all available relevant animal and human data should be performed for each compound. This review should be done by a qualified toxicologist. This is an individual that has many years of experience setting health-based limits such as ADE values and OELs, preferably in the pharmaceutical industry. Specific training in toxicology is necessary, whether at MS or PhD level, but degrees in related fields such as pharmacology or medicine may be sufficient when coupled with appropriate specific training and experience.

For the innovator companies that developed the API, the data used in the analysis should include the data submitted in the regulatory filing. Contract Manufacturing Organizations (CMOs) should request this information, and the rationale for the ADE that may have already been derived, from the innovator company asking them to manufacture the drug.

The reviewer should have access to the full range of preclinical and clinical data required for approval of the drug. For non-proprietary compounds, all relevant information on the potential hazards of the material should be obtained through reliable sources. Standard toxicology and pharmacology reference texts should be consulted and a literature search (e.g., on PubMed) should be performed.

Caution should be used when utilizing Safety Data Sheets (SDSs) as a reference source, since the credibility of the information may vary.

The toxicologist performing the hazard assessment and calculating the health-based exposure limit is responsible for assessing the gathered data from the publicly available sources with regard to relevancy, adequacy, and reliability of the collected information.

解說 Commentary

合格毒理學家 (Qualified Toxicologist)

ADE/HBEL 必須由合格毒理學家建立，不得由一般 QA 或化學人員代替。資格要求：

  • 毒理學、藥理學或相關學科碩士或博士學位。
  • 具有設定 ADE/OEL 的實際工作經驗（偏好製藥業背景）。
  • DABT（美國毒理學委員會認證）或同等認證為加分項，但非強制。

CDMO 如無內部毒理學家，應委託有資格的第三方毒理諮詢機構。

資料來源優先順序

  1. 最優先：創新藥廠提交的法規申請文件（NDA/MAA 的毒理數據包）。
  2. 次選：PubMed 同行評審文獻，FDA/EMA 公開摘要。
  3. 輔助：毒理學教科書、藥理學參考書。
  4. 謹慎使用：SDS（安全資料表）— 品質參差不齊，不應作為主要毒理依據。

CMO/CDMO 的特殊責任

當受託製造時：

  • 應主動向委託方索取完整毒理數據包和已建立的 ADE 文件。
  • 若委託方無法提供，CMO 有責任自行委外建立 ADE。
  • EU GMP Annex 15 明確要求：多產品設施每個化合物都需有 HBEL，無論是創新藥廠還是 CMO 操作。
5.3.2

Identification of the Critical Effect

First clinically significant adverse effect as dose increases | p41

Original Text — Section 5.3.2

The purpose of a hazard evaluation is to identify all possible hazards associated with a compound and to rank them according to their severity. When combined with a dose-response assessment, the critical effect can be defined. This is typically the first clinically significant adverse effect that is observed as the dose increases.

The critical effect should be used for the derivation of an ADE. Ideally, the critical effect should be derived from studies for the same route that the ADE value will be used to evaluate. Extrapolation from data for other routes may be necessary if relevant route specific data are not available.

Exposures below the NOAEL for the critical effect should not, by definition, lead to other effects, as these will only occur at higher doses.

The reviewing toxicologist should determine which of the effects reported at low dosages is the critical effect. It may be necessary to evaluate several endpoints, which may involve different sets of adjustment factors. A justification should be made considering the final ADE value, which is based on the most sensitive effect relevant to humans.

Due to differences in the route of exposure, the toxicological profile of the compound in question and the potential for local effects at the site of contact, the critical effect may be different for patients and operators.

Professional judgment is required to discern between biological effects that may be physiological or adaptive changes or subclinical pharmacological effects of the drug, which would have associated Lowest-Observed-Effect Levels (LOELs). These biological effects should be distinguished from clinically significant effects which are considered adverse effects.

Clinically significant effects should be considered adverse effects for anyone not under the supervision of a physician prescribing this drug for a specific medical condition. These would have associated Lowest-Observed-Adverse-Effect Level (LOAELs). Quite often, the LOAEL for these effects is used as the Point-of-Departure (PoD) for derivation of the ADE value.

解說 Commentary

臨界效應 (Critical Effect) 的定義

定義：隨劑量增加，最早出現的臨床顯著不良效應。

選擇邏輯：

  • 在所有已記錄的毒理效應中，找出最低劑量即出現且具臨床意義的效應。
  • 以此效應的 NOAEL 作為推導 ADE 的起始點（Point-of-Departure）。
  • 理論上，若暴露低於 critical effect 的 NOAEL，其他效應（在更高劑量才出現）也不會發生。

病患 vs. 操作員的臨界效應可能不同

口服藥物：病患暴露路徑為口服，臨界效應可能是全身性毒性。

製造操作員：主要暴露路徑為吸入或皮膚接觸，臨界效應可能是局部刺激、呼吸道敏感化。

因此，同一化合物的 OEL（保護操作員）和 ADE（保護病患）可能基於不同的臨界效應，使用不同的調整因子組合。

比喻

選擇臨界效應如同橋樑設計的「最弱構件」原則：整座橋的承重能力由最脆弱的那根樑決定。ADE 由最敏感的毒理端點（臨界效應的 NOAEL）決定，而不是取所有效應的平均值。

5.3.3

Dose-Response Assessment

Threshold for systemic toxicity vs. no-threshold for genotoxic carcinogens | p41–42

Original Text — Section 5.3.3

During the hazard characterization process, all effects potentially attributed to a compound should be documented. Each effect, whether considered adverse or not, has a dose-response relationship. In general, as the dose increases, the incidence and severity of the effect increases.

For systemic toxicity endpoints, there is a dose below which no effects are expected. This is often referred to as the threshold for toxicity.

For some endpoints such as cancer, due to direct damage to DNA, it is often assumed that a threshold does not exist and some effects (e.g., mutations) are possible at low doses. In this case, it is necessary to determine the acceptable level of response for the effect (e.g., a 1/100,000 excess cancer risk). It should be noted that this may be viewed as a conservative approach given that there are DNA repair mechanisms that may reverse the mutations and immunosurveillance mechanisms that prevent cancers from developing.

解說 Commentary

劑量反應關係的兩種模型

閾值模型 (Threshold Model)：適用於大多數毒理端點（肝毒性、腎毒性、生殖毒性）。存在 NOAEL，低於此劑量無不良效應。使用調整因子法（Safety Factor Approach）計算 ADE。

無閾值線性模型 (Linear No-Threshold)：適用於基因毒性致癌物（Genotoxic Carcinogens）。理論上任何劑量都有風險（DNA 一次損傷可能導致突變）。需以「可接受風險水準」推算，如 1/100,000 額外致癌風險。ICH M7 採用此方法。

比喻：閾值 vs. 無閾值

閾值毒性：就像杯子容量，少量飲料不會溢出（低於 NOAEL = 無效應）。

無閾值致癌性：就像骰子，每擲一次都有機率出現 6（每次 DNA 損傷都有可能成為突變）。劑量越低，風險越小，但永遠不為零。

實務意義

  • 一般 API（有 NOAEL 數據）：用調整因子法計算 ADE，設計清潔限量。
  • 基因毒性化合物（如烷化劑、某些 API 雜質）：用線性外推，TDI = 1.5 µg/day 為終身暴露基準（ICH M7）。
  • DNA 修復機制的存在使無閾值假設較保守，但因無法準確量化每個人的修復能力，監管機構仍以保守值為預設。
5.3.4

Establishment of the NOAEL or Benchmark Dose

NOAEL definition, LOAEL limitation, BMD as mathematical alternative | p42

Original Text — Section 5.3.4

For most toxicity endpoints, there is a clear dose-response relationship for the critical effect. The aim is to define the NOAEL for the critical effect, which may be used to derive the ADE. The application of adjustment factors (see Section 5.3.5) results in ADE values that are unlikely to produce any undesirable compound-related effects.

It may not be possible to define the NOAEL for some toxicology data sets, and therefore, it may be necessary to derive the health-based limit using a LOAEL. This occurs when statistically significant adverse effects are observed at the lowest dose used in a study. The Benchmark Dose (BMD) can be used in this situation.

The BMD is a value, equivalent to a NOAEL, that is derived mathematically by fitting a curve to the dose-response data for the critical effect. The BMD10 is defined as the dose that corresponds to a 10% response rate, the minimum level of response typically detected by standard toxicology studies. The statistical lower bound on the BMD10 (BMDL10) is often used in risk assessments as a surrogate for a NOAEL. Caution should be taken when extrapolating well below the observable range.

解說 Commentary

BMD 與 NOAEL 的關係

當最低劑量組已出現統計顯著的不良效應（即只有 LOAEL 無 NOAEL 時）：

方案 1：以 LOAEL 作為 PoD，並加上 AFL（LOAEL-to-NOAEL factor）= 3 來補償。

方案 2：使用 BMD 軟體（US EPA BMDS）對劑量反應數據擬合曲線，取 BMDL10 作為等效 NOAEL。

BMDL10 ≈ NOAEL equivalent (no AFL needed)

BMD 方法在數學上更嚴謹，但需要足夠的劑量組數據以擬合曲線。

為何 NOAEL 有局限性？

NOAEL 受研究設計影響：若研究只有 3 個劑量組且間距大，NOAEL 可能高估無效應劑量。BMD 方法透過數學建模，能更精確反映劑量反應關係，不受劑量組設計限制。

5.3.5

Application of Adjustment Factors — ADE/PDE Calculation

Interspecies, intraspecies, duration, severity, LOAEL conversion, PK adjustments | p42–47

Original Text — Section 5.3.5

Health-based exposure limits, such as ADE values, are derived by dividing the NOAEL for the critical effect (after adjusting for body weight, e.g., 50 kg) by various adjustment factors (also termed assessment, safety, or uncertainty factors) to extrapolate to the "true" no effect level in the subpopulation of interest (e.g., elderly patients).

These are multiplied together to form a Composite Adjustment Factor (AFC) that is used in the denominator of the general equation used to set health-based limits.

ADE Calculation Formula (ISPE Risk-MaPP):
ADE (mg/day) = (PoD × BW) / (AFC × MF × PK)
PDE Calculation Formula (EMA):
PDE = (NOAEL × BW) / (F1 × F2 × F3 × F4 × F5)

Key adjustment factors:

  • AFA / F1 (Interspecies): Extrapolates from animal NOAEL to human. Allometric scaling, values 2–12 depending on species.
  • AFH / F2 (Intraspecies): Accounts for variability within the human population (kinetics + dynamics). Default = 10.
  • AFS / F3 (Study Duration): Adjusts when study duration is shorter than exposure scenario. Typically 3 (Risk-MaPP) or 10 (EMA, studies <4 weeks).
  • AFL / F5 (LOAEL-to-NOAEL): Applied when only LOAEL is available. Default = 3.
  • AFD (Database Completeness): Missing DART studies. Default = 3.
  • MF / F4 (Modifying Factor / Severity): Residual uncertainties, severity of effect, slope of dose-response. Range: <1 to 10.
  • PK (Pharmacokinetic): Bioavailability correction for route-to-route extrapolation.

Table 5.2: Adjustment Factors Used in EMA Guidance and Risk-MaPP

解說 Commentary

ADE / PDE 計算公式解析

ISPE Risk-MaPP (ADE)：

ADE = (PoD × BW) / (AFC × MF × PK)

EMA Guideline (PDE)：

PDE = (NOAEL × BW) / (F1 × F2 × F3 × F4 × F5)

各參數意義：

  • PoD / NOAEL：臨界效應的無不良效應劑量（mg/kg/day）
  • BW：標準病患體重，通常 50 kg（考量最脆弱族群）
  • AFC：複合調整因子 = AFA × AFH × AFS × AFL × AFD
  • MF：修正因子，處理剩餘不確定性和效應嚴重度
  • PK：藥代動力學調整，如生物利用度校正

計算範例（簡化）：

NOAEL = 5 mg/kg/day (大鼠 90-day oral study)
BW = 50 kg
AFA = 5 (大鼠 → 人, allometric)
AFH = 10 (人體個體差異)
AFS = 3 (90 天 → 終身)
AFL = 1 (有 NOAEL)
AFD = 1 (DART 研究完整)
MF  = 1 (無額外不確定性)
PK  = 1 (口服 → 口服, 無需校正)

AFC = 5 × 10 × 3 × 1 × 1 = 150
ADE = (5 × 50) / (150 × 1 × 1) = 250/150 ≈ 1.67 mg/day

Risk-MaPP vs. EMA — 主要差異

研究時長因子（F3/AFS）：EMA 對 <4 週研究使用 F3 = 10，Risk-MaPP 使用 AFS = 3。Risk-MaPP 基於更廣泛的實證文獻，認為 3 已足夠保護。

嚴重度因子（F4/MF）：EMA 在 F4 和 F5 各自處理，Risk-MaPP 以 MF 統一處理殘餘不確定性。需注意避免雙重計算（double counting）。

結果：相同化合物，兩種方法的 ADE/PDE 應相近，但具體值可能有差異。監管機構通常接受任一方法，只要有充分的科學說明。

化合物特異性調整因子 (CSAF)

當有具體的 PK/PD 數據時，可用 CSAF 取代默認的 10 倍種內差異因子（AFH）。

CSAF 由實測數據的統計分佈計算（均值 + 2 個標準差）/均值。

對新藥開發階段（有大量 PK 數據）特別有用，可讓 ADE 更精確，避免過度設計製造控制。

生物利用度校正的實際情境

若 NOAEL 來自口服研究（oral bioavailability = 50%），但需評估靜脈注射產品的跨污染風險（100% bioavailability）：

ADE_IV = ADE_oral × (oral BA / IV BA) = ADE_oral × (50% / 100%) = ADE_oral / 2

即靜脈產品的 ADE 需減半，清潔限量更嚴格。這在口服和靜脈產品共線生產（如 CDMO 同廠生產多劑型）時尤為重要。

5.4

Setting Occupational Exposure Limits (OEL)

Worker protection vs. patient protection — different targets, same toxicological data | p48–49

Original Text — Section 5.4

The primary purpose of this Chapter is to describe methods to set ADE values for patient protection; however, similar quantitative health-based assessments are performed to set OELs to protect workers handling these substances.

The safe level of exposure for patients may be different from that established for workers. This is because the critical effect used to derive the limits may be different due to differences in the anticipated route of exposure, and even where this is the same, the choice of adjustment factors may differ. Workers are generally healthy individuals, whereas patients may be children or elderly, and by definition, have at least one active medical condition.

Adjustments may be necessary to address route-to-route extrapolation, even if the same critical effect is used. For example, an OEL derived from the ADE may need to be adjusted for differences in bioavailability between the route used to identify the critical effect (e.g., oral) and the anticipated route of exposure (e.g., inhalation).

If the same assumptions apply regarding the critical effect, susceptible subpopulations, and bioavailability (e.g., 100%), an OEL can be calculated directly from the ADE by dividing the dose allowed by the volume of air breathed by a worker, typically 10 m³, engaged in light work for 8 hours:

OEL (µg/m³) = ADE (µg/day) / 10 m³

Surface target values (e.g., wipe limits), which are used for worker protection, can also be derived by dividing the dose permitted in 8 hours at the OEL (i.e., OEL × 10 m³) by a standard surface area (e.g., 100 cm²).

While it may be tempting to use wipe limits to assess the potential for cross-contamination, it is important to emphasize that they are developed for worker safety purposes. Any other use must be done within the context of a risk assessment for patient safety (cross-contamination) when considering specific plausible pathways of exposure to product.

解說 Commentary

OEL 與 ADE 的換算

假設條件：相同臨界效應、相同調整因子、吸入生物利用度 = 100%

OEL (µg/m³) = ADE (µg/day) ÷ 10 m³

例如：ADE = 100 µg/day

OEL = 100 ÷ 10 = 10 µg/m³

表面擦拭限量（Wipe Limit，用於工作場所保護）：

Wipe Limit = OEL × 10 m³ ÷ 100 cm² = ADE ÷ 100 cm²

注意：此擦拭限量用途為工業衛生，不等同於清潔驗證的殘留限量。

關鍵區別：擦拭限量 ≠ 清潔驗證限量

擦拭限量（工業衛生 Wipe Limit）：評估設備外表面，確保不會污染操作員的接觸環境。目的：保護工人。

清潔驗證殘留限量（Cleaning Validation Limit）：評估產品接觸面的殘留，確保後續批次不會使病患暴露超過 ADE。目的：保護病患。

兩者來源相似，但情境不同。用工業衛生擦拭限量來判定清潔驗證合格，是錯誤的方法。

為什麼 OEL 和 ADE 數值可能不同？

  • 臨界效應不同：操作員主要吸入暴露，臨界效應可能是肺部刺激；病患口服，臨界效應可能是肝毒性。
  • 目標族群不同：OEL 保護健康成人（較少調整），ADE 保護病患含敏感族群（調整因子更保守）。
  • 生物利用度不同：口服吸收率與吸入吸收率可能差異很大，需各自校正。
5.5

Documentation of the Health-Based Exposure Limit

Formal written document requirements for ADE/HBEL assessment | p49

Original Text — Section 5.5

The scientific rationale for the recommended health-based limit (e.g., ADE) should be summarized in a formal written document. The document should include a summary to facilitate review by stakeholders and the basis for the ADE should be clearly described.

The reader should be able to readily determine:

  • The health endpoint (critical effect) on which the ADE was established
  • The values chosen for adjustment factors
  • Which sources of variability and uncertainty they address
  • Any further adjustments (e.g., bioavailability correction)

The format of the documentation of the ADE does not need to be standardized; however, it should be used consistently within a given company. The documentation should include sections addressing the following:

  1. Identity information, physico-chemical properties and chemical structure
  2. Intended use and mechanism of action
  3. Pharmacokinetics and pharmacodynamics in animals and humans
  4. Animal data including acute toxicity, local effects, repeat dose toxicity, developmental and reproductive toxicity, genotoxicity, carcinogenicity
  5. Veterinary use if applicable
  6. Human data including clinical use, adverse reactions, susceptible subpopulations, pregnancy and nursing mothers
  7. Identification of the critical effect
  8. References
  9. Qualifications of the expert author (e.g., toxicologist)
  10. Appendices with detailed calculations of ADE value, chemical-specific adjustment factors, etc.

The level of detail in the documentation should be commensurate with the level of hazard and risk associated with the specific compound.

解說 Commentary

HBEL 文件的目的

ADE/HBEL 文件不只是計算報告，更是一份毒理科學論證，用於：

  • 支持清潔驗證殘留限量設定的科學依據。
  • 供監管機構審核（EU GMP Annex 15 要求）。
  • 作為廠房分類和工程控制決策的依據。
  • 在審計或客戶技術轉移時提供透明的數據鏈。

ADE 文件的 10 個必要章節

  1. 化合物識別：CAS 號、分子式、結構式、物化特性（溶解度、揮發性、粒徑分佈）
  2. 用途與作用機制：適應症、藥理機制、治療劑量範圍
  3. PK/PD 數據：動物和人體的吸收、分佈、代謝、排泄、生物利用度
  4. 動物毒理數據：急性毒性、重複劑量毒性（28 天/90 天/慢性）、發育生殖毒性、基因毒性、致癌性
  5. 獸藥使用：若為獸醫用 API，需說明對人類食品安全的影響
  6. 人體數據：臨床試驗、上市後不良反應報告、敏感族群資料
  7. 臨界效應識別：選定依據、端點、NOAEL/LOAEL 值
  8. 參考文獻：所有引用的研究來源
  9. 作者資格：毒理學家的學歷、認證、相關經驗
  10. 附錄：完整計算過程、調整因子選取理由、化合物特異性數據

文件詳盡程度 = 風險等級

指南明確指出：文件詳盡程度應與化合物的危害和風險等級相稱。

  • 低危化合物（ADE > 1 mg/day）：精簡版文件，重點列出關鍵數據點和 ADE 計算即可。
  • 高危化合物（ADE < 10 µg/day）：完整版文件，須包含所有毒理端點的詳細分析和充分的科學論證。
  • 基因毒性/致癌物：還需納入線性外推方法的說明和癌症風險計算。

實務思考：你的組織 ADE 管理現況如何？

  • 公司內有合格毒理學家，還是都委外執行 ADE 評估？
  • 每個在廠生產的化合物是否都有書面 ADE 文件？
  • ADE 文件是否定期更新（如新毒理研究發表、適應症擴展）？
  • 清潔驗證的殘留限量是否可以追溯到 ADE 文件？
  • 客戶要求製造新化合物時，ADE 文件是商業合約的交付項目嗎？

EU GMP Annex 15 的文件要求實踐

2015 年版 Annex 15 明確要求：多產品設施的清潔驗證必須以毒理學評估（即 ADE/HBEL 文件）作為依據。

查驗要點：查核員可能要求查閱：

  • ADE 文件（含毒理學家簽署）
  • ADE 到殘留限量的計算追溯
  • 毒理學家的資格證明
  • 文件的版本管理和定期審查記錄
∑

本節重點整理 Section Summary

Chapters 4–5 key concepts consolidated | p37–52

Chapter 4–5 Key Concepts at a Glance
核心要點總結

從危害到限值：完整推導鏈

危害識別（哪些化合物有哪些毒理端點）

↓ 劑量反應評估（找出 NOAEL / LOAEL）

↓ 選定臨界效應（最低劑量出現的最敏感不良效應）

↓ 應用調整因子（AFA × AFH × AFS × AFL × AFD × MF × PK）

↓ 計算 ADE/PDE（PoD × BW / 複合調整因子）

↓ 推導清潔驗證殘留限量（依設備面積、批量、劑量計算）

↓ 書面文件（合格毒理學家簽署，定期更新）

HBEL 與 OEL 的平行關係

相同基礎：兩者都源自毒理數據（NOAEL、劑量反應）。

不同目的：HBEL 保護病患（每日攝入量），OEL 保護工作人員（空氣濃度）。

換算關係：OEL ≈ ADE / 10 m³（工作者 8 小時換氣量），但須考慮路徑差異與族群差異。

監管機構的期待（EU GMP Annex 15）

  • 所有多產品設施的清潔驗證限量必須以 HBEL/ADE 為依據。
  • ADE 文件由合格毒理學家建立並簽署。
  • 文件必須可供審核，並定期複查。
  • 廠房設計（containment strategy）應與 ADE/OEL 等級一致。
6

Chapter 6: Risk Analysis

風險分析 | p53-p78

ISPE Baseline® Guide Volume 7 (2nd Ed.): Risk-Based Manufacture | p53–p68

ISPE Vol.7 — Chapter 6: Risk Analysis & Cross-Contamination Routes (Part A)
