  • 掌握 PPE / RPE 在有害化合物製造中的角色與限制
9.6

HVAC and Environmental Control — 概論

Three levels of proximity: Room → Local → Equipment Enclosure | p98-p99

9.6 HVAC and Environmental Control

The key requirement of life science HVAC is to assure a suitable environment for the product and process with regard to temperature, humidity, and most importantly, airborne particulate, molecular, and viable cleanliness. This requirement is in addition to the usual industrial HVAC requirements of making workers comfortable and protecting them from hazardous airborne fumes, vapors, aerosols, and dust.

Often, the need to control hazardous compounds complicates environmental control as cleanliness and containment may require conflicting pressurization schemes.

As product potency increases, the need for control of airborne product/API also increases. The effectiveness of HVAC related contamination controls improve as proximity to the product increases. Three levels of increasing proximity are considered:

  • Room Level HVAC — dilutes airborne contaminants by entrainment in air streams, extracted from the room. Susceptible to behavior, technique, and operational failures.
  • Local Ventilation — "near field" effect by placing exhaust and/or supply close to emission sources. Higher particulate concentration at source enables more efficient filtration or exhaust disposal.
  • Equipment Level Ventilation — e.g., isolator, RABS, vented balance enclosure, or closed equipment. Combines physical barriers with HVAC to control particulate buildup within the enclosure. Closing a process reduces the size of the critical environment, making the surrounding room a support area.

This triumvirate of control technologies can provide significant safety and product protection benefits, individually and in concert. They can safely handle highly hazardous materials with very low OELs.

At HVAC equipment level, removal of undesirable airborne contaminants is achieved through exhaust (disposal) or depth filtration. Filters also serve as an enhanced boundary protecting against unintended backflow or migration of API dust through duct systems upon loss of HVAC. Terminal filters at air inlets and outlets of processing rooms are therefore common.

解說：三層 HVAC 控制概念

三層控制距離原則

HVAC 控制效能與距離成反比。越靠近污染源，控制越有效：

  • Room Level（房間層）：靠大量換氣稀釋，效果依賴人員行為與操作技術，是最脆弱的一層。
  • Local Ventilation（局部層）：LEV（局部排氣通風）在污染源附近直接捕集，比房間換氣更高效，捕集的是高濃度空氣。
  • Equipment Level（設備層）：隔離器、RABS 等將製程完全包覆，把「潔淨區」縮小到最小範圍，周圍環境降為支援區。

比喻：廚房油煙機

把炒鍋油煙想成 API 粉塵。
房間換氣 = 開窗讓風吹散 → 效果差
LEV = 油煙機抽直接在鍋上方 → 效果好
密閉設備 = 在密閉蒸汽爐裡烹調 → 幾乎零逸散

生命科學 HVAC 設計就是讓每一層互補，形成縱深防禦。

重點提示：潔淨度 vs 密閉度的矛盾

高效能藥品廠常見矛盾：
- 產品保護需要正壓（防外部污染進入）
- 人員和環境保護需要負壓（防 API 逸出）
設計時需根據產品毒性（OEL/HBEL）決定哪個優先，並採用氣鎖隔離兩種需求。

交叉參考

詳細 HVAC 設計規範請參考：
- ISPE Good Practice Guide: HVAC（專門處理 HVAC 系統設計）
- ISPE Baseline® Guide Vol. 3（Sterile Manufacturing Facilities）

9.6.1

Once-Through versus Recirculation

When is 100% exhaust required for hazardous compounds? | p99-p100

9.6.1 Once-Through versus Recirculation

Recirculated HVAC systems offer energy savings and operational cost benefits over once-through systems. The air recirculated from manufacturing areas is often cleaner and much closer to the desired temperature and humidity conditions than fresh air.

However, recirculation of air from powder handling spaces, especially in multiproduct concurrent manufacturing facilities, can convey airborne product particles to other areas and may maintain aerosols in suspension, depending on particle size and room air patterns.

Regulations suggest that if air is to be recirculated, when potentially contaminated with airborne product particles, it should be adequately treated. The definition of adequate treatment is amenable to a risk-based approach, as described in Section 9.6.2.

Three Levels of HVAC Control (recap)

解說：單通 vs 循環系統的決策邏輯

核心概念

單通系統（Once-Through / 100% Exhaust）：供氣全部來自新鮮外氣，排氣全部排至室外（經處理）。無再循環，交叉污染風險最低，但能耗極高。

循環系統（Recirculation）：部分或全部回風再使用，節能，但需要過濾處理以移除 API 粒子。

法規核心要求

EU GMP Annex 15 及多國 GMP 規定：多品種共用設施中，若空氣循環使用，必須「充分處理」（adequately treated）。「充分」的定義由風險評估決定（見 9.6.2）。

對於高毒性化合物（低 OEL / HBEL），「充分處理」通常意味著：
→ 雙重 HEPA 過濾，或
→ 100% 排氣（完全不循環）

比喻：辦公室空調 vs 化學實驗室抽風

一般辦公室空調把排氣循環再用是合理的（無毒性氣體）。但化學實驗室通風櫃的排氣一定要 100% 排到室外，不能循環回辦公室。API 粉塵處理邏輯相同：毒性越高，越傾向 100% 排氣。

9.6.2

Quantitating the Risk of Airborne Cross-Contamination

Calculation method, filter efficiency tables, particle mass relationships | p99-p104 (Advanced Topic)

9.6.2 Quantitating the Risk of Airborne Cross-Contamination

(Advanced Topic)

Control of cross-contamination is primarily a matter of understanding the mass of "product A" which might be carried into "product B". For contaminants spread through the air, the process involves:

  • Understanding the potential maximum mass of airborne product that may be produced
  • Determining how much of this mass could be delivered to other spaces
  • Evaluating upset cases (e.g., spills) and potential failures of abatement equipment (failure sensitivity evaluation)

The method is similar to the approach used by Industrial Hygienists for worker safety: the actual quantity of product aerosolized during a working day is measured, and correction factors for PPE are applied.

A quantitative evaluation provides:

  • More robust understanding of contamination risks and appropriate controls
  • Verification measures through facility life
  • Data for investigations, event response planning, and critical management tasks
  • Assurance that resources are commensurate with risk — neither inadequate nor wasteful

Contamination Sources and Potency

The potency of the product and the potential maximum concentration of airborne product drive the need for more rigorous abatement. The highest particle concentration air streams — such as from dust collectors, especially when handling potent products — require the most stringent abatement and may not be candidates for recirculation.

Results from Environmental Health and Safety studies are generally expressed in µg/m³, which couples well with the quantitative method outlined here. To determine appropriate filtration, fractional removal efficiencies across twelve particle size ranges from standards such as ANSI/ASHRAE 52.2, EN 1822, EN 779, or ISO 29463-1 are used.

Filter Efficiency Examples

Table 9.2/9.3/9.4 (source tables) demonstrate mass reduction through filtration stages:

A properly installed and maintained MERV 15 (~95% ASHRAE) filter can provide a 3 log reduction in contaminants. A MERV 11 (~50% ASHRAE) gives a 1.5 log (20:1) reduction.

Large Particles — Greater Cross-Contamination Risk

While small particles (<10 µm) are of interest in worker safety (greater respirability), large particles (>10 µm) pose greater cross-contamination risk for two reasons:

  1. In any heterogeneous particle dispersion, the greatest mass resides in large particles. A 10 µ particle is ~10,000 times heavier than a 0.5 µ particle and 1,000,000 times heavier than a 0.1 µ particle. At example specific gravity, it takes 15,000,000 of 0.5 µ particles to deliver 1 µg; only 2,000 of 10 µ particles are needed.
  2. Lower buoyancy of large particles (higher settling rate) makes them more likely to contaminate product by falling out of an airstream as velocity decreases in a production room.

This is good news for filtration: even moderate efficiency filters are quite effective at removing large particles.

Failure Analysis Considerations

Analysis must always consider failure causes including:

  1. Filter and/or frame leakage
  2. Spills and other upsets which cause an excess of airborne API

解說：空氣傳播交叉污染量化方法

核心計算公式：空氣傳播污染質量評估

量化方法的核心邏輯分三步：

步驟 1：確定污染源的空氣中 API 濃度
  來源：EHS 監測數據，單位 µg/m³
  → 代入粒徑分布（各粒徑質量佔比）

步驟 2：計算過濾效率的保護因子
  各粒徑殘留質量 = 總質量 × (1 - 過濾效率%)
  → 參考 ANSI/ASHRAE 52.2 或 EN 1822 分效率數據
  → 對 12 個粒徑區間逐一計算
  → 加總得到過濾後空氣總殘留質量

步驟 3：驗證殘留濃度 ≤ 可接受限度
  接受限度 = HBEL / ADE（基於健康的暴露限值）
  → 若超標：升級過濾或改為 100% 排氣

關鍵公式（粒子質量）：

粒子體積 = (4/3) × π × r³
粒子質量 = 粒子體積 × 比重 (density)
  （常用比重：0.6–1.0 g/cm³）

粒徑效應：
  10 µm 粒子質量 ≈ 5.2×10⁻⁴ µg
  0.5 µm 粒子質量 ≈ 6.5×10⁻⁸ µg
  質量比 = 10µm / 0.5µm ≈ 8,000倍

關鍵變數說明

  • Total Mass（各粒徑總質量）：來自 EHS 監測，單位 µg/m³
  • Fractional Filter Efficiency（分效率）：各粒徑的過濾效率，來自 MERV 或 EN 標準測試
  • Fractional Mass After Filtration：= Total Mass × (1 - Efficiency)
  • MERV（Minimum Efficiency Reporting Value）：美國 ASHRAE 過濾器分級標準
  • EN 1822：歐洲 HEPA/ULPA 過濾器標準（對應 H13/H14）

重要洞察：大粒子是交叉污染主要威脅

直覺上可能以為小粒子（可飄浮更遠）風險更高，但實際上：

  • 大粒子（>10 µm）含有的質量遠遠大於小粒子（體積與半徑三次方成正比）
  • 大粒子沉降速度快，更容易落入開放容器或製程中
  • 中等效率過濾器（MERV 11-13）對大粒子已有很好的捕集效果

這意味著：交叉污染風險控制靠中等效率過濾即可有效管理，無需全部裝 HEPA（除非 API 毒性極高）。

比喻：沙塵 vs 花粉

沙塵粒子大但重，飄不遠就落地，但一旦落在食物上就帶來大量質量（污染）。花粉雖細小但質量輕，飄很遠但每顆攜帶的污染量極少。API 粉塵的邏輯與此相同：大粒子才是交叉污染的主要質量來源。

與工業衛生學方法的連結

本方法源自工業衛生師（Industrial Hygienist）用於工人安全的評估方法，差別在於：

  • 工業衛生：保護工人，關注吸入小粒子（<10 µm）
  • 交叉污染控制：保護產品，關注大粒子（>10 µm）質量轉移
  • 兩者均用 µg/m³ 表達，數據可共用

思考練習

假設 EHS 監測數據顯示某粉塵處理間空氣中 API 濃度為 50 µg/m³，產品 HBEL = 0.5 µg/day，員工每日吸入量假設 10 m³：

  • 每日吸入 API 質量 = 50 × 10 = 500 µg/day → 超過 HBEL 1000 倍
  • 需要過濾效率達到 99.9%（3 log）以上才能降至可接受水準
  • → 建議：MERV 15 或 HEPA，或 100% 排氣
9.6.3

Directional Airflow and Pressure Regimens

Positive vs negative pressure, pressure cascades, airlock configurations | p103-p105

9.6.3 Directional Airflow and Pressure Regimens

In order to control the migration of product aerosols from one room or area to another, it is important to manage the airflow between spaces. Two approaches are possible:

Approach 1 — High Mass Airflow Entrainment: Entrain the aerosol in a large mass of air, typically moving at 0.2 m/s (40 fpm) or greater. Typically used in open downflow booths and similar devices, but not preferred for rooms due to large and rapid changes in airflow when doors are opened or closed (typically 400 m³/h (800 cfm)).

Approach 2 — Controlled Direction with Adequate Velocity (preferred): Control the direction of airflow and assure adequate velocity to transport particles, typically in the range of 0.5 to 1.0 m/s (100 to 200 fpm). Two sub-approaches:

  • Maintain a fixed offset between air entering and leaving via the HVAC system (fixed balance or airflow tracking)
  • Measure and control room pressurization, typically in steps of 10 to 15 Pa (0.4 to 0.6 in. W.G.), but no lower than 5 Pa (0.02 in. W.G.). High-pressure difference across doors results in high velocities at leak points, on the order of 3 to 3.5 m/s (600 to 700 fpm).

Pressure Cascade Design Principles

The pressure cascade and direction of airflow should be designed to be protective of product, personnel, and environment:

  • To prevent environmental contaminants from entering: production area positive with respect to surrounding environment
  • However, a positive manufacturing space can spread product aerosols to other products and personnel; therefore, open product handling areas should be negative with respect to other GxP areas (e.g., the GxP corridor)

Airlock Configurations

Single door configurations between production room and corridor are challenged when the door is open. For greater protection, airlocks with interlocked doors are used. Three configurations (Figure 9.7🔍):

  • Simple Pressure Cascade: Corridor (positive) → Production (negative). Effective for API containment.
  • Sink-type Airlock: Process room positive to airlock AND corridor positive to airlock. Airlock is the lowest pressure (sink).
  • Bubble-type Airlock: Airlock is positive with respect to both corridor and process room. Testing has shown greater emission potential with this configuration — generally not preferred for hazardous compounds.

解說：定向氣流與壓力梯度設計

壓力梯度基本原則

氣流從高壓流向低壓。壓力梯度設計的目標：讓「乾淨空氣」永遠往「可能被污染的區域」流，污染源區域維持負壓以防逸散。

  • 正壓（Positive Pressure）：防外部污染進入（保護產品）
  • 負壓（Negative Pressure）：防 API 逸出（保護人員和其他產品）

對於高毒性 API 製造，通常以負壓為主，防止有害物質向外擴散。

壓力差設計數值

建議壓差（相鄰房間）：10–15 Pa
最低可接受壓差：5 Pa（低於此值難以維持方向性氣流）

門縫氣流速度（在壓差作用下）：
  3.0–3.5 m/s (600–700 fpm)
  → 足以攜帶並阻止粒子逆向移動

空氣流速（大面積掃流）：
  ≥ 0.2 m/s (40 fpm)：用於降流罩
  0.5–1.0 m/s (100–200 fpm)：用於定向控制

矛盾困境：正壓 vs 負壓

製造廠常遇到的設計矛盾：

  • 產品保護 → 製造間正壓（防外部微生物污染）
  • 人員 / 環境保護 → 製造間負壓（防 API 粉塵外洩）

解決方案：在製造間與走廊之間插入氣鎖（Airlock），形成壓力緩衝區，走廊保持正壓，製造間保持負壓，兩者不直接相通。

比喻：病房隔離室

傳染病隔離室採用負壓（防止病毒外洩）；無塵室採用正壓（防止外部粒子進入）。API 製造間兼具兩種需求，氣鎖就是讓兩種需求共存的「緩衝帶」。

交叉參考

氣鎖設計詳見：ISPE Good Practice Guide: HVAC 及 ISPE Baseline® Vol. 3 (Sterile Manufacturing Facilities)。具體壓差監控與驗證方法參考 ISPE C&Q 指引。

9.7

Containment Related Technologies

Selection of containment systems matched to compound hazard level | p105-p106

9.7 Containment Related Technologies

Containment related technologies are typically used to make a process step, or a process a closed system, keeping the product and the room environment separate. Employing containment related technologies can reduce the risk of cross-contamination by airborne or mechanical transfer routes.

9.7.1 Selection of Appropriate Containment Systems

The equipment selection process should result in individual equipment items or systems identified which give high confidence that the design target/performance expectation will be met. Success depends on an early understanding of the full range of activities, including normal operation, sampling, and cleaning, shared with the full team including supplier(s) and integrators.

Planned and breakdown maintenance activities should be discussed at an early stage. Requirements for activities such as sampling should be questioned, as they may present significant difficulties in effective containment design and may present an exposure risk that outweighs other benefits.

Information Required for Successful Equipment Selection

  • Detail of all activities to be undertaken including normal operation, sampling, and cleaning
  • Appreciation of the rate of movement of particles or the energy with which they may be released
  • Variety of containers in and out of the equipment
  • Way waste and contaminated equipment will be removed
  • Need for aids for heavy, awkward, or restricted space lifting
  • Operators' understanding of risks and how behavior affects containment performance — behavior has the greatest impact on local extract and enclosures and least impact on closed systems and isolators
  • Ergonomics of activities, especially repetitive actions, access requirements, working position, load characteristics, and operator stature range
  • Knowledge of containment or emission performance of equipment in similar applications
  • How containment performance may change with time due to ineffective cleaning and/or wear
  • Understanding of the problem by the design team
  • Potential for powder to ignite or support a dust cloud explosion — contained systems have smaller volumes and low air change rates creating risk of explosive concentrations; nitrogen inerting may be required
  • To dissipate electrostatic buildup, all metal parts should be grounded (earthed), including elements docked and insulated by plastic wear elements

解說：密閉系統選擇層級

密閉系統選擇層級（依 OEL/HBEL 分級）

密閉技術的選擇遵循「能量控制層級」原則：先考慮工程控制（密閉）而非依賴行政控制（SOP）或 PPE。以下為從低到高的密閉層級：

開放作業（Open Processing）
OEL > 100 µg/m³ | 適合低毒性化合物
↓ 毒性增加
局部排氣通風（LEV / Downflow Booth）
OEL 10–100 µg/m³ | 近場捕集，半開放
↓
密閉容器 / 密封設備（Closed Vessels / Systems）
OEL 1–10 µg/m³ | 降低逸散，人工干預點受控
↓
手套箱 / 隔離器（Glovebox / Isolator）
OEL < 1 µg/m³ | 完全物理隔離，最高等級

人員行為對不同密閉技術的影響

關鍵洞察：密閉程度越低，操作人員行為對實際密閉效果的影響越大。

  • 開放操作 / LEV：操作技術、站位、移動速度對密閉效能影響最大
  • 半密閉（手套箱外接）：中等依賴人員行為
  • 隔離器 / 完全密閉：人員行為影響最小，設備本身提供保障

→ 高毒性化合物不應依賴人員行為作為主要控制手段

比喻：口罩 vs 防護艙

開放作業 + PPE 就像戴口罩防病毒，效果取決於佩戴方法。隔離器就像把病毒放在完全密封的防護艙裡處理，效果幾乎不依賴人員技術。API 越毒，越需要靠近「防護艙」端的解決方案。

爆炸風險：常被忽略的設計考量

密閉系統的副作用：體積小、換氣率低，可能形成爆炸性粉塵濃度（Dust Explosion Limit）。設計時必須：

  • 評估 API 粉塵的爆炸風險（MEC：Minimum Explosive Concentration）
  • 若有風險：通入氮氣（Nitrogen Inerting）降低氧氣濃度
  • 所有金屬部件需接地，防止靜電火花引燃

採樣設計挑戰

密閉系統設計中最困難的環節之一是「採樣」（Sampling）。文件強調應主動質疑採樣是否必要——有時採樣的暴露風險遠大於獲得的品質資訊價值，應在工廠設計初期即納入討論，而非事後補救。

9.8

Personal Protective Equipment and Gowning

PPE vs RPE distinction, roles, and cross-contamination risk from mechanical transfer | p106-p108

9.8 Personal Protective Equipment and Gowning

Personal Protective Equipment (PPE) refers to gowns, gloves, booties, hair covers, hoods, respiratory protection, face masks, etc.

Respiratory Protective Equipment (RPE) covers devices designed only to protect the mouth and nose.

The distinction is important because PPE, without RPE, is recommended for protecting the product from contamination and cross-contamination as well as for dermal protection for the operators at all times.

Whenever RPE is used, it is important to consider its use, storage, maintenance, and decontamination, and whether or not it could lead to a risk of cross-contamination from mechanical transfer.

PPE is Normally Worn to:

  • Help limit mechanical transfer of materials
  • Provide appropriate outer clothing to protect the product, e.g., made of non-shedding material
  • Provide a psychological and physical indication of transfer from the outside environment into a GxP facility where specific procedures, rules of conduct, and action apply
  • Provide dermal and chemical protection to the operator so that any drug exposure related effects are minimized

Risk Acceptance Requirement (Section 10 cross-reference)

Where risk reduction strategies (including PPE, containment, HVAC) are implemented, the manufacturer must demonstrate to all stakeholders that strategies are effective in maintaining cross-contamination and worker exposure at or below acceptable limits. This requires demonstration that:

  • Procedures and detection devices are in place to minimize mix-up potential even in accident or error scenarios
  • Any residues on product contact and non-product contact surfaces fall within health-based limits, in support of cleaning processes
  • Flow of personnel, product, material, and HVAC are designed to minimize potential for mechanical transfer
  • Any product that may escape the process is maintained below levels that could impact cross-contamination and worker safety

解說：PPE / RPE 的角色與限制

RPE 的隱藏風險：機械轉移

RPE 本身可能成為交叉污染載體！

若 RPE 在高 API 濃度環境中使用後，未妥善儲存/去污就帶到其他區域，RPE 表面殘留的 API 會造成機械轉移。因此：

  • RPE 的使用、儲存、維護、去污程序必須文件化
  • 高毒性環境的 RPE 應視為危險廢棄物，不可帶出
  • 建議在更衣間/氣鎖區域脫除 RPE，而非帶至走廊

PPE 的四個功能（按重要性）

  1. 限制機械轉移：防止人員將 API 粉塵帶到其他區域（保護其他產品）
  2. 保護產品：不脫屑材質的防護衣防止人員粒子污染產品（雙向保護）
  3. 心理 / 行為標誌：穿上特定防護衣代表進入 GxP 環境，強化人員的合規意識
  4. 皮膚化學防護：防止 API 的皮膚吸收（dermal exposure），對潛在毒性化合物尤為重要

比喻：廚師帽的雙重意義

餐廳廚師的帽子（防脫髮）：
- 保護食物不被頭髮污染（保護產品）
- 防止廚師吸入食物蒸汽（保護人員）
API 製造的 PPE 同樣具有雙向保護功能，但在有毒藥品環境中，人員保護的需求更為迫切，RPE 的選擇必須基於定量風險評估。

PPE 是最後一道防線，不是第一道

依照 ISPE Vol.7 的風險降低層級邏輯（第 9 章整體框架）：

  • 優先：工程控制（密閉設備、隔離器、LEV）
  • 其次：行政控制（SOP、人員限制、更衣程序）
  • 最後：PPE / RPE（個人防護）

過度依賴 PPE 而不解決工程層面的問題，是 GMP 稽查常見缺失。

與其他章節的整合：風險接受

第 9 章（風險降低）的所有措施——HVAC 設計、密閉系統、PPE——最終都要回到第 10 章（Risk Acceptance）：製造商需向所有利害相關人證明這些措施有效地將：

  • 交叉污染維持在健康基礎限值以下（HBEL/ADE）
  • 工人暴露維持在 OEL 以下

這需要監控數據、驗證記錄，以及偏差調查機制的整體配合。

總結

Chapter 9 (Part B) 綜合總結

HVAC、密閉技術、PPE 三者的整合應用邏輯

Key Takeaways — English Summary

  • Once-Through vs Recirculation: Recirculation is permitted with adequate treatment; for potent APIs (low OEL), double HEPA or 100% exhaust is required. Dust collectors handling potent products are not candidates for recirculation.
  • Quantitative CC Risk: Large particles (>10 µm) carry the greatest mass and pose the greatest cross-contamination risk. MERV 11 provides ~1.5 log reduction; MERV 15 provides ~3 log. Filtration efficiency data by particle size range is available from ASHRAE 52.2 and EN 1822.
  • Pressure Regimens: Typical steps of 10–15 Pa; minimum 5 Pa. Sink-type airlocks are preferred for potent API areas. Bubble-type airlocks show higher emission potential and are generally not recommended for hazardous compounds.
  • Containment Hierarchy: Open → LEV/Downflow Booth → Closed Vessels → Gloveboxes → Isolators. Higher containment levels reduce dependence on operator behavior.
  • PPE is the last line of defense: Engineering controls (closed systems, HVAC) take priority. RPE must be managed to prevent becoming a cross-contamination vector via mechanical transfer.

實務應用矩陣

章節間連結

本節（第 9 章後半）的技術選擇，均需對應回：

  • 第 5 章：OEL / HBEL / ADE 的設定（選擇依據）
  • 第 8 章：設施與設備設計（含 GMP 區域規劃）
  • 第 10 章：風險接受的文件化與驗證要求
  • 第 11 章：FMEA 等工具對失效情境的量化分析
10-13

Chapter 10-13: Risk Tools, Review & Communication

風險工具、審查與溝通 | p109-p124

ISPE Baseline® Guide Volume 7 (2nd Ed.): Risk-Based Manufacture | p109–p124

本節涵蓋章節

Ch.10 風險接受 Ch.11 風險管理工具總覽 11.1 風險排序 / 風險矩陣 11.2 魚骨圖 11.3 FMEA 11.4 統計分析 Ch.12 風險審查 Ch.13 風險溝通 13.1 摘要文件範本

學習目標

  • 理解殘餘風險接受的條件，以及與 HBEL（ADE/OEL）的連結關係
  • 掌握風險矩陣（Risk Matrix）的構成邏輯與色碼熱圖的解讀方式
  • 應用魚骨圖（Ishikawa / 6M 架構）識別交叉污染的根本原因

10

Risk Acceptance — 風險接受

p109–p110 | ICH Q9 residual risk decision framework, link to HBEL

Original Text (English)

10 Risk Acceptance

ICH Q9 states that risk acceptance is a decision to accept a defined level of risk. This can be a formal documented decision process with residual risks specified or a more informal process where the residual risk is not specified. The documentation and the acceptable residual risk should be commensurate with the risk.

Acceptance of residual risk based on the health-based limits described in this Guide should provide adequate protection of both patient and the worker.

Where risk reduction strategies are implemented in order to get to a risk acceptance decision, the manufacturer should be able to demonstrate to all stakeholders that the risk reduction strategies are effective in maintaining cross-contamination and worker exposure at or below acceptable limits.

This requires demonstration that:

  • Procedures and detection devices are in place to minimize the potential for mix-up even in the case of accident or error
  • Any residues on product contact and nonproduct contact surfaces fall within the health-based limits in support of cleaning processes
  • Flow of personnel, product, material, and HVAC are designed to minimize the potential for mechanical transfer
  • Any product that may escape the process is maintained below levels that could impact the potential for cross-contamination and worker safety
解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

核心概念：什麼是風險接受？

風險接受（Risk Acceptance）不是「忽視風險」，而是一個有意識的、基於充分證據的決策——確認殘餘風險在可接受範圍之內。

ICH Q9 允許正式或非正式兩種型態，但文件程度必須與風險大小相稱（commensurate with the risk）。

HBEL 連結：ADE 與 OEL 是接受門檻的基礎

本指南強調，殘餘風險接受的依據應為健康基礎暴露限值（HBEL），具體包括：

  • ADE（Acceptable Daily Exposure）——患者保護（產品交叉污染角度）
  • OEL（Occupational Exposure Limit）——員工保護（職業暴露角度）

只有當實際殘留量 ≤ 基於 ADE/OEL 推導的清潔限值時，才可正式接受風險。

比喻：風險接受像「結案核准」

就像工廠送審一份 CAPA — 必須提供證據證明改善措施有效，主管才能「核准結案」。風險接受也是：你必須拿出數據，證明四種交叉污染途徑（混料、殘留、機械轉移、空氣傳播）都已控制在 ADE/OEL 以下，才能正式簽署接受。

四項必要舉證條件

  • 防止混料（mix-up）的程序與偵測裝置已到位
  • 產品接觸表面與非接觸表面的殘留量符合健康基礎清潔限值
  • 人員、物料、HVAC 動線已設計為最小化機械轉移
  • 逸散至製程外的產品量低於影響安全的閾值

稽核重點

稽核員常問：「你的殘餘風險接受決定有沒有文件？是誰批准的？依據哪個 ADE 值？」——確保這條邏輯鏈清晰，從毒理報告 → ADE → 清潔限值 → 驗證結果 → 風險接受文件。

11

Risk Management Tools — 風險管理工具總覽

p111–p112 | ICH Q9 tool selection, risk ranking, organizational standards

Original Text (English)

11 Risk Management Tools

Risk can be assessed and managed using risk management tools. The level of effort or the tools used should be based on the level of potential risk and knowledge of the process. It is important that each manufacturer set standards for risk assessment tools including, but not limited to, the types of tools to be used, when to use certain tools, defining the categories, setting acceptable risk levels, action levels, etc.

It is essential that the numbers or designation are carefully chosen and defined and are not modified because the outcome is unwelcome.

ICH Q9 refers to a number of risk assessment tools that may be used. Organizations should determine which tools they wish to use or they can create custom tools:

  • Basic risk management facilitation methods (flowcharts, check sheets, etc.)
  • Failure Mode and Effects Analysis (FMEA)
  • Failure Mode, Effects, and Criticality Analysis (FMECA)
  • Fault Tree Analysis (FTA)
  • Hazard Analysis and Critical Control Points (HACCP)
  • Hazard Operability Analysis (HAZOP)
  • Preliminary Hazard Analysis (PHA)
  • Risk ranking and filtering
  • Supporting statistical tools

The tools shown in this Chapter are examples that should ideally be developed and used by a team of stakeholders working together.

解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

工具選擇原則：複雜度應與風險等級相稱

本指南不強制規定使用哪種工具，但強調：

  • 工具投入程度應與潛在風險水準成比例
  • 每家製造商應建立自己的標準化工具體系（包含使用時機、評分類別、可接受標準）
  • 一旦標準確立，不能因為結果不如預期而修改評分定義

關鍵原則：評分定義不可因結果不好而事後修改

這是業界常見的合規陷阱——有人在 FMEA 結果出現高 RPN 後，重新調整評分定義讓數字「好看」。ICH Q9 和本指南明確反對此做法。評分標準必須在評估前定義，且貫穿整個項目一致適用。

ICH Q9 工具清單（本節涵蓋工具加粗）

  • 流程圖、查核表（基礎方法）
  • FMEA — 失效模式與影響分析
  • FMECA — 含嚴重度分析的 FMEA
  • FTA — 故障樹分析
  • HACCP — 危害分析關鍵控制點
  • HAZOP — 危害與可操作性分析
  • PHA — 初步危害分析
  • 風險排序與篩選（Risk Matrix）
  • 統計分析工具

比喻：工具箱思維

就像水電工不會只用一種扳手——風險管理也需要視問題性質選用適當工具。FMEA 適合流程步驟層級的細節分析；Risk Matrix 適合快速排序整廠製程；統計分析適合有量化監測數據的場景。

11.1

Risk Ranking / Risk Matrix — 風險排序與風險矩陣

p112 | Probability vs Severity grid, color-coded heat map, unit operation classification

Original Text (English)

11.1 Risk Ranking or Risk Matrix

Qualitative risk assessments may be performed at manufacturing sites for the purpose of determining which unit operations pose the greatest risk or the greatest opportunity. A risk ranking or risk matrix provides a very simple high level objective process to consistently evaluate all the unit operations at a manufacturing site and rank the operations by risk.

To apply the risk ranking, all the unit operations at a site are identified. To complete the ranking, the following parameters should be considered:

  • Health Effects: ADE value, residue levels for cleaning, inactivation, etc.
  • Product Considerations: percent active in batch, batch size, product form (impact on API becoming airborne), maximum daily dosage
  • Operational Considerations: number of employees involved, frequency of the process, energy input, open or closed processing, surface area of product contact parts, batches per year, relative positions of source and at-risk materials, duration of process

For each parameter a numerical value, or high, medium, and low indicator is assigned, and for each unit operation, the scores are totaled. After all unit operations have been assessed, the risk ranking scores can be compared and activities prioritized.

Unit Operation Risk Ranking — Airborne Concentration Examples

  • High (H): sampling, weighing and dispensing, sample testing (analytical), charging, milling, granulation, extruding (cleaning), compounding
  • Medium (M): mixing, blending, extruding, compression, capsule filling
  • Low (L): coating, charging, drilling, printing, packaging
  • Negligible (N): membrane coating, discharging cores, drying, pouching, gel dispensing, curing, assembling, inspection
解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

風險矩陣的核心邏輯

風險矩陣以發生機率（Probability/Likelihood）對嚴重度（Severity）繪製二維網格，每個交叉格以色碼標示風險等級：

色碼對應行動要求

  • 低 — 可接受，監控即可
  • 中 — 需評估是否採取改善措施
  • 高 — 需要風險控制措施
  • 極高 — 必須立即採取行動或暫停

無菌填充廠應用示例

以無菌填充廠交叉污染風險排序為例：

  • 高風險：稱量分裝、API 充填（高空浮濃度）
  • 中風險：混合/調配操作
  • 低風險：包裝、貼標（密閉系統）
  • 可忽略：乾燥、外觀檢查

三個評分維度（健康影響、產品因素、操作因素）加總後決定整體排序，優先處理高分製程步驟。

11.2

Cause and Effect Diagram (Fishbone) — 魚骨圖（石川圖）

p113 | Ishikawa diagram for cross-contamination root cause analysis, 6M framework

Original Text (English)

11.2 Cause and Effect Diagram (Fishbone Diagram)

Use the Ishikawa Fishbone diagram to brainstorm how the four modes of cross-contamination can occur. In addition, a second diagram can be used to identify how each of the four modes of cross-contamination can be or are controlled.

This can be a helpful precursor to more detailed analysis or data gathering exercises.

"The Fishbone diagram is a structured brainstorming tool that maps potential causes to an observed effect, enabling a team to systematically explore root causes before committing to remediation actions."

The four modes of cross-contamination addressed by the fishbone analysis are:

  • Mix-up — incorrect product or label identification
  • Retention — residues remaining from prior campaigns
  • Mechanical transfer — physical movement via personnel, equipment, materials
  • Airborne transfer — product aerosols migrating via air currents

Two diagrams are recommended:

  1. First diagram: How can each mode occur? (cause identification)
  2. Second diagram: How is each mode currently controlled? (control mapping)
解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

魚骨圖的 6M 架構

標準魚骨圖使用「6M」分類框架，從六個維度系統性地識別根本原因：

Man（人員） 訓練不足、操作失誤、人員流動、更衣程序不當
Machine（設備） 清潔不徹底、磨損產生顆粒、設計難以清潔的死角
Method（方法） SOP 不完整、清潔驗證失效、製程順序安排不當
Material（物料） 容器標籤錯誤、共用物料架、包材殘留
Measurement（量測） 殘留量監測不足、取樣點不代表性、分析方法靈敏度不夠
Mother Nature（環境） HVAC 壓差不足、空氣循環帶入交叉污染、溫濕度影響揚塵
6M 根本原因 ► 交叉污染發生

雙圖使用策略

第一張圖（找問題）：針對每種交叉污染模式，用 6M 列舉所有可能的成因。這是 brainstorming 階段，不預設答案。

第二張圖（找控制）：針對相同模式，列出現有控制措施（工程控制、行政控制、程序控制）。兩張圖對比，缺口（gap）就是需要改善的地方。

比喻：魚骨圖是「反向工程」

你已知道問題（魚頭 = 效果），現在沿著魚骨往回追溯原因。就像交通事故調查員從「追撞」倒推「路面濕滑 + 車距不足 + 疲勞駕駛」——把每條骨頭想成一個可能的原因分支。

無菌填充廠實際應用

針對「空氣傳播（Airborne）」模式的魚骨分析示例：

  • 人員：更衣不完整導致外部污染物帶入
  • 設備：RABS/隔離器的 HEPA 完整性破損
  • 方法：開瓶操作在非 A 級環境進行
  • 環境：B 級室對 C 級室壓差反向（失控狀態）
11.3

Failure Mode and Effects Analysis (FMEA) — 失效模式與影響分析

p114–p117 | RPN = S × O × D, scoring tables, FMEA form structure

Original Text (English)

11.3 Failure Mode and Effects Analysis

Many pharmaceutical companies use FMEA techniques for risk ranking and have standard protocols for its use. It is used in Six Sigma evaluations and can be used for a wide range of risk assessments.

FMEA was originally developed by the US Military in the 1940s and further developed by the automotive and aerospace industries. Where companies do not have a formally documented system, it is recommended that they use a recognized system such as in IEC 60812.

FMEA Form Column Headings (Table 11.1)

11.3.1 Scoring Severity, Occurrence, and Detection (Table 11.2)

The possible scores in this example range from 1 (1×1×1) to 1,000 (10×10×10). Each organization should determine the scoring systems to be used in FMEAs.

Scoring or RPNs should be viewed as a general indicator/aid for risk ranking and not treated as an absolute indicator of risk. Caution should be used when prioritizing risks on just the RPN number.

One method to address possible inequalities of RPNs is to require review of any item (severity, occurrence, or detection) that has the highest value regardless of the resultant RPN.

Detectability is a vital issue: if reliable means exist to detect a failure, increased occurrence may be tolerable; if the event cannot be detected, then the occurrence and severity have to be low.

解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

FMEA 起源與藥廠應用

FMEA 最初由美國軍方在 1940 年代開發，後來被汽車（AIAG）和航太工業廣泛標準化。藥廠版本加入了製藥特有的因素：ADE 值、職業暴露限值、交叉污染四種模式。

ICH Q9 將 FMEA 列為推薦工具；參考標準為 IEC 60812，企業可在此基礎上客製化。

RPN 公式

RPN = Severity (S) × Occurrence (O) × Detection (D)

範圍：1（最低風險）→ 1,000（最高風險）

S = 10：患者/員工受傷，ADE < 1 µg/day
O = 10：每批次發生一次以上
D = 10：現有方法完全無法偵測

說明：
Detection 分數「反向」——偵測能力越差，分數越高
10 = 完全無法偵測
1 = 顯而易見或有自動監控警報

RPN 的局限性：不能只看總分

以下兩個組合的 RPN 相同，但風險性質截然不同：

  • 案例 A：S=10, O=10, D=1 → RPN=100（嚴重且頻繁，但能偵測）
  • 案例 B：S=10, O=1, D=10 → RPN=100（嚴重但罕見，且完全無法偵測）

案例 B 實際上更危險。因此指南建議：任何單項分數達到最高值（10），無論 RPN 為何，都應強制審查。

偵測力（Detectability）的特殊重要性

在製藥 FMEA 中，偵測力往往是最被低估的維度：

  • 如果事件可以及時偵測，較高的發生頻率尚可管理（因為可以中斷、糾正）
  • 如果事件無法偵測，即使發生機率低，嚴重度又高，就可能已造成患者傷害而無人察覺
  • 無菌填充廠常見的偵測力弱點：培養基灌裝僅能事後驗證、清潔殘留監測覆蓋率不足

比喻：RPN 如信用評分

兩個人可能信用評分相同，但一個是「從未借貸」，另一個是「借了很多但都準時還」——背後的風險輪廓截然不同。RPN 也一樣：同樣的數字可能代表完全不同的風險結構，需要看各分項才能真正理解風險。

思考練習：計算 RPN

情境：無菌填充線的隔離器手套破損（Glove Integrity Failure）

  • 嚴重度（S）：手套破損可能導致操作員污染無菌製程 → 患者可能接受微生物污染產品 → S = 10
  • 發生機率（O）：手套每月例行性完整性測試，歷史紀錄顯示每年約發生 1–2 次 → O = 3
  • 偵測力（D）：有線上手套完整性監測系統，可即時警報 → D = 1
  • RPN = 10 × 3 × 1 = 30

注意：即使 RPN = 30（相對低），但 S = 10，依照指南建議仍需強制審查此項目。

11.4

Statistical Analysis — 統計分析

p117 | Process Capability (Cpk/Ppk), application to risk assessment

Original Text (English)

11.4 Statistical Analysis

Statistical analysis is used to analyze quantitative data to identify trends, variations and likelihood processes will provide the desired results.

Typical outputs of statistical analysis are Process Capability (Cpk) and Process Performance Indices (Ppk).

Statistical analysis capabilities are available in Excel or software packages such as Minitab. It is very important that the statistical analysis of data including interpretation of output from the software packages noted is completed by a properly qualified statistician or similar.

Advanced Topic: Statistical analysis is designated as an advanced topic in this Guide, indicating its application requires additional expertise beyond standard risk management practitioners.
解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

統計分析在風險評估中的角色

統計分析為 FMEA 和風險矩陣提供量化佐證——從「我們認為發生機率低」轉變為「歷史數據顯示 Cpk = 1.8，製程能力充分」。

製程能力指數概念

Cpk（短期製程能力）：
  衡量製程在受控條件下相對於規格限的集中能力
  Cpk ≥ 1.33 → 通常視為合格（4σ）
  Cpk ≥ 1.67 → 較高標準（5σ）

Ppk（長期製程績效）：
  衡量製程在實際長期運行中的表現
  通常 Ppk < Cpk（因包含特殊原因變異）

風險評估應用：
  Cpk 低 → 製程不穩定 → FMEA 中 O（發生機率）分數應較高
  Cpk 高 + 受控 → 可支持降低 O 分數的決策依據

「必須由合格統計師解讀」的重要性

本指南特別強調：統計輸出（如 Cpk/Ppk）的解讀必須由具備統計能力的人員執行。常見誤用包括：

  • 用非正態分配的數據直接計算 Cpk
  • 以過少的數據點（n < 30）做能力分析
  • 誤解 Minitab 輸出圖形的統計意義

統計分析在清潔驗證的應用

在交叉污染風險管理中，統計分析最常用於：

  • 清潔驗證趨勢分析：追蹤多批次清潔後殘留量趨勢，確認不超過 ADE 基礎限值
  • 環境監測數據：分析微粒/微生物監測結果的統計分布，設定行動限與警戒限
  • 製程參數監控：以 Cpk 評估填充量精準度等關鍵參數的製程能力
12

Risk Review — 風險審查

p119 | Periodic reassessment, trigger events, ADE review, change control link

Original Text (English)

12 Risk Review

ICH Q9 states risk management should be an ongoing part of the quality management process. A mechanism to review internal processes and external events should be implemented.

Periodic reviews should be performed on all aspects of the risk management system to ensure that it is being applied effectively and that any potential improvements are identified and incorporated into the process.

This should include a periodic review of the ADE, especially if established early in the drug development timeline, as new information is being gathered from preclinical and clinical studies on a continuous basis.

Any manufacturing deviations or system changes that could impact the potential for exposure (product or personnel) or might compromise the conclusions drawn from previous risk assessments should be closely reviewed. The system may need to be modified so that it does not present an increased potential for exposure.

Any review or, where necessary, reassessment should be documented accordingly.

An organization's quality management processes also should consider need for any reassessment to ensure that original assumptions and performance data remain valid. This may include or require:

  • Auditing of processes and activities
  • Qualitative or quantitative monitoring of performance

Any change to the risk profile should be communicated as described in risk communication.

解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

風險審查的本質：持續性而非一次性

ICH Q9 強調風險管理是持續性的生命週期活動（ongoing lifecycle activity），不是「做了一次 FMEA 就結束」。

風險審查體系要求兩種機制並行：

  • 定期審查（Periodic）：排程、主動、有節奏
  • 觸發式審查（Triggered）：由事件驅動、反應性

必須觸發重新評估的事件清單

  • ADE 值更新：新的毒理學數據發布，原 ADE 值需要修訂
  • 製程偏差（Deviation）：清潔驗證失敗、環境監測超標、無菌測試陽性
  • 設備/廠房變更：引入新設備、HVAC 修改、房間重新規劃
  • 產品組合變更：引入新化合物（尤其是高活性 API）、停產某產品
  • 監管要求更新：新版 EMA/FDA 指引、新版 ICH Q9
  • 審計/稽查發現：內外部稽查發現現有風險評估的假設不成立

ADE 定期審查的特殊重要性

本指南特別強調 ADE 的定期複查，原因是：

  • 早期開發階段建立的 ADE 往往基於有限的毒理數據
  • 隨著臨床研究進展，新的安全性數據可能會降低（更嚴格）或提高（更寬鬆）ADE
  • ADE 改變直接影響清潔限值，進而影響整個風險評估結論

比喻：風險審查像車輛定期保養

汽車需要定期保養（定期審查），但也需要在事故後立即送廠檢修（觸發式審查）。「上次保養才三個月，所以不用管這次追撞」——這個邏輯在風險管理中同樣是錯誤的。事件發生就必須重新評估，不論上次定期審查是何時。

文件要求

所有風險審查（無論定期或觸發式）都必須文件化，包含：

  • 審查觸發原因（或排程日期）
  • 審查範圍與方法
  • 結論：原評估仍有效 / 需要修訂
  • 如需修訂：變更內容及批准記錄
  • 溝通記錄（如適用）
13

Risk Communication — 風險溝通

p121 | Stakeholder layers, escalation, ADE/OEL change notifications, CAPA linkage

Original Text (English)

13 Risk Communication

ICH Q9 defines risk communication as the sharing of information about risk and risk management between the decision makers and others. Organizations should document, within their quality management systems, who needs to communicate what, to whom, and at what frequency, in support of a risk management process.

Different levels of information will be appropriate to different stakeholders who may be internal or external to the organization. It is important to have an escalation process that allows management to be informed of areas that have risk that is unacceptable or near unacceptable.

The holistic approach described in this Guide is predicated on the fact that all of those involved have received appropriate education or training and have ready access to supporting risk assessment and management documentation.

Risk Communication can be enhanced by incorporating linkages within the change control, product quality review and CAPA quality systems.

It is important that companies have a means to widely and effectively communicate to all parties that might be affected including company manufacturing sites, contract manufacturers and QA departments any identified amendments to ADEs (and OELs) or other items that may affect the risk assessment.

In addition if a company chooses to have product-specific ADEs (where the following product is known) or ADEs for specific routes of exposure or dosage types (such as OSD or parenteral) rather than address these issues in the risk assessment, the company should have a robust process to manage these values and make clear to all that may depend on these values what the criteria used to determine the ADEs are and how they should be modified for other usage.

解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

風險溝通的三個維度

ICH Q9 對風險溝通的定義強調的是「雙向資訊共享」而非單向通知。有效的風險溝通需要回答三個問題：

  • Who（誰）：溝通主體（決策者）與接受方（利害關係人）
  • What（什麼）：根據利害關係人的角色，提供不同層次的資訊
  • When（何時）：頻率（定期）＋觸發時機（風險改變時）

ADE/OEL 修訂的溝通義務

本指南明確要求：當 ADE 或 OEL 值發生更新時，必須即時廣泛溝通至所有受影響方，包括：

  • 公司內各製造廠區
  • 合約製造商（CMO/CDMO）
  • QA 部門

這對 CDMO 尤其重要——客戶更新了某化合物的 ADE，CDMO 必須同步更新自己的清潔限值和風險評估。

比喻：風險溝通像「廣播系統」與「升級電梯」

良好的風險溝通需要兩個系統並存：一個廣播系統（讓所有人都能接收到例行更新），以及一個緊急升級電梯（當風險超標時，訊息能立即到達決策層）。只有廣播沒有電梯，管理層永遠不知道有問題；只有電梯沒有廣播，執行層人員缺乏日常風險意識。

與 QMS 整合：變更控制 + PQR + CAPA

本指南建議將風險溝通嵌入三個現有 QMS 系統：

  • 變更控制（Change Control）：任何製程/設備/產品變更觸發風險重評，結論通過變更控制傳遞
  • 產品品質審查（PQR）：年度 PQR 包含風險趨勢回顧，作為定期審查載體
  • CAPA：風險控制行動項目通過 CAPA 系統追蹤與關閉，確保可追溯
13.1

Summary Document Template — 摘要文件範本

p122–p123 | QRMP document structure, required sections and content guidance

Original Text (English)

13.1 Summary Document Template

Introduction
[insert brief introduction to the purpose of the document/report]

Scope
[insert scope of the document/quality risk management process]

Responsibilities
[insert a listing of the disciplines/personnel participating in the quality risk management process]

Manufacturing Facility and Processes

  • Facility Description: [brief summary of manufacturing, including segregation philosophy, design for prevention of cross-contamination, layout, independent HVAC systems, airflows, HEPA filtration on exhaust air, cleanable surfaces, material flows, etc.]
  • Process and Manufacturing Equipment Description: [brief summary of the process from start to finish, including all points where API or formulated product is handled, transferred, isolated, and which pieces of equipment are used; emphasis on shared equipment (e.g., lyophilizers) where there is a potential for cross-contamination]
  • Standard Operating Procedures, Personnel, Validation Plans: [listing of all applicable SOPs, validation of cleaning procedures, studies, and personnel issues (training, hygiene, access restrictions)]

Risk Assessment

  • Risk Identification
  • Hazard Identification and Dose-Response Assessment: [statement on how hazard identification and dose-response assessment was performed, where monographs are archived, who is responsible, and summary of rationale for each ADE value established]
  • Risk Analysis: [description of risk analysis process; tools used; data collected such as monitoring data from internal/external equipment surfaces and manufacturing areas; comparison to ADEs]
  • Exposure Assessment: [summaries, graphs, or other information on outcome of analyses and exposure assessments; available monitoring results for the facility and specific equipment]
  • Risk Evaluation: [company scoring for risk with actions — unacceptable/acceptable/reduce risk; list of issues requiring risk reduction if FMEA was used]

Risk Control
[summary of control strategies; justification for accepting risk; balancing medical benefit to the patient and the level of risk accepted; use the CAPA system to manage risk reduction items]

Risk Communication
[statement about how this QRMP and its application to specific processes and products was documented and communicated to all appropriate stakeholders; how all those involved have received appropriate training]

Risk Review
[statement on how periodic reviews are performed on all aspects of the quality risk management system; how any deviations or system changes that could lead to exposures above accepted internal benchmarks are addressed; how the system is modified to prevent future occurrences]

Summary
[overall summary concluding that the QRMP has addressed all hazards and exposure pathways and controls have been implemented to maintain risks below acceptable levels]

解析與詮釋（繁體中文）

QRMP 摘要文件：品質風險管理計劃的「結案報告」

QRMP（Quality Risk Management Plan）是整個風險管理流程的書面記錄，包含從危害識別到風險接受決定的完整邏輯鏈。它是稽查員最常要求查閱的核心文件之一。

稽查重點：Facility Description 的「共用設備」條款

範本特別要求在製程描述中強調所有共用設備（如冷凍乾燥機 lyophilizers）。這是因為共用設備是交叉污染風險最高的環節，稽查員會重點審查：

  • 是否識別了所有共用設備？
  • 每個共用設備是否有驗證的清潔程序？
  • 清潔限值是否基於 ADE 計算？

比喻：QRMP 是「風險管理的病歷

就像病歷完整記錄了患者的診斷、治療、後續追蹤——QRMP 完整記錄了製程的危害識別（診斷）、風險控制（治療）、定期審查（後續追蹤）。一份好的 QRMP 應該讓任何新進的 QA 人員或稽查員，都能快速理解「這個廠的風險在哪裡，如何控制，誰負責」。

Hazard Identification 章節的 ADE 連結

範本要求 Hazard Identification 章節必須說明：

  • 危害識別和劑量-反應評估如何執行
  • 毒理學報告（Monograph）存放位置
  • 誰負責維護和更新這些信息
  • 每個化合物 ADE 值的設定依據摘要

這確保 ADE 值有完整的毒理學支撐文件，而非「拍腦袋」決定的數字。

CDMO 應用：撰寫 QRMP 的實務建議

對於無菌填充 CDMO，QRMP 撰寫時需特別注意：

  • Scope 要明確邊界：每次客戶引入新產品，應評估是否需要新的 QRMP 或只是既有文件的修訂
  • Shared equipment list 要完整：填充機、CIP/SIP 系統、過濾器組件都應列入
  • ADE 由誰提供：客戶 API 的 ADE 通常由客戶毒理學家提供，CDMO 需確認來源的可靠性並留存文件
  • Risk Control 要具體：「執行清潔驗證」不夠——應說明「清潔限值 X µg/cm²，依據 ADE Y µg/day 計算，驗證報告編號 Z」

Chapter 14: Appendix 1: Case Scenarios

附錄1：情境案例 | p125-p162

ISPE Baseline® Guide Volume 7 (2nd Ed.): Risk-Based Manufacture of Pharmaceutical Products | p125–p138

本節內容導覽

14.1 附錄介紹 14.2 情境一：明顯可接受 情境一：設施與產品 情境一：風險評估 情境一：結論 14.3 情境二：表面可接受（但實際不可） 情境二：設施與工程控制 情境二：風險評估 情境二：結論與教訓
Original Text — English

14 Appendix 1 – Risk-MaPP Application Examples

14.1 Introduction

The examples provided in this Guide are intended to illustrate four scenarios showing the application of the Risk-MaPP tools. Examples were selected to illustrate suboptimal facility and process configurations. This is intended to demonstrate how a well conducted Quality Risk Management Plan (QRMP) can be used.

None of the examples should be seen as setting a precedent, nor are they a benchmark of an acceptable standard. The examples are intended simply to illustrate that when science and risk-based approaches are applied diligently, facilities and processes that seem to present unacceptable levels of patient risk can consistently deliver product within defined margins for patient safety.

If the risk assessment is for a new product being brought into an existing facility, the QRMP should be part of the change control process.

There are four scenarios which can be summarized as:

  • Scenario 1: Obviously Acceptable
  • Scenario 2: Apparently Acceptable (but was not)
  • Scenario 3: Apparently Unacceptable (but was)
  • Scenario 4: Existing facility with a large product portfolio

To make comparisons easier, examples 1 to 3 use the same basic facility layout, processes, and existing product range. The API being introduced varies between each scenario.

Table 14.1: Compounds Currently Manufactured in the Facility

The ADEs were set by a qualified toxicologist.

The compounds being introduced in each scenario are: Scenario 1 — Another Anti-hypertensive; Scenario 2 — Anti-neoplastic; Scenario 3 — Sex hormone.

A steering committee was set up of the stakeholders including management, legal, regulatory, quality, operations, validation and cleaning specialists, engineering and EHS, and with significant input from toxicology.

The first task of the committee was to conduct a risk analysis, beginning with the logic diagram (see Section 14.6) followed by the use of risk management tools. All stakeholders took part in these exercises.

Outcomes are not as may be perceived by a superficial look.
繁體中文解析

14.1 附錄導論

附錄的核心目的

本附錄提供四個真實情境案例，示範如何將 Risk-MaPP 工具實際應用於多產品製造設施中的新產品引入決策。重點在於說明：表面看起來有問題的設施，透過嚴謹的 QRMP 分析，可能仍可安全生產；反之，看似沒問題的情況，可能隱藏著關鍵風險。

重要聲明

這些案例不是「標準答案」或可引用的先例。每個設施情況不同，不可直接套用。案例的價值在於展示思考過程，而非提供固定結論。

四個情境概覽

  • 情境一（明顯可接受）：引入相似類型的抗高血壓藥，風險輪廓相近，評估過程直接清晰。
  • 情境二（表面可接受，但實際不可）：引入抗腫瘤藥，最終因清潔驗證瓶頸而放棄。
  • 情境三（表面不可接受，但實際可以）：引入性荷爾蒙，透過工程控制最終獲批。
  • 情境四：現有設施多產品組合的全面評估。

如何閱讀這些案例

情境一至三使用同一個基礎設施（Kingswood, CT），只有引入的新 API 不同。這個設計讓讀者能直接比較：同一個廠房，引入不同風險等級的化合物，決策路徑如何分岐。把它想成「同一個廚房，做不同料理」——設備一樣，但某些食材的交叉污染風險就是不一樣。

Logic Diagram 的作用

Logic Diagram（第 14.6 節）是整個評估流程的導引工具，類似決策樹。評估團隊從第一個問題出發，逐步回答每個節點，最終得出是否需要隔離設施，或是否可以透過工程控制解決問題。每個情境的評估都從這裡開始。

CDMO 操作要點

當客戶要求導入新產品時，根據此框架，QRMP 應納入變更控制（Change Control）程序中正式執行，而不是個案討論。跨部門指導委員會（含毒理、EHS、法規、生產、清潔驗證）的組建是成功評估的前提條件。

Original Text — English

14.2 Scenario 1 (Obviously Acceptable)

Scenario 1 — Obviously Acceptable

In this example, the owner wishes to introduce an anti-hypertensive product (AntitenseTM) into the facility. The owner has an excellent history of compliance with the agencies that cover the territories in which the products are sold.

After the FMEA review, the final version of a QRMP summary was produced to show how ICH Q9 had been applied to minimize or prevent risk to product/patient.

Quality Risk Management Plan for Technology Transfer and Commercialization of Antitense™

Overview

The document covers the introduction of Antitense™ into an existing multiproduct manufacturing facility. A formalized risk management approach was applied to the Kingswood, CT manufacturing facility. The assessment supported the development of a QRMP that addressed the manufacture of the following products: antacid, anti-hypertensive, and NSAID.

A cornerstone of the QRMP is the establishment of Acceptable Daily Exposure (ADE) values for the active ingredients handled in the manufacturing facility. The ADEs serve as the starting point for the rest of the risk assessment process as described by ICH Q9, which ultimately leads to risk controls sufficient to provide adequate protection of workers and patients.

Table 14.2: Scenario 1 – ADE Values for Active Ingredients

The ADEs were set by a qualified toxicologist.

Facility Description

The facility under review is a single corridor facility with access from a GMP gowning area for personnel and a material airlock to a warehouse, in which a pharmacy and sampling area are located. Each of the unit processes is located off the common corridor. Air is supplied on a recirculation basis. Up to two compounds are processed at one time. See Figure 14.1.

Process Equipment Description

The range of operations and equipment used includes:

  • Sampling of the API
  • Weighing to batch weight of the API
  • High shear granulation and wet milling prior to charging to a fluid bed dryer
  • Discharge into the fluid bed dryer
  • Vacuum discharge to an inline cone mill transfer to a bin
  • Bin or V-Shell blend
  • Lubricant is added
  • V-shell discharged into a bin or bin connection to compression
  • Coating for some products
  • Products are bottle or blister packed

Standard Operating Procedures, Personnel, Validation Plans

The facility has an excellent history of compliance with the agencies that cover the territories in which the products are sold.

繁體中文解析

14.2 情境一：明顯可接受

情境一 — Obviously Acceptable

情境設定：為何「明顯可接受」？

業主希望將一個新的抗高血壓藥 Antitense™ 引入現有設施。此設施已有一個相同治療類別的抗高血壓藥在生產中（Anti-hypertensive A，ADE = 0.5 mg/day）。新產品的 ADE 為 0.3 mg/day，略低於現有品，但屬於同一數量級，且現有清潔流程已被驗證能控制類似風險。

關鍵數據解讀：ADE 比較

Antitense™ 的 ADE = 0.3 mg/day，計算如下：

  • 臨床最低治療劑量：10 mg/day
  • 個體間差異調整因子（AFH）：10
  • 外推至無效應劑量的調整因子（AFL）：3
  • ADE = 10 mg ÷ 10 ÷ 3 = 0.33 mg/day ≈ 0.3 mg/day

與現有 Anti-hypertensive A（ADE = 0.5）相比，Antitense™ 只是稍微更嚴格，並未跨越一個數量級的門檻。

設施條件：重要背景

此情境中的設施使用空氣循環（recirculation）系統，這在後續情境二中會是一個問題點。情境一之所以能接受，部分原因是引入的化合物風險等級與現有品相當，不需要特殊隔離設計。

設施特點：單一通道設計、共用走廊、同時最多加工兩種化合物。

Risk Assessment

Risk Identification — Hazard Identification and Dose-Response Assessment

A review of all available data on each API (e.g., data included in the Clinical Investigators Brochure or New Drug Application or the scientific literature) was completed to identify all possible adverse effects. For each compound, the critical effect (the first adverse effect observed at the low end of the dose-response curve) was identified.

The ADE value was derived by dividing the no effect level for the critical endpoint by appropriate adjustment (uncertainty or safety) factors. The ADE was used to derive product contact surface cleaning target values. Additional calculations were made to reflect batch size, product contact equipment surface area, and maximum daily dose of the next product, to arrive at the final surface target value or rinse concentration.

Establishment of ADE for Antitense™

An ADE value of 0.3 mg/day was established for Antitense™. The ADE was based on the low clinical dose of 10 mg and incorporates appropriate adjustment factors: interindividual variability (AFH = 10) and extrapolation to a no effect level (AFL = 3).

Risk Analysis

A review of monitoring data for the existing products and processes was completed to ensure the facility can safely manufacture the products.

Risk Evaluation

The analysis quickly showed that the new compound posed less risk than some compounds already in manufacture, for which data existed showing that they posed an acceptably low level of risk to patient or products.

風險評估解析

ADE 推導邏輯（關鍵概念）

ADE（Acceptable Daily Exposure，每日可接受暴露量）是整個 Risk-MaPP 評估的基石。其推導流程：

  1. 文獻回顧：找出化合物所有不良反應
  2. 識別「關鍵效應」（critical effect）：劑量-反應曲線低端的第一個不良效應
  3. 找出該效應的無不良效應劑量（NOAEL 或等效值）
  4. 除以適當的調整因子（AFH、AFL 等）得出 ADE
  5. 用 ADE 推算清潔驗證目標值（cleaning limits）

思考框架：比較風險，而非絕對風險

風險評估的關鍵洞察：不是問「這個新化合物安不安全？」而是問「這個新化合物的風險，比我們現在已在生產的化合物更高嗎？」。如果現有系統已成功控制 Anti-hypertensive A（ADE 0.5），那麼 ADE 0.3 的 Antitense™ 只需驗證清潔效果稍微更嚴格即可，不需要重新設計設施。

Risk Evaluation 的速捷判斷

「The analysis quickly showed that the new compound posed less risk than some compounds already in manufacture」——這句話是情境一成立的核心。現有監測資料已顯示設施可控制更高挑戰性的化合物，新品的 ADE 雖稍低，但整體風險輪廓未超出現有能力範圍。

Summary — Scenario 1

The new anti-hypertensive has an ADE that is slightly lower than the current anti-hypertensive agent which is manufactured under existing QRMP No. 170129. The new anti-hypertensive can be cleaned to acceptable levels using the current cleaning protocols and methods. The introduction of this new anti-hypertensive poses no additional risk of patient exposure.

情境一：CDMO 結論與應用啟示

為何評估「快速」完成？

情境一之所以稱為「Obviously Acceptable」，是因為：

  • 新品與現有品屬同一藥理類別（抗高血壓），毒理輪廓相似
  • 新品 ADE（0.3 mg/day）與現有品（0.5 mg/day）在同一數量級
  • 現有清潔流程已被歷史數據驗證能達到更嚴格的要求
  • 現有監測數據庫充足，不需要額外的暴露評估

Logic Diagram 路徑（情境一）

Q1
新 API 的風險等級是否超過現有產品？
答：否（ADE 相似，同類藥物）
Q2
現有清潔系統能否達到新的清潔限值？
答：是（歷史數據顯示現有程序可達）
結論
可引入，無需設施改造。納入現有 QRMP 範疇，更新清潔驗證目標值即可。

CDMO 實務啟示

對 CDMO 而言，情境一代表最理想的新產品引入情況：客戶帶來的新品與現有產品在毒理學上可比較，且設施已有相應的控制能力。關鍵文件工作：更新 QRMP 以納入新品，更新清潔驗證計劃（cleaning validation plan）以反映略微更嚴格的目標值，並確認現有 SOP 覆蓋新品的所有製程步驟。

Original Text — English

14.3 Scenario 2 (Apparently Acceptable (but was NOT))

Scenario 2 — Apparently Acceptable (but was NOT)

In this example, the owner wishes to introduce an anti-neoplastic agent into the facility. The owner has an excellent history of compliance with the agencies that cover the territories in which the products are sold.

After the FMEA review, the final version of a QRMP summary was produced to show how ICH Q9 had been applied to minimize or prevent risk to product/patient.

Quality Risk Management Plan for Technology Transfer and Commercialization of Anti-neoplastic Agent C

Overview

The document covers the introduction of anti-neoplastic Agent C into an existing multiproduct manufacturing facility. A formalized risk management approach was applied to the Kingswood, CT manufacturing facility. The assessment supported the development of a QRMP addressing: antacid, anti-hypertensive, anti-neoplastic, and NSAID.

Table 14.3: Scenario 2 – ADE Values for Active Ingredients

The ADEs were set by a qualified toxicologist.

Facility Description

The facility under review is a single corridor facility with access from a GMP gowning area for personnel and a material airlock to a warehouse. Each of the unit processes is located off the common corridor. Air is supplied on a once through basis. Up to two compounds are processed at one time. See Figure 14.2.

Segregation Philosophy

Following the FMEA analysis, changes were made to the facility to protect the existing products from cross-contamination by the proposed anti-neoplastic. The philosophy behind these changes:

  • The processes were closed by the retrofitting of engineering control methods. API handling for sampling and subdivision takes place in an isolator for anti-neoplastic Agent C. Closed transfer using bins and split butterfly valves (SBV) was introduced for all transfers for all compounds.
  • Fan assisted safe change room boundary filtration introduced to reduce the risk of fugitive API distribution by HVAC system.
  • Additional gowning: disposable coveralls, bootees, and hair nets in rooms where anti-neoplastic Agent C is being processed. Gowning removed at room boundary.
  • Access to process rooms controlled by electronic verification. Only correct materials and personnel allowed to enter.
  • Cleaning bay divided into clean and dirty sides with a pass through for equipment. Gowning to prevent cross-contamination for dirty side personnel.
  • Anti-neoplastic Agent C equipment subjected to a closed in place clean before leaving the process room.
  • All walls, floors, and ceilings of hard washable coved construction.
  • Material flows controlled by electronic verification (bar code readers) allowing separation in time between material transits in the corridor. Movement of more than one compound at a time with a 1-minute dwell is enforced.
繁體中文解析

14.3 情境二：表面可接受（但實際不可）

情境二 — Apparently Acceptable (but was NOT)

情境設定：為何「表面可接受」？

業主希望引入抗腫瘤藥 Anti-neoplastic Agent C，一種烷化劑。初步看來，業主已:

  • 在設施中大量投入工程控制（隔離器、密閉傳輸、獨立空調）
  • 建立完整的 SOP 體系（進出人員管制、清潔程序等）
  • 使用一次性通風（once-through）以避免循環污染

光看工程控制清單，似乎已做到位。問題出在哪裡？

關鍵差異：ADE 數量級的跳躍

Anti-neoplastic Agent C 的 ADE = 0.001 mg/day（即 1 μg/day），遠低於設施現有化合物：

  • Antacid：50 mg/day（高出 50,000 倍）
  • Anti-hypertensive：0.5 mg/day（高出 500 倍）
  • NSAID：40 mg/day（高出 40,000 倍）

這個數量級的差距，意味著清潔限值的要求將比現有設備歷史表現嚴格得多。

為何 ADE 如此低？

Anti-neoplastic Agent C 是一種直接作用型基因毒性致癌物（direct acting genotoxic material）。其毒理特性：

  • 烷化劑，干擾 DNA 複製與 RNA 轉錄
  • 動物試驗：低至 2.5 mg/kg/day 即產生發育毒性
  • 損傷成年大鼠精子 DNA
  • 多種動物中增加惡性腫瘤發生率
  • 人類研究確認具致癌性

ADE 推算基於癌症風險外推，1 μg/day 對應 1 × 10⁻⁵ 的額外癌症風險（即百萬分之十的超額風險）。

「Once-Through」vs「循環」通風的意義

情境一設施使用空氣循環（recirculation），對於情境二這樣的高毒性化合物是不可接受的風險。業主在情境二中已切換為一次通過式（once-through）通風——這是正確的工程決策，確保空氣中的微粒不會在設施內循環。

工程控制架構（情境二特有）

情境二中導入的控制措施比情境一更全面，包括：

  • 隔離器（Isolator）：取樣、稱重在隔離器內進行
  • 密閉傳輸：Split Butterfly Valve（SBV）、Rapid Transfer Port（RTP）
  • 房間邊界 HEPA 過濾：風扇輔助安全換氣，防止逸散 API 進入 HVAC
  • 電子門禁：條碼讀取器控制人員與物料流動，走廊內強制 1 分鐘間隔
  • 就地密閉清洗（CIP）：設備離開製程室前先進行密閉式清潔

Process and Manufacturing Equipment Description

The range of operations and equipment used includes:

  • Sampling of incoming API in an isolator; sample sent to QA lab in a closed transfer device — Rapid Transfer Port (RTP).
  • Weighing to batch weight in an isolator; closed transfer in a bin with a Split Butterfly Valve (SBV).
  • High shear granulation and wet milling prior to charging to a fluid bed dryer. The active is layered into the granulator; heel retention is very high, requiring manual scraping for yield. Process conducted in an isolator; transfer in a closed bin.
  • Discharge into the fluid bed dryer bowl in an isolator. Fluid bed dryer is a closed operation: vacuum discharge to an isolator with a hammer type mill; collection in a weigh hopper; vacuum transfer to a bin via SBV.
  • Bin blend or bin to V-Shell transfer using transfer valves and bins.
  • Lubricant added via transfer valve on side arm of V-shell or via charge using SBV to a bin.
  • V-Cone® discharged into SBV bins or blending bin used without transfer. Bins tested for blend uniformity using PAT.
  • Products that are tableted passed to compression with the bin connected via SBV.
  • Products B and C are coated; A is not. Data shows no risk of exposure from coating.
  • Products are bottle or blister packed.

Following the steps in the logic diagram (see Section 14.6), manufacture of the compound was possible.

Personnel access into the process rooms is controlled by card reader. Personnel are trained in gown/de-gown procedures. Personnel who clean equipment put on wet gear and boots at the designated position.

製程設備：密閉系統設計要點

密閉系統的設計邏輯

整個製程設計圍繞一個核心原則：在任何可能產生逸散 API 的節點，全面實施密閉操作。重要設備節點：

  • 隔離器（Isolator）：取樣、稱重、造粒
  • Split Butterfly Valve（SBV）：所有物料傳輸密閉接口
  • Rapid Transfer Port（RTP）：實驗室樣品傳遞
  • 流化床乾燥器：密閉操作、真空排料
  • V-Blender（V 型混合機）：物料進出均使用 SBV

Logic Diagram 路徑（情境二——初步評估）

Q：需要隔離？
Anti-neoplastic ADE = 0.001 mg/day，屬高活性化合物（HPAPI）
→ 需要工程控制
Q：工程控制夠用？
已安裝隔離器、密閉傳輸、once-through 通風、門禁
→ 表面上看似充足
Q：清潔可達標？
需要進一步 FMEA 分析…
→ 此處發現問題

HVAC

Figure 14.5🔍 shows the pressure cascade and airflow direction in the rooms. The flow is always away from the corridor and toward the rear wall. Supply is through HEPA filters; exhaust via roughing and HEPA filters to protect the ductwork. The MALs and PALs create lock chambers with door operation delay to allow the airlock to be purged. The system is once through — no risk of recirculating particulate.

Exhausts are protected by redundant HEPA filtration (two passes through 99.997% filters with pressure differentials indicated and alarmed). Routine challenge testing is performed.

For product to cross-contaminate another product it must: escape the process; pass through airlocks against low velocity airflow; travel into the corridor; enter another airlock; enter another room; enter the other process.

Key SOPs Brought About by FMEA Analysis

  • Access control procedures for personnel and materials into process areas
  • Cleaning procedures and gowning
  • Health-based cleaning protocol
  • Material handling procedures
  • Gowning/de-gowning procedures
  • HVAC performance monitoring and filter replacement
  • Procedures to cover closed operation
  • Sampling and subdivision protocols
  • Handling and storage of anti-neoplastic Agent C
  • Upset recovery protocols

HVAC 與 SOP 系統解析

多重氣流屏障設計

情境二的 HVAC 設計展示了「縱深防禦（defence in depth）」原則：即使製程室發生逸散事件，污染物仍需突破多個屏障才能進入走廊或其他製程室：

  1. 製程室本身負壓（相對走廊）
  2. 門廳（airlock）的吹掃延遲
  3. 走廊正壓（相對製程室）
  4. 排氣雙重 HEPA 過濾（99.997% × 2）
  5. 一次通過式通風（無循環風險）

SOPs 的 FMEA 驅動設計

值得注意的是：SOP 清單中包含「Upset recovery protocols」（異常恢復程序）。這表明評估團隊認識到，即使在正常操作時系統可控，但當發生設備異常（如密封失效、溢漏）時，需要預定義的應對程序。此類「最壞情境」SOP 是 HPAPI 設施的必要文件。

「表面可接受」的陷阱

此時，若只看工程控制清單——隔離器、SBV、HEPA、電子門禁——的確看起來很完整。但 Risk-MaPP 的力量在於不允許評估在此止步。FMEA 強制團隊逐一檢視每個製程步驟的殘留風險，其中隱藏的炸彈在下一步才被發現。

Risk Assessment — Scenario 2

Establishment of ADE for Anti-neoplastic Agent C

Anti-neoplastic Agent C is an alkylating agent used in the treatment of numerous myeloproliferative and lymphoproliferative disorders and solid malignancies. It disrupts nucleic acid function by interfering with DNA replication and transcription of RNA. The recommended oral dosage ranges from 1 to 5 mg/kg/day for adults or 10 to 15 mg/kg IV every 7 to 10 days.

Anti-neoplastic Agent C is considered moderately toxic orally and produced adverse developmental effects in animals at dosages as low as 2.5 mg/kg/day. It was shown to damage DNA in spermatozoa from adult male rats and increased the incidence of malignant tumors by several routes of administration. The compound has been shown to be a human carcinogen.

The critical endpoint for deriving a health-based value is cancer. Because it is a direct acting genotoxic material, the ADE was derived by extrapolating cancer risks from animal and human tumor data. An ADE of 1 μg/day was calculated corresponding to a 1 × 10⁻⁵ excess cancer risk.

Risk Analysis — Plausible Pathways

Mix-up: Bar code reading control of all equipment and materials; separation of clean and dirty equipment by room; tagging of clean and dirty equipment.

Retention on Product Contact Surfaces: Swab monitoring of cleaning performance against health-based limits; visually clean inspection; routine monitoring shows consistent performance well below the health-based limit — except where the FMEA identified the blender issue.

Mechanical Transfer: Critical transfers are closed; all equipment and materials wiped down or bagged before leaving the process room; tack mats used at room boundaries.

Airborne Transfer: Processes occur in rooms protected by airlocks; corridor positive relative to process rooms; redundant HEPA filtration on exhausts.

Cleaning Review

Cleaning Process Development activities:

  • Cleanability assessments
  • Cleaning agent(s) selection
  • Design of cleaning processes
  • FMEAs for each cleaning process
  • Modification of cleaning processes based on FMEA results

Cleaning Risk Evaluation activities:

  • Collection of swab sample data on each cleaning procedure
  • Process capability evaluations of swab sample data
  • FMEAs of overall cleaning program to identify high risk procedures
  • Improvement/optimization of high risk procedures

Cleaning Process Review: a cleanability assessment was performed on the product and the product was found to be easily cleaned by the existing processes. The cleanability rank was a 2, with a rank of 4 for the hardest to clean product. Current cleaning agents were found to be appropriate for solubilizing and suspending the product.

風險評估深度解析

致癌物的 ADE 推算：無閾值模型

Anti-neoplastic Agent C 屬於直接作用型基因毒性物質（direct acting genotoxic），不同於一般毒性物質使用 NOAEL ÷ 調整因子的方法。基因毒性致癌物通常採用線性無閾值外推（linear no-threshold extrapolation）：

  • 從動物或人類腫瘤數據推算癌症風險
  • 選定可接受的超額癌症風險水準（此案為 1 × 10⁻⁵）
  • 反推出對應的每日暴露量 = ADE = 1 μg/day

這解釋了為何 ADE 比普通化合物低了 3 個數量級。

四條暴露途徑的評估架構

Risk-MaPP 要求評估所有「合理可能的暴露途徑（plausible pathways）」：

  • Mix-up（混藥）：標籤錯誤、設備誤置 → 條碼管制
  • Retention on product contact surfaces（殘留）：清洗不乾淨 → 清潔驗證
  • Mechanical transfer（機械傳遞）：設備移動帶出污染 → 密閉系統
  • Airborne transfer（氣載傳遞）：揚塵或氣流帶出 → HVAC 設計

清潔可行性：初步令人放心

注意：清潔可行性評估（cleanability rank = 2，最難清潔品為 4）顯示 Agent C 相對容易清洗，清潔劑也適用。這讓評估團隊最初以為清潔不是問題。但這只是化合物本質的清潔性，尚未考慮設備的幾何形狀與表面積帶來的挑戰。

Ppk 分析：從「數量」到「限值」的挑戰

想像清潔驗證就像射靶：現有設備一直射在靶心附近（Ppk 高），清潔表現穩定。但引入 Agent C 後，靶心的位置（清潔限值）移動到了之前從未達到的極小值。即使你的射擊精準度（製程能力）沒有改變，靶心太遠就是射不中。

Risk Evaluation — The Critical Finding

New Product Review

The new anti-neoplastic product was evaluated against the existing program for its compatibility with the cleaning processes and its ADE was assessed against the existing swab sampling database for the facility.

The FMEA analysis of cleaning showed a significant risk occurring in the V-blender which, due to its significant surface area, required a level of residue significantly below the historically achievable results.

Cleaning Risk Evaluation — Ppk Analysis

The swab data for all cleaning processes were found to have high Process Performance Indices (Ppk) with undetectable levels Defects per Million Opportunities (ppm) — with the exception of the blender.

The Ppk for the blender was 0.34 with the potential for Defects per Million Opportunities of 14,994. This evaluation indicated that the current cleaning process for the blender is not satisfactory to safely clean the new product.

In order to introduce the new product into the facility, the cleaning process for the blender would need to be improved or a new blender would have to be purchased.

Risk Control

A conclusion was made that the risks to patients with the existing manufacturing process was unacceptably high. This was due to the potential carryover of residuals of Anti-neoplastic Agent C to other products from the V-blender.

A Design of Experiment (DoE) was performed to improve the Blender Cleaning Process. Cleaning agent concentration, cleaning time, cleaning temperature, and rinse time were evaluated. The new data indicate that the blender cannot be effectively cleaned to safe levels for the new product. The introduction of a dedicated blender was not possible and so the proposal was abandoned and the anti-neoplastic will not be manufactured at this site.

Risk Communication

No further communication on the proposed introduction of Anti-neoplastic Agent C is required because the proposal was rejected.

Summary — Scenario 2

The FMEA analysis of cleaning showed a significant risk occurring in the V-blender which due to its significant surface area required a level of residue significantly below the historically achievable results. Since the other processes required a V-blender and no space was available for a dedicated blender, the owner decided not to manufacture Anti-neoplastic Agent C.

情境二：關鍵發現與教訓

核心發現：V-Blender 成為阻斷因素

整個情境二的轉折點在於 FMEA 清潔評估的量化數據：

  • 除 V-Blender 以外，所有設備的清潔 Ppk 值高，ppm（缺陷率）趨近於零
  • V-Blender 的 Ppk = 0.34（正常標準為 Ppk ≥ 1.33 表示能力充足）
  • 對應的缺陷率 DPM = 14,994 ppm（即每百萬次清潔中有近 1.5 萬次無法達標）
  • 問題根源：V-Blender 表面積大，對 ADE = 1 μg/day 的化合物，清潔限值極低，遠超現有能力

Ppk 數值的意義

製程能力指數（Ppk）代表製程實際輸出相對於規格限值的能力：

  • Ppk ≥ 1.33：製程能力良好（cGMP 通常要求）
  • Ppk = 1.00：邊界值，約 0.27% 的失敗率
  • Ppk = 0.34：嚴重不足，幾乎 1.5% 的批次清潔後殘留超標

換算成患者風險：每 67 批（≈1000 ppm ÷ 14.994）就可能有一批清潔失敗，導致下一個產品被致癌物污染。

DoE 嘗試失敗：邊界在哪裡？

評估團隊沒有輕易放棄。他們進行了正式的實驗設計（DoE），系統性地優化：

  • 清潔劑濃度
  • 清潔時間
  • 清潔溫度
  • 沖洗時間

DoE 結論：即使在最佳化條件下，V-Blender 就是無法被清潔至足夠安全的水準。這是設備幾何形狀（大表面積）與物理化學限制共同決定的結果，非 SOP 可以克服。

最終決定：拒絕引入

解決方案本可以是購買專用 V-Blender（dedication）——但廠房無法容納。在無法解決設備問題的情況下，業主做出了正確的決策：拒絕在此設施生產 Anti-neoplastic Agent C。

這本身是一個重要的監管信號：Risk-MaPP 流程的價值不在於「讓所有產品都能生產」，而在於提供科學依據拒絕無法安全生產的品項。

Logic Diagram 完整路徑（情境二）

步驟 1
ADE = 1 μg/day → 屬高活性物質（HPAPI）
→ 需要工程控制 / FMEA
步驟 2
導入隔離器、SBV、once-through 通風 → 氣載、機械傳遞途徑受控
→ 表面上可以繼續
步驟 3
清潔 FMEA：V-Blender 表面積大，清潔限值超出歷史能力（Ppk = 0.34）
→ 關鍵風險識別：清潔無法達標
步驟 4
DoE 嘗試優化 → 失敗；購買專用 Blender → 廠房無空間
→ 最終結論：無法引入，拒絕提案

CDMO 核心教訓

對 CDMO 最重要的啟示：

  • 工程控制完備，不等於清潔驗證必然可達。兩者需要獨立評估。
  • 清潔驗證的挑戰不只是「能不能洗乾淨」，更要看設備幾何形狀（表面積）是否允許達到所需的清潔限值。
  • Ppk 分析是清潔風險量化的有效工具——不要只看「合格/不合格」，要看製程能力指數是否足夠應對新品的嚴格限值。
  • 能夠拒絕客戶要求（在科學依據下），本身就是 Risk-MaPP 系統發揮價值的體現。
  • 在報價或技術轉移評估早期，應先查清設施中最大表面積設備的歷史清潔 Ppk，再評估能否引入高活性化合物。

Cross-Scenario Comparison: Scenarios 1 vs. 2

情境一 vs. 情境二：比較總結

決定性差異：數量級跳躍觸發不同評估路徑

兩個情境使用同一個設施，評估結果截然相反。關鍵在於：

  • 情境一：新 ADE（0.3）與現有最低 ADE（0.5）在同一數量級，現有系統可覆蓋。
  • 情境二：新 ADE（0.001）低了兩到三個數量級，觸發完全不同的工程控制要求，且進一步發現清潔設備的物理限制無法克服。

本章的核心訊息

不要以「看起來有嚴格工程控制 = 可以引入」作為評估終點。Risk-MaPP 要求你系統性地走完所有路徑——特別是清潔驗證的製程能力量化分析——才能得出真正基於科學的結論。

給監管審查員的信號

情境二最終的主動拒絕（self-rejection）本身就是品質文化成熟度的體現。監管機構最希望看到的是：企業能在問題變成缺陷前，用科學方法找到邊界，並做出正確決策——不論那個決策是否有利於商業利益。

ISPE Baseline® Guide Volume 7 (2nd Ed.): Risk-Based Manufacture of Pharmaceutical Products | p139–p162
