14.4 Scenario 3 概述 QRMP 計畫 設施描述 風險評估 風險控制 Scenario 3 總結 14.5 Scenario 4 概述 背景資訊 風險評估 FMEA 分析 風險評價與控制 Scenario 4 總結 14.6 邏輯圖
14.4 Scenario 3 — Apparently Unacceptable (but WAS) | 表面上不可接受（但其實可行）
Original Text (English)

In this example, the owner wishes to introduce a sex hormone into the facility. Sex hormones have been under increased scrutiny because of the risk of effects on fertility and birth defects. The owner has an excellent history of compliance with the agencies that cover the territories in which the products are sold.

A steering committee was set up of the stakeholders including management, legal, regulatory, and quality, operations, validation and cleaning specialist, engineering and Environment, Health, and Safety (EHS), with input from toxicology.

The first task of the committee was to conduct a risk analysis, beginning with the logic diagram (see Section 14.6) followed by the use of FMEA tools. All stakeholders took part in these exercises.

As soon as the committee had assembled sufficient data, they sought informal discussion with the regulatory agencies and discussed the proposal in concept. Supporting scientific data was made available and a draft of the QRMP document was tabled.

Following the logic diagram, segregation was possibly required for this product because it is being supplied to a country that has historically required segregation for sex hormones. An FMEA analysis was then undertaken with a team of stakeholders, this technique was chosen because it addresses a wide range of ICH Q9 topics, including:

  • Risk identification
  • Risk ranking (using the RPN scores)
  • Exposure control assessment
  • Risk analysis

After the FMEA review, the final version of the QRMP was produced to show how ICH Q9 had been applied to minimize or prevent risk to product and operators.

繁體中文解說

為何「表面上不可接受」？

性荷爾蒙（sex hormone）在全球多個監管地區歷史上被要求使用專屬廠房（dedicated facility）。初步看來，將其引入現有多產品設施似乎明顯違規。然而，本場景的關鍵教訓是：透過嚴謹的風險評估流程，可以科學地論證共用設施是可行的。

情境要點

  • 新引入物質：性荷爾蒙 Agent H（極低 ADE = 0.001 mg/day）
  • 挑戰：部分國家法規歷史上要求專屬設施
  • 策略：早期與監管機構非正式溝通 + FMEA + QRMP
  • 結論：透過適當管控措施，可在共用設施製造

比喻：法規要求 vs. 科學論證

就像駕駛人在不確定某條路段是否允許通行前，先主動詢問交通主管單位，而非直接行駛或放棄。提前與主管機關溝通、展示科學數據，是合規策略的核心。

監管溝通的重要性

委員會在擁有足夠數據後，立即主動與監管機關進行非正式討論，並提交 QRMP 草稿。這種「先溝通、再行動」的策略，降低了後期審查風險，也展現了廠商的透明度與責任感。

14.4 Scenario 3 — QRMP Overview | 品質風險管理計畫概述
Original Text (English)

Quality Risk Management Plan (QRMP) for Technology Transfer and Commercialization of Sex Hormone Agent H

Overview

This document summarizes the QRMP for XYZ Pharma at the Kingswood, CT site. The plan embraces the principles of ICH Q9 and uses risk management tools to support manufacturing strategies designed to minimize risks to product and operators.

The proposal is to introduce a sex hormone Agent H into the facility. The existing compounds all have QRMPs in place.

A formalized risk management approach was applied to the manufacturing facility. This involved a holistic assessment that identified the potential hazards and risks to product and operators for all products handled in the facility to ensure that appropriate controls were in place to manufacture these products safely.

A cornerstone of the QRMP is the establishment of ADE values for the active ingredients handled in the manufacturing facility. The ADE values serve as the starting point for the rest of the risk assessment process as described by ICH Q9.

Table 14.4: Scenario 3 — Active Ingredients in the Facility

繁體中文解說

QRMP 的作用

品質風險管理計畫（QRMP）是一份整合性文件，將 ICH Q9 框架系統性地套用於特定設施或產品引入。它不只是風險評估報告，更是一份行動計畫，說明：

  • 識別了哪些危害
  • 採用了哪些評估方法
  • 實施了哪些控制措施
  • 如何監控與審查

ADE 數值差異的意義

從表格可以清楚看出 Agent H（性荷爾蒙）的 ADE 遠低於其他化合物：

  • Antacid A：50 mg/day（相對安全）
  • Anti-hypertensive B：0.5 mg/day
  • Agent H：0.001 mg/day（最低，高效價）
  • NSAID D：40 mg/day

ADE = 0.001 mg/day = 1 µg/day，代表設備表面殘留量必須控制在極低水平。這是此情境「表面上不可接受」的核心原因。

ADE（可接受每日暴露量）定義

ADE 是每日接觸劑量的上限，低於此值預期不會對最敏感族群（包括患者、作業員）產生不良反應，且涵蓋終身暴露。它由合格毒理學家基於毒理數據推導，並包含適當的安全係數。

14.4 Scenario 3 — Facility Description & Controls | 設施描述與管控措施
Original Text (English)

Facility Description

The facility under review is a single corridor facility with access from a GMP gowning area for personnel and a material airlock to a warehouse, in which a pharmacy and sampling area is located. Each of the unit processes is located off the common corridor with both MALs (Material Airlocks) and PALs (Personnel Airlocks); both are single chamber and are pressurized to create a pressure cascade between the processing area and the corridor.

A suite of rooms are provided for dirty side wash, clean side dry, and separate clean storage of equipment. The area is served by a single Air Handling Unit (AHU) with a positive pressure corridor. Air is supplied on a once through basis (no recirculation). Room boundary redundant filtration is provided. Up to two compounds are processed at one time.

Segregation Philosophy (Post-FMEA)

  • The sex hormone API processes were closed. Surrogate testing showed that all other exposures provided an acceptable level of risk and plausible pathways had sufficient redundancy to be protective of other products.
  • Additional gowning introduced: operators wear disposable coveralls, bootees, and hair nets in sex hormone processing rooms. This gowning is removed at the room boundary.
  • Access to process rooms controlled by electronic verification; only the correct materials and personnel are allowed to enter.
  • Sex hormone handling equipment subjected to a closed in-place clean before leaving the process room.
  • All walls, floors, and ceilings are of hard washable coved construction.

Process and Equipment

  • Sampling of incoming API in an isolator with RTP (Rapid Transfer Port) to QA lab
  • Weighing in isolator — closed transfer bin with SBV (Split Butterfly Valve)
  • High shear granulation and wet milling in isolator; heel retention requires manual scraping
  • FBD discharge via SBV; vacuum discharge to in-line cone mill → bin via SBV
  • Bin blend; lubricant via transfer valve; PAT for blend uniformity
  • Compression via SBV-connected bin; coating (data shows no risk of exposure)
  • Bottle or blister packing

HVAC (Figure 14.10🔍)

Pressure cascade: flow always away from corridor and operator zones toward rear wall. Supply through HEPA filters, exhaust via roughing and HEPA filters. MALs and PALs create lock chambers with door operation delay (purge before door release). System is once through — no recirculation risk. Hanging vinyl strip screens at room entrances.

繁體中文解說

單廊式設施（Single Corridor Facility）佈局

設施以單一走廊為主軸，各製程室由 MAL（物料氣閘）和 PAL（人員氣閘）隔離。此設計的優點：

  • 壓力階梯（pressure cascade）可控制空氣流向
  • 氣閘的「淨化延遲」（dwell period）防止門開時的瞬間污染
  • 走廊對製程室保持正壓，確保污染不會從走廊流入

封閉製程（Closed Processing）的核心邏輯

性荷爾蒙 ADE 僅 1 µg/day，若使用開放製程，微量揚塵即可能超標。解決方案是透過工程控制：

  • 隔離器（Isolator）：取樣、稱重在隔離環境進行
  • SBV（裂蝶閥）：密封物料轉移，防止揚塵
  • RTP（快速轉移口）：樣品安全移轉至 QA 實驗室
  • 就地封閉清潔（CIP）：設備離開製程室前先清潔

比喻：SBV 的作用

Split Butterfly Valve（裂蝶閥）像一個「對接連接器」——兩半分別安裝在物料桶與設備接口，對接時同時打開，分離時各自密封，全程粉末不接觸外界空氣，大幅降低揚塵風險。

HVAC 設計的多重防護

HVAC 系統採用「直流式」（once-through，無再循環），這意味著：

  • 污染物不會被再循環風帶回其他區域
  • 排氣通過 HEPA 過濾（粗效 + 高效，兩段保護）
  • 氣閘淨化確保開門時的污染不進入走廊

此設計使得「空氣傳播途徑」的風險透過多重屏障降至可接受水平。

14.4 Scenario 3 — Risk Assessment | 風險評估
Original Text (English)

Risk Identification

A risk assessment process was used to derive criteria to support decision making and control of risks to product and workers. The risk assessment involved an evaluation of all data relevant to support hazard identification, assessment of potency (dose-response) and severity, exposure assessment, and characterization of risk. Risk controls were implemented in a manner commensurate with the risk.

A review of all available data on each API was completed to identify all possible adverse effects. The critical effect (first adverse effect at the low end of the dose-response curve) was identified. The ADE value was derived by dividing the no-effect level for the critical endpoint by appropriate adjustment (uncertainty or safety) factors or to extrapolate to an acceptable level of cancer risk. ADE was used to derive product contact surface cleaning limits.

Establishment of ADE for the Sex Hormone (Agent H)

An ADE value of 1 µg/day was established for sex hormone Agent H. The rationale is summarized in the quality document "Risk Assessment for Sex Hormones." The ADE was based on the low clinical dose and incorporates appropriate adjustment factors to address:

  • Interindividual variability
  • Extrapolation to a no-effect level
  • Differences in bioavailability
  • Residual uncertainties regarding potential developmental effects

Risk Analysis — Plausible Pathways

Mix-up:

  • Bar code reading control of all equipment and materials where they pass into processing rooms
  • Separation of clean and dirty equipment by room; tagging of clean and dirty equipment

Retention (Product Contact Surfaces):

  • Swab monitoring against health-based limits; visually clean inspection
  • Routine monitoring shows consistent performance well below health-based limit (Figure 14.11🔍)
  • Cleaning procedures include disassembly; dedicated blending bin

Mechanical Transfer:

  • Critical transfers are closed
  • All equipment and materials wiped down or bagged before leaving process room
  • Tack mats at room boundaries; outer gowning removed at boundaries

Airborne Transfer:

  • All processes in rooms protected by airlocks with interlocked doors and dwell period
  • Corridor positive pressure to process room; redundant HEPA filtration (99.997% × 2 passes)
  • For cross-contamination to occur, product must: escape process → pass through airlocks against low-velocity flow → travel corridor → enter another airlock → enter process room
  • Gowning protocols and access restriction prevent unauthorized entry
繁體中文解說

四大交叉污染途徑

  • 混淆（Mix-up）：錯誤物料進入製程室（人為錯誤）
  • 殘留（Retention）：前批物料殘留於設備表面
  • 機械轉移（Mechanical Transfer）：殘留物附著於人員、設備、物料表面帶出
  • 空氣傳播（Airborne Transfer）：微粒透過空氣系統傳播

空氣傳播的「多道障礙」論證

ISPE 原文詳細列出空氣傳播必須跨越的每一個障礙：

  1. 逃離製程（escape the process）
  2. 逆低速氣流通過氣閘進入走廊
  3. 在走廊中傳播
  4. 再次逆低速氣流進入另一氣閘
  5. 進入另一製程室及製程

每一步都有物理屏障阻攔，整條路徑的機率極低。這種「多重障礙論證」（multiple barrier argument）是現代 GMP 風險評估的核心邏輯。

ADE 到清潔限度的推導

ADE（1 µg/day）是起點，再結合：

  • 接受患者的最大每日劑量
  • 設備產品接觸面積
  • 批次大小

計算出設備表面最大允許殘留量（µg/cm²），作為清潔驗證的接受標準。

Surrogate Testing（替代物測試）

對於潛在有害物質（如性荷爾蒙），不能使用真實 API 進行清潔驗證的暴露測試。替代物（surrogate）應具有相似的物理化學特性（溶解度、黏附性），但毒性較低，可安全操作。

14.4 Scenario 3 — Cleaning Review, FMEA & Risk Control | 清潔審查、FMEA 及風險控制
Original Text (English)

Cleaning Review — Process Capability

The existing swab sample database was statistically evaluated against the new product's ADE. The swab data for all cleaning processes were found to have high Process Performance Indices (Ppk) with undetectable levels of Defects per Million Opportunities, with the exception of the blender.

The Ppk for the blender was 0.34 with potential for 14,994 Defects per Million Opportunities. This indicated the current cleaning process for the blender is not satisfactory to safely clean the new product.

A Design of Experiment (DoE) was performed to improve the blender cleaning process. Cleaning agent concentration, cleaning time, cleaning temperature, and rinse time were evaluated. The new data indicate the blender can be effectively cleaned to safe levels for the new product.

  • Ppk after DoE: 2.01
  • Defects per Million Opportunities: 251

Because these data indicate a small possibility of product residue, the blender will require a visual inspection and monitoring after each cleaning. To minimize regulatory impact, it was decided to dedicate the blending bin.

Risk Control

It was concluded that sex hormone Agent H could be introduced into the multiproduct manufacturing facility without causing a risk to patients. The control measures adopted were based on a belief that technique and skill-based procedures have a tendency to fail. The controls implemented are of a procedural, mechanical, and electronic nature and are designed to fail safe. Implemented controls include:

  • Electronic access and inventory control — entry and exit from any room permitted only for materials and personnel required at that time. Secondary systems ensure it cannot be bypassed.
  • Critical processes were closed and tested to ensure they afforded both operator and product protection robustly.
  • Automated cleaning introduced to minimize variability from manual cleaning. Small parts still manually cleaned with updated procedures to reduce errors.
  • Air flows and pressures were reversed to maintain security in the event of an upset. Redundant HEPA filtration protects the rest of the facility.
  • Control system effectiveness was verified with quantitative data.
  • Hierarchy of controls closely followed to ensure selection of appropriate technology.
  • Systems designed to alarm when out of range and default to a safe condition.

Risk Communication

A stakeholder team comprising toxicology, formulations, development, operations, quality, regulatory, EHS, and senior management was set up. Key stakeholder members from regulatory, quality, operations, and management were present during FMEA sessions. A web-based bulletin board was set up for collaborative document sharing.

Risk Review

The Quality Risk Plan is reviewed every six months. Stakeholders are rotated so that new members join for each review. Assessments from operators, a log of excursive events, and operability of the system are reviewed. An incentive program solicits input from operators — suggestions leading to risk reduction or quality improvement are implemented and evaluated continuously.

繁體中文解說

Ppk（製程效能指標）解讀

Ppk 衡量製程整體效能（包含製程平均值偏移）：

  • Ppk < 1.0：製程不穩定，超規風險高
  • Ppk = 0.34（改善前）：約 15,000 ppm 超標機率，不可接受
  • Ppk = 2.01（DoE 後）：約 251 ppm，可接受（需加強監控）
  • 工業標準：清潔驗證通常要求 Ppk ≥ 1.33

Scenario 3 的關鍵轉折點

不同於 Scenario 2（混摻機無法達到要求，最終放棄引入），Scenario 3 中：

  • DoE 成功改善清潔製程（Ppk 0.34 → 2.01）
  • 混摻桶（blending bin）改為專屬（dedicated），消除最高風險環節
  • 其他所有管控措施共同論證風險可接受

這正是「表面上不可接受，但實際上可行」的核心：工程措施加上科學數據，成功翻轉了初始的悲觀判斷。

管控層級（Hierarchy of Controls）

ISPE 強調選擇管控措施時應遵循優先順序（由高至低）：

  1. 消除（Elimination）：移除危害源
  2. 替代（Substitution）：以低危害替代
  3. 工程控制（Engineering Controls）：隔離器、密閉轉移
  4. 行政管控（Administrative Controls）：程序、訓練
  5. 個人防護（PPE）：防護服

本情境中，封閉製程（工程控制）是核心，程序和電子管制作為輔助。

「Fail-Safe」設計原則

ISPE 特別強調管控措施應設計為「fail safe」（失效安全）：當系統出現異常，應自動進入安全狀態（例如警報、鎖閉），而非依賴人員反應。電子門禁、HEPA 壓差警報均符合此原則。

六個月滾動審查的實踐意義

風險評估不是「做一次就完成」。定期審查、輪換委員（引入新視角）、結合操作人員的回饋，確保風險計畫與現實製程保持同步，這是 ICH Q9 持續改善精神的體現。

14.4 Scenario 3 — Summary | 總結
Original Text (English)

The stakeholder team has used the range of tools proposed in ICH Q9 and in this Guide to carefully evaluate the facility. During the initial qualitative analysis, deficiencies were identified and actions were implemented to mitigate these deficiencies. An evaluation team spanning relevant disciplines ensured that all hazards and exposure pathways were assessed and controls were implemented to maintain risks at acceptable levels so that the introduction of the new sex hormone Agent H product could be manufactured within the existing facility.

繁體中文解說

Scenario 3 的三大學習要點

  1. 避免過度保守決策：初始感覺「不可行」不等於真的不可行，需要數據支持。
  2. 工程控制優先：DoE 驅動清潔改善、封閉製程設計，讓高效價物質的共用生產成為可能。
  3. 跨職能協作 + 監管早期溝通：降低後期審查風險，建立信任基礎。
14.5 Scenario 4 — Existing Facility with Large Product Portfolio | 現有設施、大型產品組合
Original Text (English)

An existing facility is currently manufacturing 32 products using 10 different APIs. The products and APIs are shown in Table 14.5.

The processes used to manufacture the products are:

  • Process 1: Sample, weigh, mill, granulate, mill, dry, mill, blend, compression, and pack (10 steps)
  • Process 2: Sample, weigh, mill, granulate, mill, dry, mill, blend, compression, coat, and pack (11 steps)
  • Process 3: Sample, weigh, mill, granulate, mill, dry, mill, blend, mill, blend, compression, mill, blend, compression, coat, and pack (16 steps)

All processes are fairly open (i.e., there are no containment devices or engineering controls used).

繁體中文解說

Scenario 4 的複雜性

這是四個情境中規模最大、複雜度最高的。關鍵特點：

  • 32 個產品、10 種 API — 清潔矩陣維度極大（10×10 = 100 種組合）
  • 完全開放製程（無工程控制）— 交叉污染風險相對高
  • 矩陣法清潔驗證 — 以最嚴格組合作為整體標準
  • 初始分析顯示不符合 EU GMP — 需要系統性重新審查

比喻：矩陣法清潔驗證

想像 10 種 API 兩兩排列，就像一個 10×10 的棋盤。矩陣法的概念是：不需要驗證每一格（100 種組合），而是找出最嚴苛的那一格（最低清潔限度），以此作為整體驗證標準——只要最難的一格通過，其餘自動滿足。

14.5.1 Scenario 4 — Background: Product Portfolio | 產品組合背景資訊
Table 14.5: Products Manufactured in the Facility

Highlighted rows: Orange = Anti-hypertensive1 (lowest ADE relevant combination); Red = Opioid (worst-case for cross-contamination risk assessment)

繁體中文解說

產品組合分析要點

10 種 API 的 ADE 範圍跨越三個數量級：

開放製程的風險意涵

「所有製程均為相當開放」（fairly open）意味著：無隔離器、無密閉轉移裝置、無工程控制。這對於 Anti-hypertensive1（ADE = 25 µg/day）和 Opioid（ADE = 50 µg/day）而言，是顯著的交叉污染風險因素。

Table 14.6 (Selected): Cleaning Limits Matrix (µg/cm²)

* Values below initial LOD; required analytical method improvement.
Original matrix approach: overall acceptance = 0.1 µg/cm² (most restrictive combination).
After analytical improvement and pulling Anti-hypertensive1→Anti-hypertensive2 from matrix: new overall limit = 2.0 µg/cm².

繁體中文解說

清潔矩陣法（Matrix Approach）邏輯

原始矩陣：所有組合中最低限度 = 0.1 µg/cm²（Anti-hypertensive1 → Anti-hypertensive2）。

問題：EU GMP 第 3.6 節要求檢測方法能可靠偵測此限度，但原始 LOD 均高於 0.1 µg/cm²，不符合要求。

解決步驟：

  1. 改善分析方法（見 Table 14.7）
  2. 新 LOD 仍無法偵測 0.1 µg/cm²（Anti-hypertensive1 新 LOD = 0.05）
  3. 將此組合（Anti-hypertensive1 → Anti-hypertensive2）從矩陣中「拉出」，改為每次化學分析確認
  4. 新矩陣整體限度提升至 2.0 µg/cm²，新 LOD 足以偵測

EU GMP Section 3.6 的要求

EU GMP 第 3.6 節規定，若毒理學評估所推導的殘留限度無法被已驗證的分析方法可靠偵測，則相關產品不得在共用設施製造。這是 Scenario 4 初始不合規的法規依據。

14.5.2 Scenario 4 — Risk Assessment | 風險評估流程
Original Text (English)

Is there a specific requirement for dedicated facility?

Regulations were reviewed. Due to the matrix approach and limits of detection, products cannot be made in shared facilities per EU GMP Section 3.6 where: "relevant residue limits, derived from the toxicological evaluation, cannot be satisfactorily determined by a validated analytical method."

The team was tasked with improving analytical methods to achieve limits of detection below 0.1 µg/cm².

Table 14.7: Limits of Detection for Cleaning Methods

Even with improved methods, Anti-hypertensive1 LOD (0.05 µg/cm²) cannot reliably detect 0.1 µg/cm². Solution: pull Anti-hypertensive1 → Anti-hypertensive2 sequence out of the matrix. Every time Anti-hypertensive2 is produced after Anti-hypertensive1, a chemical analysis will be completed to verify residue below limit. New overall matrix limit = 2.0 µg/cm² (detectable).

Data Gathered for Risk Analysis

Prior to Risk Analysis phase, the following information was gathered:

  1. Floor plans, flow plans, HVAC diagrams, room pressurization diagrams
  2. SOPs: Risk Management, Labeling, Man/Material Movement, Line clearance, Cleaning and Cleaning Validation, HVAC maintenance, Gowning/gloving
  3. Historical Data:
    • Cleaning results (30 samples; one failure — root cause: procedure not followed; CAPA: additional training)
    • Alarm reports: pressure differential out of range — 2011: 3×; 2012: 5×; 2013: 3×; 2014: 4×; 2015: 4×
    • Audit results
    • Regulatory actions
  4. Incident reports
  5. Deviations
  6. Change control list
繁體中文解說

風險評估的起點：法規符合性檢查

邏輯圖的第一個問題就是：「是否有法規要求使用專屬設施？」在 Scenario 4 中，初始答案幾乎是「是」，因為檢測方法無法偵測最嚴格的清潔限度。這驅動了整個改善行動。

分析方法改善的策略意義

提升 LOD（偵測下限）等同於提升對清潔有效性的「信心」。當 LOD 優於清潔限度，才能可靠地宣稱設備「清潔至符合標準」。若 LOD 高於清潔限度，則結果「合格」只代表「在方法偵測範圍內未發現問題」，科學意義不足。

「拉出矩陣」的實務操作

Anti-hypertensive1 → Anti-hypertensive2 被從矩陣拉出後，每次此序列發生時，需要：

  • 在 Anti-hypertensive2 生產前執行棉棒取樣（swab sampling）
  • 以化學分析確認殘留 < 0.1 µg/cm²
  • 合格後才能確認設備清潔並放行

這是一種「排除後個別處理」（case-by-case）的管控策略，既滿足法規要求，又不需要完全改變矩陣法。

歷史清潔數據的解讀

30 次清潔中有 1 次失敗（3.3%），根本原因是「未遵照程序」（human error），而非清潔製程本身失效。這是重要區別——製程能力本身沒問題，問題在行為。CAPA 選擇加強訓練（而非改變製程），具有針對性。

Table 14.8: Risk Ranking of APIs

A worst-case approach determines which product combination is used in risk assessments. Factors considered: ADE, %API, volumes manufactured, frequency of manufacture, process type, openness of equipment.

Factors making the opioid the highest risk product:

  1. ADE is fairly low compared to other compounds
  2. Manufactured fairly regularly (79 batches/year)
  3. Maximum daily dose in the middle range
  4. Process type has minimal differential impact — most products use the same process; those with more steps have greater batch sizes and ADEs

The opioid covers all 10 process steps used in the facility — no additional products need to be analyzed as worst case.

繁體中文解說

最差情況選擇的邏輯

Opioid 被選為最差情況（worst case），而非 Anti-hypertensive1（ADE 更低 = 25 vs 50 µg/day）。原因：

  • Anti-hypertensive1 批次數少（36/年）、批量小（7 kg）
  • Opioid 批次頻繁（79/年）、批量中等（115 kg），接觸面積大
  • Opioid 使用 Process 2，涵蓋設施中所有製程步驟

風險 = 危害（ADE 低）× 暴露（頻率高、接觸面積大）。單純以 ADE 排名並不足夠。

「最差情況」與清潔驗證的「最差情況」不同

原文特別說明：用於交叉污染風險評估的最差情況（opioid）不等同於清潔驗證的最差情況。

  • 交叉污染 worst case：考量危害性 + 製程暴露頻率 + 接觸面積
  • 清潔驗證 worst case：通常選擇最難清潔的物質（cleanability rank 最高）

「涵蓋所有製程步驟」的意義

選擇 Opioid（Process 2，10 步）作為風險評估對象，並非因為它是最危險的，而是因為它的製程涵蓋設施中所有製程步驟。一次評估即可代表所有產品的製程節點，避免重複工作。

14.5.2.1 Scenario 4 — Fishbone & FMEA Analysis | 魚骨圖與 FMEA 分析
Original Text (English) — Table 14.9: FMEA Analysis (partial)

S = Severity; O = Occurrence; D = Detection. RPN = S × O × D.
Corporate RPN thresholds: <125 Acceptable | 125–343 Risk Reduction needed | >343 Cease until reduced.

繁體中文解說

RPN（風險優先係數）計算與閾值

RPN = 嚴重度（S）× 發生率（O）× 偵測性（D）

  • RPN < 125：可接受風險，無需立即行動
  • 125 ≤ RPN ≤ 343：應實施風險降低措施（可繼續生產）
  • RPN > 343：不可接受風險，須停止生產直到降低風險

高 RPN 項目分析

RPN = 700（最高）：出現兩次，均為「設備未清潔（視覺檢查不足）」

  • 嚴重度 10（患者暴露）× 發生率 7（視覺常常無法發現）× 偵測性 10（無化學分析）= 700
  • 核心問題：僅靠視覺檢查無法可靠確認設備清潔到 0.1 µg/cm² 水平

RPN = 490 和 350：機械轉移問題（著裝未更換、設備帶殘留）

關鍵發現：最高風險來自「制度性缺陷」（視覺清潔驗證不足、著裝程序不完善），而非設施設計。

魚骨圖（Fishbone Analysis）的用途

魚骨圖（Ishikawa diagram）是 FMEA 的前置工具，用來系統性地腦力激盪四種交叉污染模式的所有可能原因（人員、方法、設備、環境、材料、量測）。完成魚骨圖後，再進行正式的 FMEA 表格分析，確保不遺漏任何失效模式。

「偵測性 = 10」的意義

偵測性評分為 10 代表「幾乎無法偵測」——現有管控完全無法發現此問題。在「Equipment not clean / Visual not adequate」這一行，視覺檢查無法偵測微量殘留，故 D = 10，直接讓 RPN 爆錶。這說明了為何化學分析（swab testing）是不可缺少的清潔驗證手段。

14.5.2 Scenario 4 — Risk Evaluation, Control & Communication | 風險評價、控制與溝通
Original Text (English)

Risk Evaluation

Corporate RPN thresholds (from Corporate Guidance on Risk Management):

  • Acceptable Risk: RPNs less than 125
  • Risk Reduction Required: RPNs 125 to 343 (activities may continue)
  • Unacceptable Risk: RPNs above 343 — cease until risk is reduced

Risk Control

Activities must cease until risk reduction is implemented for:

  1. Mix-up: staging in the corridor
  2. Retention: visual inspection not adequate to meet acceptance criteria
  3. Mechanical transfer: gowns not changed when changing API
  4. Mechanical transfer: residue on materials and equipment brought into/out of process room

Activities can continue but risk reduction should be implemented for:

  1. Mix-up: wrong label on container
  2. Retention: equipment not clean / did not follow procedure
  3. Airborne transfer: loss of pressure differential

Risk Communication

Immediate notification was provided to senior management on the unacceptable risk areas. Weekly updates on progress will be provided to senior management and operations until risk is reduced to allow production to resume.

Change control will be used to alert of possible changes that could alter the assessments, conclusions, and risk profile.

CAPA will be used to manage all risk reduction activities.

Training on how to manage the risk of cross-contamination will be provided to all staff involved in manufacture and/or packing.

Risk Review

The risk assessment will be reviewed:

  1. When products are added or removed from the facility portfolio
  2. When facilities, equipment and/or processes change or are added
  3. When there is a change to a product's properties (MDD, ADE, etc.)
  4. At least annually
繁體中文解說

四大「必須停工」項目的實務意涵

  1. 走廊暫存（staging in corridor）：材料和設備在走廊中混合暫放，極易導致不同 API 的物料混淆。改善：禁止走廊暫存，所有物料直接進出製程室。
  2. 視覺清潔驗證不足：對 ADE 低的 API（如 Anti-hypertensive1），肉眼無法確認清潔至 0.1 µg/cm²。改善：引入棉棒取樣化學分析。
  3. 更換 API 時未更換著裝：操作人員從一個 API 製程區移至另一個時，若不更換防護服，會機械性地攜帶殘留物。改善：制定強制換裝程序。
  4. 設備殘留帶出製程室：設備移出前未充分清潔，導致殘留物散播至走廊和其他製程室。改善：設備離室前必須清潔驗收。

風險溝通的三個層次

  • 即時通報：不可接受風險 → 立即通知高管
  • 定期更新：每週更新直到風險降至可接受水平
  • 系統性管理：CAPA 管理所有改善行動；Change Control 確保評估持續有效

觸發重新審查的四種情況

風險評估不是靜態文件，以下任何情況均需重新評估：

  • 產品組合變動（新增/移除）
  • 設施、設備或製程變更
  • 產品特性變化（MDD、ADE 修訂）
  • 定期年度審查（最低頻率）

這與 ICH Q10「持續改善」精神一致，也是法規（EU GMP、FDA）對品質系統的基本要求。

14.5 Scenario 4 — Risk Summary | 風險總結
Original Text (English)

There are several items that must be remediated in order to resume production. These are:

  • Staging of materials in the corridor
  • Visual detection for clean equipment is not always adequate based on the acceptance criteria
  • Gown changes when changing API
  • Residue escaping rooms on materials and equipment

The team is preparing remediation plans and will update senior management and operations on a weekly basis until the risk is reduced to allow production to resume.

繁體中文解說

Scenario 4 的核心教訓

  • 矩陣法 + 分析方法改善：當最嚴格組合的清潔限度無法被偵測時，優先改善分析方法或重新界定矩陣邊界，而非直接放棄共用設施。
  • 開放製程需要更嚴格的程序管控：無工程控制的設施，人員行為（著裝、清潔程序、物料管理）是風險的主要來源。
  • 視覺清潔驗證的侷限性：對低 ADE 物質，視覺檢查遠不足夠，必須有化學分析支持。
  • 最差情況選擇需綜合考量：危害特性（ADE）僅是其中一個因子，製造頻率和接觸面積同等重要。
14.6 Logic Diagram — Risk-Based Manufacturing & Sourcing Decisions | 風險基礎製造決策邏輯圖
14.6 Logic Diagram (Structural Reproduction)

The Logic Diagram spans pp. 161–162 and is referenced throughout Appendix 1 as the decision framework guiding all four scenarios. It covers three focus areas: cGMP/Regulatory Focus, Health and Hygiene Focus, and Asset Accommodation and Risk Management Approach. The following reproduces the key decision nodes in HTML flowchart form.

繁體中文解說

邏輯圖的三大決策區塊

本邏輯圖（Logic Diagram）是 ISPE Vol. 7 整個附錄 1 的核心工具，涵蓋三個決策維度：

  • cGMP/法規焦點：是否有監管要求使用專屬設施？分析方法能否偵測清潔限度？
  • 健康與衛生焦點：患者和作業員的風險是否在可接受範圍？若否，是否可透過管控措施降低？
  • 設施適應與風險管理：製程能否在現有設施中設計實施？管理框架是否完備？

邏輯圖的實際應用方式

在實務中，邏輯圖不是線性步驟清單，而是一個迭代式決策框架：

  • 每個問題的答案可能觸發新的調查（如改善分析方法）
  • 管控措施實施後需要重新評估（如 DoE 後重新計算 Ppk）
  • 最終結論需要所有路徑均通過，才能宣告風險可接受

法規要求的「二元篩選」

邏輯圖的最初兩個節點構成「法規篩選門檻」：

  1. 是否有明確法規要求專屬設施？若是，直接需要專屬設施，無需進一步分析。
  2. 分析方法能否偵測清潔限度？若否，EU GMP 3.6 不允許共用設施（直到方法改善）。

只有通過這兩個前提，才能進入風險分析階段。這也是 Scenario 4 初始「不合規」的根本原因，並驅動了整個分析方法改善工作。

邏輯圖的設計哲學

此邏輯圖體現了 ICH Q9 的核心精神：風險管理是一個動態過程，而非一次性評估。每個問題節點都允許「若現在不可行，是否可以改善後再試？」的路徑，避免了過度保守（直接放棄）或過於冒進（忽視風險）兩個極端。

  18. ICH Q7/Q7A — Good Manufacturing Practice Guide for Active Pharmaceutical Ingredients, Step 4, 10 November 2000.
  19. ICH Q7 Implementation Working Group: Questions and Answers, June 2015.
  20. ICH Q8(R2) — Pharmaceutical Development, August 2009.
  21. ICH Q11 — Development and Manufacture of Drug Substances, Step 4, 1 May 2012.
  22. ICH Q12 — Technical and Regulatory Considerations for Pharmaceutical Product Lifecycle Management, Step 1, 9 September 2014.
  23. Pharmaceutical cGMPs for the 21st Century – A Risk-Based Approach: Final Report, September 2004, FDA.
  24. Pharmaceutical Quality for the 21st Century – A Risk-Based Approach: Progress Report, May 2007, FDA.
  25. FDA general website, www.fda.gov.
  26. FDA Guidance: Process Validation — General Principles and Practices, January 2011, FDA.
  27. US Environmental Protection Agency (EPA), www.epa.gov.
  28. Occupational Safety and Health Administration (OSHA), www.osha.gov.
  29. American Conference of Governmental Industrial Hygienists (ACGIH®), www.acgih.org.
  30. Institut für Arbeitsschutz der Deutschen Gesetzlichen Unfallversicherung (DGUV/IFA), Germany OEL database.
  31. European Commission Scientific Committee on Occupational Exposure Limits (EC SCOEL).
  32. Proposition 65: Safe Drinking Water and Toxic Enforcement Act of 1986, CalEPA/OEHHA.

繁體中文解說 — 核心監管文件

最重要文件：EMA HBEL 指引（參考文獻 #6）

EMA/CHMP/CVMP/SWP/169430/2012 是本指引最核心的監管參照。此指引確立了在共用設施中以 健康暴露限值（HBEL）取代傳統 1/1000 劑量標準的法規框架。2014年正式生效後，全球製藥廠須重新評估清潔驗證的接受限值基礎。

ICH Q9 & Q10（#1 & #8）— 品質風險管理雙柱

ICH Q9（2005）建立了藥品品質風險管理的系統化框架，定義 FMEA、HAZOP、FTA 等工具的應用原則，是本 Vol.7 指引的理論基礎。

ICH Q10（2008）確立藥品品質系統（PQS）概念，將 QRM 嵌入產品生命週期管理，與 Vol.7 的 CAPA 及風險回顧機制直接銜接。

EU GMP EudraLex Vol.4（#4, #5, #10, #11）

第3章（廠房設備）與第5章（生產）2015年修訂版明確要求製造商採用 HBEL/ADE 作為交叉污染控制的科學依據，取代過去「可見殘留」標準。

附件2（生物製品）與附件15（確效）定義了生物活性物質製造與清潔驗證的特殊要求。

21 CFR Part 211（#13）— FDA cGMP 核心法規

美國 FDA 現行良好製造規範，涵蓋廠房設備、人員、製程管控、成品測試等完整要求。Vol.7 中所有風險管理措施均以符合此法規為前提。

ICH M7（#7）— DNA 反應性雜質

針對基因毒性雜質引入毒理學關注門檻（TTC）概念：1.5 μg/day 終生暴露為基準。在多產品共用設施中，若前一批次產品含基因毒性雜質，清潔驗證限值需特別嚴格。

FDA Process Validation Guidance（#26）

2011年指引引入持續製程驗證（CPV）概念，強調以統計製程控制（SPC）取代傳統一次性驗證。Vol.7 的 CPP 監控體系與此指引直接呼應。

繁體中文解說 — 科學文獻與標準

ADE/OEL 建立方法學核心文獻

參考文獻 #36–#64 構成 ADE 與 OEL 建立的毒理學方法論基礎。以下為關鍵作者與貢獻：

  • Naumann & Weideman（#39）：製藥 API 的不確定係數科學基礎，奠定 PDE/ADE 計算框架
  • Sargent et al.（#42）：ADE 建立實務指引，直接影響 EMA HBEL 指引
  • Sussman et al.（#34, #44）：高危害藥物識別與 ADE 調整係數諧調
  • Lehman & Fitzugh（#61）：1954年「100倍安全係數」原典，現代毒理學安全評估的歷史起點

毒理學關注門檻（TTC）文獻群組（#43, #69–#78）

TTC 概念源自 FDA 1995年 21 CFR 170.39，後經 Munro、Kroes 等系列論文發展為結構-活性關係基礎的閾值體系。應用於製藥製造的關鍵論文為 Dolan et al.（2005，#69），將 TTC 延伸至短期臨床試驗的交叉污染評估。

Fourman & Mullen（#84）— 清潔驗證限值的原典

1993年 Pharmaceut. Technol. 論文首次系統化提出 MACO 計算公式：

MACO = (Smallest daily dose of product A × Batch size of product B) / (Largest daily dose of product A × Safety factor)

此公式後被修改為以 ADE/PDE 為基礎的現代版本，但原理相同。

HVAC 與空氣過濾標準（#104–#111）

Vol.7 的空氣傳播交叉污染控制需符合多項標準：

  • ASHRAE 52.2：MERV 額定值測試方法
  • BS EN 1822：HEPA/ULPA 過濾器分類（EPA、HEPA、ULPA 等級）
  • IEC 60812：FMEA 分析技術標準

清潔驗證科學文獻（Sharnez 系列，#88–#103）

Sharnez 博士的系列論文涵蓋清潔製程的 QbD 方法、小規模模型建立、清潔動力學參數（流速、土壤負荷、濕度），為 Vol.7 附錄一中清潔驗證計算提供科學支撐。

16.1

Appendix 3 — Acronyms and Abbreviations

p167–p170 | 完整縮寫對照表，含重點術語中文說明

16.1 Acronyms and Abbreviations

繁體中文解說 — 重點縮寫詳解

HBEL — Health-Based Exposure Limit｜健康暴露限值

雖然 HBEL 本身未列入縮寫表，但為本指引最核心概念。HBEL 是以 ADE（Acceptable Daily Exposure）或 PDE（Permitted Daily Exposure）為基礎計算出的暴露限值，用於共用設施交叉污染風險評估，取代傳統 1/1000 最小治療劑量或 10 ppm 可見殘留標準。

ADE vs PDE — 兩個核心暴露限值

ADE（可接受每日暴露量）：由 ISPE 風險管理社群推廣，適用於多路徑暴露評估（包括口服、吸入、皮膚）。終生暴露不產生不良效應的劑量。

PDE（允許每日暴露量）：EMA HBEL 指引與 ICH Q3C 採用的術語。計算邏輯與 ADE 相同，但命名來自監管文件。

實務上：ADE ≈ PDE，兩者常互換使用，計算公式相同。

MACO — Maximum Allowable Carryover｜最大允許殘留轉移量

MACO 未列入本縮寫表，但為清潔驗證最重要計算結果。公式：

MACO (mg) = ADE (mg/day) × Batch size of next product (g) / Maximum daily dose of next product (g/day)

此結果轉換為表面殘留限值（μg/cm²），指導清潔驗證取樣標準。

OEB — Occupational Exposure Band｜職業暴露分級帶

OEB 是在尚未建立完整 OEL 時，依據毒性資料初步分類化合物危害等級的工具：

NOAEL / NOEL / LOAEL — 毒理學劑量描述符

  • NOAEL（無可觀察不良效應劑量）：動物實驗中未觀察到不良效應的最高劑量，是 ADE 計算的主要起始點（Point of Departure, PoD）
  • NOEL（無可觀察效應劑量）：比 NOAEL 更嚴格，連適應性效應都未出現
  • LOAEL（最低可觀察不良效應劑量）：當 NOAEL 不可得時作為替代 PoD，通常需額外增加不確定係數（UF = 3–10）

RPN — Risk Priority Number｜風險優先數

FMEA 中核心量化指標：RPN = 嚴重性（S）× 發生頻率（O）× 可偵測性（D），各項 1–10 分，RPN 範圍 1–1000。Vol.7 附錄1案例中：RPN < 125 可接受；125–343 需降低風險；> 343 不可接受，須停止作業。

CPP / CQA / CPV — 製程生命週期三角

  • CPP（關鍵製程參數）：必須被監控和控制的製程變數
  • CQA（關鍵品質屬性）：必須符合規格的產品特性
  • CPV（持續製程驗證）：商業化生產期間的持續監控，對應 FDA 2011年製程驗證指引

FMEA / HAZOP / FTA — QRM 工具三劍客

  • FMEA（失效模式與效應分析）：前瞻性，適合設備/製程設計審查，計算 RPN
  • HAZOP（危害與可操作性分析）：關鍵字驅動（More/Less/No/As Well As），適合連續製程和管道系統
  • FTA（故障樹分析）：後推性分析，從頂事件（不良結果）向下找根本原因
16.2

Appendix 3 — Definitions

p170–p176 | 45項定義，涵蓋 ADE、OEB、PDE、MACO、ALARP 等核心術語

16.2 Definitions of Terms

As used in this Guide, derived from multiple sources: FDA, other ISPE documents, ICH, EFPIA Resource Document (Assessing Facilities Needs, 14 November 2005), EU EudraLex Volume 4, and various WHO documents.

Acceptable Daily Exposure (ADE)

A dose that is unlikely to cause an adverse effect if an individual is exposed, by any route, at or below this dose every day for a lifetime. By definition the ADE is intended to be protective of all subpopulations and by all routes of administration. Establishment of the ADE value is an important first step in a risk assessment and the inherent assumptions should be consistent with how it is applied within the product mix in a given facility.

Active Pharmaceutical Ingredient (API)

Any substance, or mixture of substances intended to be used in the manufacture of a drug (medicinal) product and that, when used in the production of a drug, becomes an active ingredient of the drug product. Such substances are intended to furnish pharmacological activity or other direct effect in the diagnosis, cure, mitigation, treatment, or prevention of disease, or to affect the structure and function of the body.

Antineoplastic (see Cytostatic and Cytotoxic)

Chemotherapeutic agent that down regulates growth or kills cancer cells. May be classified as cytotoxic or cytostatic.

Aerosol

Suspension of fine solid or liquid particles (e.g., dust, fiber, fog, fume, mist, smoke) in a gas (i.e., typically in air).

Barrier

Facility/room/area, process, equipment, or isolation devices (e.g., glovebox) designed to achieve API or product containment.

Beta-lactam Antibiotics

Penicillins, cephalosporins, monobactams, and carbapenems, other APIs containing beta-lactam rings, beta-lactamase inhibitors with beta-lactam rings (e.g., clavulanic acid, and sulbactam and tazobactam).

Bulk

Any product that has completed all processing stages up to, but not including, final packaging.

Campaign

The manufacture of more than one product in a facility, with strict adherence to accepted cleaning procedures between these products. The products may be run in the same equipment, but not at the same time.

Carry Over

The residue or accumulated product on product contact surfaces that is retained after cleaning and may be available to enter the next product processed with the same product contact surfaces (i.e. it is carried-over to the next product in production). See definition of Retention.

Clean Zone

An area with defined environmental control of particulate and microbial contamination, constructed and used in such a way as to reduce the introduction, generation, and retention of contaminants within the area.

Closed Process

A process step (or system) where the product is not exposed to the immediate room environment (and vice versa). It is the manufacturer's responsibility to define and prove closure for a process step.

Contained Area

Specific manufacturing space constructed and equipped with appropriate air handling and filtration and operated to prevent contamination of the external work environment.

Containment

State achieved by enclosures with separation between manufacturing environment and manufacturing operation. The action of confining a biological agent or other entity within a defined space.

Contaminant

Any particulate, molecular, non-particulate, or biological entity that can adversely affect the product or process.

Contamination

The undesired introduction of impurities of a chemical or microbiological nature, or of foreign matter, into or onto a raw material, intermediate, or API during production, sampling, packaging or repackaging, storage, or transport.

Controlled Area

Facility space with restricted access and operated to restrict introduction of potential contamination, consequences of accidental release of airborne contaminants.

Cross-Contamination

Contamination of a starting material, intermediate product or finished product with another starting material or product during production.

Cytostatic (see Antineoplastic)

Chemotherapeutic agent capable of impairing cell proliferation.

Cytotoxic (see Antineoplastic)

Chemotherapeutic agent intended to control or kill cancer cells, which may act as an indiscriminate poison preventing cell reproduction or growth and causing death of cancerous and potentially healthy cells.

Decontamination

Process that reduces, detoxifies, and/or eliminates contaminated substances to a predetermined acceptance level.

Dedicated Area

Separate area, which may comprise one or more rooms within a multipurpose facility with its own air locked personnel/material accesses, dedicated to a specific product or product range.

Dedicated Building/Facility

Physically separate or segregated building with its own personnel/material accesses and HVAC systems, dedicated to process steps associated with a specific product or product.

Dedicated Change Part

An equipment change part (e.g., sieve, filter, etc.) that is dedicated to a specific product or product range, and is identified accordingly.

Dedicated Equipment

Equipment that is dedicated to a specific product or product range, and is identified accordingly.

Dedicated Suite

One or more rooms within a multipurpose facility or dedicated area that is dedicated to a specific product or product range, and is identified accordingly.

Detectability

Ability to discover or determine the existence, presence, or fact of a hazard.

Drug (a.k.a., API)

Chemical compound that may be used on, or administered to, humans as an aid in the diagnosis, treatment, cure, mitigation, or prevention of disease or other abnormal conditions.

Drug Product

A finished dosage form, for example, tablet, capsule, solution, etc., that contains one or more APIs generally, but not necessarily, in association with inactive ingredients. The term also includes a finished dosage form which does not contain an API but is intended to be used as a placebo.

Excipient (USP)

Components of a finished medicinal drug product other than the API. They are included in the formulation to facilitate manufacture, enhance stability, control release of API from the product, assist in product identification, or enhance other product characteristics.

Genotoxic

Substances which damage or modify DNA.

GxP Regulation

The underlying international pharmaceutical requirements, such as those set forth in the US FD&C Act, US PHS Act, FDA regulations, EU Directives, Japanese regulations, or other applicable national legislation or regulations under which a company operates. These include, but are not limited to: Good Manufacturing Practice (GMP), Good Clinical Practice (GCP), Good Laboratory Practice (GLP), Good Distribution Practice (GDP), Good Quality Practice (GQP), Good Pharmacovigilance Practice, Medical Device Regulations, and PDMA regulations.

Hazard

Inherent pharmacologic and toxicologic property of a substance that adversely affects the health of people, environment, process or product.

Hazardous Substance

A substance which by reason of being explosive, flammable, toxic, poisonous, corrosive, oxidizing, irritant or otherwise harmful, is likely to cause injury.

Health Hazard

Classification of a chemical for which there is statistically significant scientific data that acute or chronic adverse health effects may occur in exposed persons. Examples include: cardiovascular toxins, carcinogens, toxic or highly toxic, developmental and reproductive toxins, immunotoxic agents, hepatotoxins, nephrotoxins, and neurotoxins.

Highly Hazardous Drugs

Genotoxic compounds that are known to be, or highly likely to be, carcinogenic to humans, compounds that can produce reproductive and/or developmental effects at low dosages, and compounds that can produce serious target organ toxicity or other significant adverse effects at low dosages.

Holistic

Considering the whole system or process and its interdependencies rather than addressing separate parts in isolation.

Intermediate

A material produced during steps of the processing of an API that undergoes further molecular change or purification before it becomes an API. Intermediates may or may not be isolated.

Manufacturing Process

All manufacturing and storage steps in the creation of the finished product from the weighing of components through the storing, packaging, and labeling of the finished product, including, but not limited to, the following: mixing, granulating, milling, molding, formulating, lyophilizing, tableting, encapsulating, coating, sterilizing, and filling.

Mix-up

The contamination, at unsafe levels, of one product with another via inadequate plant and process design or human error.

Multiproduct Facility

A facility that supports production of two or more products, either in a campaigned or concurrent manner.

Mutagenic

Capable of inducing inheritable effect either in vitro and/or in vivo at the genetic (i.e., DNA or chromosomal) level.

No-Observed-Adverse-Effect Level (NOAEL)

The dose in a study which produces no adverse effects.

Occupational Exposure Band (OEB)

A range of airborne concentrations, usually spanning an order of magnitude, corresponding to a category assigned to a compound based on its inherent toxicological and pharmacological properties. The OEB also corresponds to control strategies, known in advance, to control airborne levels within the range of concentrations associated with the band.

Occupational Exposure Limit (OEL)

A health-based airborne concentration for a conventional 8-hour workday and a 40-hour workweek, to which it is believed that nearly all workers may be repeatedly exposed, day after day, for a working lifetime without adverse effect.

Open System/Process

A system that fails to meet one or more of the requirements that set the criteria for a closed system.

Permitted Daily Exposure (PDE)

A substance specific dose that is unlikely to cause an adverse effect if an individual is exposed at or below this dose every day for a lifetime.

Pharmaceutical Product

Substance or combination of APIs and excipients, or preservatives which has a therapeutic, prophylactic, or diagnostic purpose, or is intended to modify physiological functions, and is presented in a dosage form suitable for administration to the patient.

Physical Segregation

The separation of materials, spaces, or operations by means of physical barriers to prevent their mixing or overlap.

Plausible Pathways

A reasonable route of potential exposure.

Point-of-Departure (PoD)

The dose in animals or humans which serves as the starting point for derivation of the ADE value. This is the dose associated with the critical effect, which is the most sensitive clinically significant adverse effect observed that is relevant to humans.

Process Boundary

The process equipment and the interface, through which it is charged, discharged, sampled, intervened, and recovered.

Product Changeover

The program by which a processing area is cleared of supplies and components used in the manufacture of a previous product and then readied for production of a new product. This often includes parts changeover and/or special cleaning to eliminate cross-contamination.

Product Life Cycle

All phases in the life of the product from the initial development through marketing until the product's discontinuation.

Primary Containment

The first level of containment, consisting of the inside portion of that container which comes into immediate contact on its inner surface with the material being contained.

Quality Risk Management (QRM)

A systematic process for the assessment, control, communication and review of risks to the quality of the drug product across the product life cycle.

Quality System

The sum of all aspects of a system that implements quality policy and ensures that quality objectives are met.

Retention

The residue, or accumulated product, on product contact surfaces that can carryover from one product to another in the same equipment used in a sequential or campaign manner.

Risk

Likelihood of an identified harmful consequence as a function of exposure to a hazard.

Risk Metrics

A collection of quality, compliance, and/or performance measurements which help management measure and control the risks associated with operating within a regulated industry. Also known as dashboards.

Secondary Containment

Level of containment that is external to, and separate from, primary containment.

Self Contained Area

Premises which provide complete and total separation of all aspects of an operation including personnel and equipment movement, with well established procedures, controls, and monitoring. This includes physical barriers as well as separate air handling systems, but does not necessarily imply two distinct and separate buildings.

Sensitizer

A compound that can cause immediate (IgE mediated) or delayed (cell-mediated) hypersensitivity reactions.

Segregation

The provision of facilities which, although dedicated to a particular use, can be within the same building as other operations. A fully segregated area within a common building is one where there is a continuous floor to roof wall. The wall should be sealed at all break points where common services breach the wall.

Severity

A measure of the seriousness of possible consequences of a hazard.

Teratogenicity

The occurrence of behavioral or structural malformations in a developing foetus when a substance is administered during pregnancy.

Vaccine

Antigens prepared from modified organisms that elicit immune response (antibody production) to protect a person or animal from a disease agent.

Wipe Limit

A surface limit applied to external equipment and facility surfaces for the purpose of evaluating worker exposures. Any use of wipe sample results should be done with caution, within the context of a risk assessment for cross-contamination based on the underlying ADE value.

繁體中文解說 — 核心定義中文對照與詮釋

ADE（可接受每日暴露量） — 最重要定義

核心意涵：ADE 是終生暴露的安全劑量，保護所有次族群（老人、兒童、孕婦、病患），適用所有暴露途徑。

計算公式：

ADE = (NOAEL × 體重調整 × 暴露頻率調整) / (不確定係數 UF1×UF2×...×UFn)

實務應用：ADE 值決定清潔驗證 MACO 限值，也是 OEB 分級的依據。製藥廠在引入新 API 時，毒理學家必須先建立 ADE。

PDE（允許每日暴露量） — 與 ADE 的關係

PDE 源自 ICH Q3C（殘留溶劑指引），後被 EMA HBEL 指引採用為共用設施交叉污染控制的標準術語。計算邏輯與 ADE 完全相同，差別僅在命名慣例：

  • ISPE / RiskMAPP 社群 → 使用 ADE
  • EMA HBEL 指引、ICH Q3C → 使用 PDE
  • 實務上：ADE = PDE

OEB（職業暴露分級帶） — 早期控制策略工具

在尚未取得完整毒理數據時，OEB 依據已知藥理/毒理特性將化合物初步分為 5 個等級（OEB 1 最低危害 → OEB 5 最高危害），並與對應的工程控制策略掛鉤：

  • OEB 1–2：開放製程，一般通風即可
  • OEB 3：局部排氣通風（LEV）
  • OEB 4：完全封閉設備、隔離手套箱
  • OEB 5：專用設施、嚴格隔離、負壓環境

MACO（最大允許殘留轉移量） — 清潔驗證核心

雖然 MACO 未出現於定義表中，但是本指引清潔驗證的核心計算值。MACO 計算需要 ADE/PDE 值，並考慮後續批次的最大批量與最大每日劑量。

MACO → 換算為表面殘留限值 → 對比清潔驗證拭抹樣品結果 → 決定清潔是否合格。

ALARP（盡可能低） — 風險管理原則

ALARP（As Low As Reasonably Practicable）雖未列入本縮寫表，但為 Vol.7 風險控制決策的指導原則。其意涵：在技術可行且經濟合理的前提下，將風險降至盡可能低的水準。不等於「零風險」，而是在風險與成本間取得合理平衡。

交叉污染相關定義層次結構

Vol.7 的隔離策略對應以下定義層次（風險由高到低）：

PoD（起始點）— ADE 計算的出發點

PoD 是毒理學家進行 ADE 推算的關鍵起點：

  • 優先選用 NOAEL（動物或人體研究）
  • 若無 NOAEL，使用 LOAEL + 額外 UF（3–10×）
  • 現代方法：BMD（基準劑量）建模取代 NOAEL，提供更精確的統計 PoD

PoD 選擇直接影響 ADE 大小，是整個 HBEL 評估中最需要毒理學專業判斷的步驟。

Retention vs Carry Over — 兩個容易混淆的定義

Retention（殘留）：產品接觸面上的殘留量，是靜態概念，指清潔後仍附著在設備表面的物質。

Carry Over（帶入）：Retention 的動態結果，指殘留物在下一批次生產時被帶入產品的量。Carry Over = Retention × 接觸因子。

清潔驗證的目標是確保 Carry Over ≤ MACO。

Highly Hazardous Drugs — 高危害藥物三大類別

本定義涵蓋三類高危害化合物，需要最嚴格的 OEB 5 控制措施：

  • 基因毒性致癌物：已知或高可能性對人類致癌（如鉑類化合物）
  • 生殖/發育毒性物質：低劑量即可產生生殖或發育毒性（如沙利竇邁類）
  • 嚴重靶器官毒性物質：低劑量產生嚴重不良效應（如細胞毒性抗癌藥）

Quality Risk Management (QRM) — Vol.7 的核心框架

QRM 的四步驟循環：

  • 評估（Assessment）：識別危害、分析暴露途徑、評估風險大小
  • 控制（Control）：工程控制（隔離、HVAC）、管理控制（SOP、CAPA）
  • 溝通（Communication）：向管理層和監管機構報告風險狀態
  • 回顧（Review）：定期審查（至少每年一次），產品組合或製程變更時立即觸發

Wipe Limit — 表面殘留監控的謹慎解讀

指引特別提醒：拭抹結果應在交叉污染風險評估的脈絡下謹慎解讀，不可脫離 ADE 值單獨使用。拭抹效率（回收率）因物質、表面材質、拭抹技術而異，實際表面殘留量可能被低估或高估 2–10 倍，需納入不確定性評估。
